########################################################################
### FILE: contracts/modules/DegenerusGamePayoutUtils.sol   (frozen 2b26ec91)
########################################################################
     1  // SPDX-License-Identifier: AGPL-3.0-only
     2  pragma solidity 0.8.34;
     3  
     4  import {DegenerusGameStorage} from "../storage/DegenerusGameStorage.sol";
     5  import {ContractAddresses} from "../ContractAddresses.sol";
     6  
     7  /// @dev Shared payout helpers for jackpot-related modules.
     8  abstract contract DegenerusGamePayoutUtils is DegenerusGameStorage {
     9      /// @notice Emitted when ETH is credited to a player's claimable balance.
    10      /// @param player The original winner (ticket holder).
    11      /// @param recipient The address receiving the credit.
    12      /// @param amount Wei credited.
    13      event PlayerCredited(address indexed player, address indexed recipient, uint256 amount);
    14  
    15      /// @dev Half whale pass price unit (each half-pass = 1 ticket/level for 100 levels).
    16      uint256 internal constant HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE =
    17          2.25 ether;
    18  
    19      /// @dev Credit ETH to a player's claimable winnings balance.
    20      /// @param beneficiary Address to credit.
    21      /// @param weiAmount Amount in wei to credit.
    22      function _creditClaimable(address beneficiary, uint256 weiAmount) internal {
    23          if (weiAmount == 0) return;
    24          unchecked {
    25              claimableWinnings[beneficiary] += weiAmount;
    26          }
    27          emit PlayerCredited(beneficiary, beneficiary, weiAmount);
    28      }
    29  
    30      /// @dev Route coin-presale-box ETH proceeds: 80% to the vault, 20% to sDGNRS,
    31      ///      both as claimable credits, while bumping claimablePool by the full
    32      ///      boxEth so the claimablePool == Σ claimableWinnings invariant holds.
    33      ///      The integer-division remainder lands on the VAULT (80%) side, so the
    34      ///      two credits sum to exactly boxEth.
    35      /// @param boxEth Box proceeds in wei to route.
    36      function _creditBoxProceeds(uint256 boxEth) internal {
    37          if (boxEth == 0) return;
    38          uint256 sdgnrsShare = (boxEth * 20) / 100;
    39          claimablePool += uint128(boxEth);
    40          _creditClaimable(ContractAddresses.VAULT, boxEth - sdgnrsShare);
    41          _creditClaimable(ContractAddresses.SDGNRS, sdgnrsShare);
    42      }
    43  
    44      /// @dev Queue deferred whale pass claims for large payouts.
    45      function _queueWhalePassClaimCore(address winner, uint256 amount) internal {
    46          if (winner == address(0) || amount == 0) return;
    47  
    48          uint256 fullHalfPasses = amount / HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE;
    49          uint256 remainder = amount - (fullHalfPasses * HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE);
    50  
    51          if (fullHalfPasses != 0) {
    52              whalePassClaims[winner] += fullHalfPasses;
    53          }
    54          if (remainder != 0) {
    55              unchecked {
    56                  claimableWinnings[winner] += remainder;
    57              }
    58              claimablePool += uint128(remainder);
    59              emit PlayerCredited(winner, winner, remainder);
    60          }
    61      }
    62  }

    27  /// @dev GNRUS interface for level-transition governance resolution.
    28  interface IGNRUSResolve {
    29      function pickCharity(uint24 level) external;
    30  }
    31  
    32  /// @notice Delegate-called module for advanceGame and VRF lifecycle handling.
    33  contract DegenerusGameAdvanceModule is DegenerusGameStorage {
    34      /*+======================================================================+
    35        |                              ERRORS                                  |
    36        +======================================================================+*/
    37  
    38      // error E() — inherited from DegenerusGameStorage
    39      error NotTimeYet();
    40      error RngNotReady();
    41      // error RngLocked() — inherited from DegenerusGameStorage
    42  
    43      /*+======================================================================+
    44        |                              EVENTS                                  |
    45        +======================================================================+*/
    46  
    47      event Advance(uint8 stage, uint24 lvl);
    48      event RewardJackpotsSettled(
    49          uint24 indexed lvl,
    50          uint256 futurePool,
    51          uint256 claimableDelta
    52      );
    53  
    54      // Advance stage constants (sequential, matching advanceGame flow)
    55      uint8 private constant STAGE_GAMEOVER = 0;
    56      uint8 private constant STAGE_RNG_REQUESTED = 1;
    57      uint8 private constant STAGE_TRANSITION_WORKING = 2;
    58      uint8 private constant STAGE_TRANSITION_DONE = 3;
    59      uint8 private constant STAGE_FUTURE_TICKETS_WORKING = 4;
    60      uint8 private constant STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING = 5;
    61      uint8 private constant STAGE_PURCHASE_DAILY = 6;
    62      uint8 private constant STAGE_ENTERED_JACKPOT = 7;
    63      uint8 private constant STAGE_JACKPOT_COIN_TICKETS = 8;
    64      uint8 private constant STAGE_JACKPOT_PHASE_ENDED = 9;
    65      uint8 private constant STAGE_JACKPOT_DAILY_STARTED = 10;
    66      /// @dev Partial-drain status for the afking process STAGE (mirrors
    67      ///      STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING): the subscriber set has not yet fully stamped
    68      ///      this cycle, so advance broke before rngGate and returns mult.
    69      uint8 private constant STAGE_SUBS_WORKING = 11;
    70      /// @dev A multi-day VRF-stall gap backfill ran this advance; the day's jackpot
    71      ///      distribution is deferred to the next advance so the backfill + jackpot never
    72      ///      share one tx (each stays under the per-tx gas ceiling). rngGate is idempotent on
    73      ///      re-entry (gapDays == 0 next call), dailyIdx is not yet advanced, so advanceDue()
    74      ///      stays true and the next advance pays the jackpot with the same frozen word.
    75      uint8 private constant STAGE_GAP_BACKFILLED = 12;
    76      event DailyRngApplied(
    77          uint24 day,
    78          uint256 rawWord,
    79          uint256 nudges,
    80          uint256 finalWord
    81      );
    82      event LootboxRngApplied(uint48 index, uint256 word, uint256 requestId);
    83      event VrfCoordinatorUpdated(
    84          address indexed previous,
    85          address indexed current
    86      );
    87      event StEthStakeFailed(uint256 amount);
    88  
    89      /// @notice Emitted when DGNRS is rewarded to the top affiliate.
    90      /// @param affiliate Address of the top affiliate.
    91      /// @param level Level for which they were top affiliate.
    92      /// @param dgnrsAmount Amount of DGNRS paid from the affiliate pool.
    93      event AffiliateDgnrsReward(
    94          address indexed affiliate,
    95          uint24 indexed level,
    96          uint256 dgnrsAmount
    97      );
    98  
    99      /*+=======================================================================+
   100        |                   PRECOMPUTED ADDRESSES (CONSTANT)                    |
   101        +=======================================================================+*/
   102  
   103      IStETH internal constant steth = IStETH(ContractAddresses.STETH_TOKEN);
   104      /// @notice GNRUS contract for governance resolution at level transitions
   105      IGNRUSResolve private constant charityResolve =
   106          IGNRUSResolve(ContractAddresses.GNRUS);
   107      /// @notice Jackpots contract — direct handle for skip-marker on losing flip days.
   108      IDegenerusJackpots private constant jackpots =
   109          IDegenerusJackpots(ContractAddresses.JACKPOTS);
   110      /*+======================================================================+
   111        |                           CONSTANTS                                  |
   112        +======================================================================+*/
   113  
   114      uint32 private constant DEPLOY_IDLE_TIMEOUT_DAYS = 365; // Level-0 only; level 1+ uses hardcoded 120 days
   115      uint48 private constant GAMEOVER_RNG_FALLBACK_DELAY = 14 days;
   116      uint8 private constant JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP = 5;
   117      uint32 private constant VRF_CALLBACK_GAS_LIMIT = 300_000;
   118  
   119      /// @dev Daily decay factor for drip projection (1 - 0.0075 conservative rate).
   120      ///      Projection uses 0.75% daily decay (conservative vs actual 1% drip)
   121      ///      to determine whether futurePool drip can cover nextPool deficit.
   122      uint256 private constant DECAY_RATE = 0.9925 ether;
   123  
   124      uint16 private constant VRF_REQUEST_CONFIRMATIONS = 10;
   125      uint16 private constant VRF_MIDDAY_CONFIRMATIONS = 4;
   126  
   127      uint256 private constant BURNIE_RNG_TRIGGER = 40_000 ether;
   128      uint32 private constant VAULT_PERPETUAL_TICKETS = 16;
   129      uint16 private constant NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_FAST = 3000;
   130      uint16 private constant NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_MIN = 1300;
   131      uint16 private constant NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_DAY_STEP = 14;
   132      uint16 private constant NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_X9_BONUS = 200;
   133      uint16 private constant NEXT_SKIM_VARIANCE_BPS = 2500;
   134      uint16 private constant NEXT_SKIM_VARIANCE_MIN_BPS = 1000;
   135      uint16 private constant INSURANCE_SKIM_BPS = 100; // 1% of nextPool -> yieldAccumulator
   136      uint16 private constant OVERSHOOT_THRESHOLD_BPS = 12500; // R > 1.25x triggers surcharge
   137      uint16 private constant OVERSHOOT_CAP_BPS = 3500; // 35% max surcharge
   138      uint16 private constant OVERSHOOT_COEFF = 4000; // numerator coefficient (0.40 in bps)
   139      uint16 private constant NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_MAX = 8000; // 80% total skim hard cap
   140      uint16 private constant ADDITIVE_RANDOM_BPS = 1000; // 0–10% additive random on bps
   141      bytes32 private constant FUTURE_KEEP_TAG = keccak256("future-keep");
   142      uint96 private constant MIN_LINK_FOR_LOOTBOX_RNG = 40 ether;
   143      uint48 private constant MIDDAY_RNG_RETRY_TIMEOUT = 6 hours;
   144  
   145      /// @dev Per-call afking process-STAGE gas-weight budget. Every day is uniform now: the
   146      ///      streak is computed on read from the Sub slot (no per-buy `playerQuestStates`
   147      ///      STATICCALL, no settle day), so there is a SINGLE budget. The STAGE consumes a
   148      ///      gas-weight per iteration — buys are weighted by true marginal cost (a lootbox buy
   149      ///      ≈34k = `SUB_STAGE_LOOTBOX_WEIGHT` (2), a ticket buy ≈73k = `SUB_STAGE_TICKET_WEIGHT`
   150      ///      (4)), and a cross-contract sub-ending finalize (cancel-reclaim / pass-evict /
   151      ///      funding-kill) ≈18k = `SUB_STAGE_EVICT_WEIGHT` (1) — and ends the chunk on accumulated
   152      ///      weight, not raw count, so the worst-case chunk (any mix) stays under the 16.7M
   153      ///      advance-chain ceiling while a normal chunk targets <10M. A large set drains across
   154      ///      several advanceGame calls. Composition-flat at ~18k per weight-unit: chunk gas ≈
   155      ///      `per-call overhead (≈83k) + budget × ~18k`. At 500 the worst chunk is ~9.2M (all-ticket
   156      ///      ≈9.2M / all-lootbox ≈8.6M / all-evict ≈5.5M), comfortably under 10M with ~7.5M headroom
   157      ///      to the 16.7M ceiling. A large set drains across several advanceGame calls.
   158      uint256 private constant SUB_STAGE_WEIGHT_BUDGET = 500;
   159  
   160      /// @notice DGNRS reward for top affiliate: 1% of remaining affiliate pool.
   161      uint16 private constant AFFILIATE_POOL_REWARD_BPS = 100;
   162  
   163      /// @notice Max share of affiliate DGNRS pool segregated per level for claims (5%).
   164      uint16 private constant AFFILIATE_DGNRS_LEVEL_BPS = 500;
   165  
   166      /// @notice Advance game state. Called daily to process jackpots, mints, and phase transitions.
   167      ///         Returns mult: the day-epoch stall multiplier (1 base / 2 / 4 / 6 by stall; 0 on
   168      ///         the gameover path = no bounty). Standalone callers earn nothing — the unified
   169      ///         afking router pays the re-homed bounty (2x * mult) only when mult > 0.
   170      function advanceGame() external returns (uint8 mult) {
   171          mult = 1;
   172          uint48 ts = uint48(block.timestamp);
   173          uint24 day = _simulatedDayIndexAt(ts);
   174          bool inJackpot = jackpotPhaseFlag;
   175          uint24 lvl = level;
   176          uint24 psd = purchaseStartDay;
   177          // Turbo: if target already met on day ≤1, flag now so the upcoming
   178          // _requestRng does the level pre-increment (matching normal
   179          // lastPurchaseDay flow). Skipped when rngLockedFlag is set because
   180          // rngGate will take the fresh-word path instead of _requestRng, so
   181          // the level pre-increment would be missed and the (lastPurchase &&
   182          // rngLockedFlag) ternary below would compute purchaseLevel = 0.
   183          if (!inJackpot && !lastPurchaseDay && !rngLockedFlag) {
   184              uint32 purchaseDays = day - psd;
   185              if (
   186                  purchaseDays <= 1 && _getNextPrizePool() >= levelPrizePool[lvl]
   187              ) {
   188                  lastPurchaseDay = true;
   189                  compressedJackpotFlag = 2;
   190                  if (gameOverPossible) gameOverPossible = false; // FLAG-03: auto-clear when target met
   191              }
   192          }
   193          bool lastPurchase = (!inJackpot) && lastPurchaseDay;
   194          // Level already incremented at RNG request when lastPurchase=true
   195          uint24 purchaseLevel = (lastPurchase && rngLockedFlag) ? lvl : lvl + 1;
   196          if (!inJackpot && !lastPurchase) {
   197              (bool goReturn, uint8 goStage) = _handleGameOverPath(day, lvl, psd);
   198              if (goReturn) {
   199                  // Gameover path: advance ran but earns NO router bounty (the flip-credit
   200                  // coin is worthless at gameover) — return mult = 0 so mintBurnie pays nothing.
   201                  emit Advance(goStage, lvl);
   202                  return 0;
   203              }
   204          }
   205  
   206          // --- Mid-day path: same-day queue draining ---
   207          if (day == dailyIdx) {
   208              // Step 1: Finish draining the read slot if not yet fully processed
   209              if (!ticketsFullyProcessed) {
   210                  // If mid-day ticket swap is pending, wait for VRF word before processing
   211                  if (_lrRead(LR_MID_DAY_SHIFT, LR_MID_DAY_MASK) != 0) {
   212                      uint256 word = lootboxRngWordByIndex[
   213                          uint48(_lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK)) - 1
   214                      ];
   215                      if (word == 0) revert RngNotReady();
   216                  }
   217  
   218                  uint24 rk = _tqReadKey(purchaseLevel);
   219                  if (ticketQueue[rk].length > 0) {
   220                      (
   221                          bool ticketWorked,
   222                          bool ticketsFinished
   223                      ) = _runProcessTicketBatch(purchaseLevel);
   224                      if (ticketWorked || !ticketsFinished) {
   225                          if (ticketsFinished) {
   226                              ticketsFullyProcessed = true;
   227                              _lrWrite(LR_MID_DAY_SHIFT, LR_MID_DAY_MASK, 0);
   228                          }
   229                          emit Advance(STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING, lvl);
   230                          // Mid-day partial-drain: mult = 1 (ADV-05/D-07 — no escalation).
   231                          return mult;
   232                      }
   233                  }
   234              }
   235  
   236              revert NotTimeYet();
   237          }
   238  
   239          // Day-epoch stall multiplier (new-day path only), written straight into the `mult`
   240          // return so the router scales the re-homed advance bounty: 2x after 20 min, 4x after
   241          // 1 hour, 6x after 2 hours. `mult` defaults to 1 (set at function entry).
   242          {
   243              uint256 dayStart = (uint256(day - 1) +
   244                  ContractAddresses.DEPLOY_DAY_BOUNDARY) *
   245                  1 days +
   246                  82_620;
   247              uint256 elapsed = ts - dayStart;
   248              if (elapsed >= 2 hours) {
   249                  mult = 6;
   250              } else if (elapsed >= 1 hours) {
   251                  mult = 4;
   252              } else if (elapsed >= 20 minutes) {
   253                  mult = 2;
   254              }
   255          }
   256  
   257          uint8 stage;
   258          do {
   259              // --- Daily drain gate: ensure read slot is fully processed before RNG ---
   260              if (!ticketsFullyProcessed) {
   261                  uint24 preRk = _tqReadKey(purchaseLevel);
   262                  if (ticketQueue[preRk].length > 0) {
   263                      uint48 preIdx = uint48(
   264                          _lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK)
   265                      ) - 1;
   266                      if (lootboxRngWordByIndex[preIdx] == 0) {
   267                          uint256 cw = rngWordCurrent;
   268                          if (cw == 0) revert RngNotReady();
   269                          unchecked {
   270                              cw += totalFlipReversals;
   271                          }
   272                          _finalizeLootboxRng(cw);
   273                      }
   274                      (bool preWorked, bool preFinished) = _runProcessTicketBatch(
   275                          purchaseLevel
   276                      );
   277                      if (preWorked || !preFinished) {
   278                          stage = STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING;
   279                          break;
   280                      }
   281                  }
   282                  ticketsFullyProcessed = true;
   283              }
   284  
   285              // --- Afking process STAGE: stamp the funded subscriber set BEFORE the day
   286              // requests its RNG. Inserted on the new-day path only, after the daily
   287              // ticket-drain gate and strictly before rngGate. The mid-day same-day path
   288              // returns earlier, so the STAGE never runs mid-day. Chunked by SUB_STAGE_BATCH across advance calls
   289              // (BUY_BATCH-style) so a large set stays under the 16.7M advance-chain
   290              // ceiling — mirrors the ticketsFullyProcessed partial-drain discipline:
   291              // break + return mult while !subsFullyProcessed; set true only at cursor
   292              // end; then fall through to rngGate.
   293              //
   294              // The STAGE runs strictly pre-RNG (before rngGate writes the day's word), so
   295              // rngWordByDay[processDay] is uncommitted when a sub is stamped — the
   296              // load-bearing freeze property. The box reads the LIVE level +
   297              // rngWordByDay[lastAutoBoughtDay] at open.
   298              //
   299              // Forward-looking per-day reset: the first time the advance enters a new `day`,
   300              // flip the drain gate + cursor BEFORE that day's STAGE runs. subsFullyProcessed
   301              // stays true after a day's STAGE completes (it means "afking done for that day")
   302              // until the next day flips it here. Stamped to `day` at the reset, so it fires
   303              // exactly once per day and never re-fires within the day (independent of when
   304              // dailyIdx catches up in _unlockRng).
   305              if (_afkingResetDay != day) {
   306                  _afkingResetDay = day;
   307                  subsFullyProcessed = false;
   308                  _subCursor = 0;
   309              }
   310              if (!subsFullyProcessed) {
   311                  if (_subscribers.length != 0) {
   312                      _runSubscriberStage(day);
   313                      if (_subCursor < _subscribers.length) {
   314                          // Partial drain: more subs remain this cycle — break before
   315                          // rngGate and return mult (no RNG request yet). subsFullyProcessed
   316                          // stays false; the next advance call resumes the cursor.
   317                          stage = STAGE_SUBS_WORKING;
   318                          break;
   319                      }
   320                  }
   321                  // Cursor reached the set end (or the set is empty) — the whole funded
   322                  // set is stamped for this cycle. Fall through to rngGate. subsFullyProcessed
   323                  // resets to false for the next day at _swapTicketSlot (the per-day reset,
   324                  // alongside ticketsFullyProcessed).
   325                  subsFullyProcessed = true;
   326              }
   327  
   328              // RNG: use existing word or request new one
   329              bool bonusFlip = (inJackpot && jackpotCounter == 0) || lvl == 0;
   330              (uint256 rngWord, uint32 gapDays) = rngGate(
   331                  ts,
   332                  day,
   333                  purchaseLevel,
   334                  lastPurchase,
   335                  bonusFlip
   336              );
   337              psd += uint24(gapDays);
   338              if (rngWord == 1) {
   339                  _swapAndFreeze(purchaseLevel);
   340                  stage = STAGE_RNG_REQUESTED;
   341                  break;
   342              }
   343  
   344              // Decouple a multi-day VRF-stall gap backfill from the day's jackpot distribution:
   345              // if rngGate just backfilled a gap (gapDays != 0), defer everything downstream (the
   346              // phase transition + the up-to-305-winner daily jackpot) to the next advance so the
   347              // backfill and the jackpot never execute in one tx (each stays under the per-tx gas
   348              // ceiling). rngGate is idempotent (rngWordByDay[day] is now set -> gapDays == 0 next
   349              // call) and dailyIdx is not yet advanced (no _unlockRng reached), so advanceDue() stays
   350              // true and the next advance pays the jackpot with the same frozen word. The break
   351              // returns mult so the keeper is paid for the backfill work (mirrors the partial drains).
   352              if (gapDays != 0) {
   353                  stage = STAGE_GAP_BACKFILLED;
   354                  break;
   355              }
   356  
   357              // Phase transition housekeeping + FF promotion
   358              if (phaseTransitionActive) {
   359                  // Drain the one FF level that entered near-future at this level transition.
   360                  // At new level L, the boundary moved from >L+4 to >L+5, making L+5 near-future.
   361                  // No new FF entries can arrive at L+5 (tickets targeting it now route to write key).
   362                  // purchaseLevel = level + 1, so the FF level is purchaseLevel + 4 = level + 5.
   363                  uint24 ffLevel = purchaseLevel + 4;
   364                  bool resumingFF = (ticketLevel ==
   365                      (ffLevel | TICKET_FAR_FUTURE_BIT));
   366                  if (!resumingFF) {
   367                      if (!_processPhaseTransition(purchaseLevel)) {
   368                          stage = STAGE_TRANSITION_WORKING;
   369                          break;
   370                      }
   371                      // Set up FF drain — ticketLevel signals we've completed transition housekeeping
   372                      ticketLevel = ffLevel | TICKET_FAR_FUTURE_BIT;
   373                      ticketCursor = 0;
   374                  }
   375                  (bool ffWorked, bool ffFinished, ) = _processFutureTicketBatch(
   376                      ffLevel,
   377                      rngWord
   378                  );
   379                  if (ffWorked || !ffFinished) {
   380                      stage = STAGE_TRANSITION_WORKING;
   381                      break;
   382                  }
   383                  phaseTransitionActive = false;
   384                  _unlockRng(day);
   385                  purchaseStartDay = day;
   386                  jackpotPhaseFlag = false;
   387                  // evaluate endgame flag on purchase-phase entry at L10+
   388                  _evaluateGameOverAndTarget(lvl, day, day);
   389                  stage = STAGE_TRANSITION_DONE;
   390                  break;
   391              }
   392  
   393              // Process near-future ticket queues before daily draws
   394              // to include fresh lootbox-driven tickets
   395              if (!dailyJackpotCoinTicketsPending) {
   396                  if (
   397                      !_prepareFutureTickets(
   398                          inJackpot ? lvl : purchaseLevel,
   399                          rngWord
   400                      )
   401                  ) {
   402                      stage = STAGE_FUTURE_TICKETS_WORKING;
   403                      break;
   404                  }
   405              }
   406  
   407              // Process current level tickets:
   408              // Purchase phase processes purchaseLevel (= level+1) where new tickets route.
   409              // Jackpot phase processes level where jackpot-phase tickets route.
   410              (bool ticketWorked, bool ticketsFinished) = _runProcessTicketBatch(
   411                  inJackpot ? lvl : purchaseLevel
   412              );
   413              if (ticketWorked || !ticketsFinished) {
   414                  stage = STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING;
   415                  break;
   416              }
   417              ticketsFullyProcessed = true; // ADV-03: set before jackpot/phase logic
   418  
   419              // === PURCHASE PHASE ===
   420              if (!inJackpot) {
   421                  // Pre-target: daily jackpots while building prize pool
   422                  if (!lastPurchaseDay) {
   423                      if (purchaseLevel == 1) {
   424                          _emitDailyWinningTraits(1, rngWord, 1);
   425                          _payDailyCoinJackpot(1, rngWord, 1, 1);
   426                          uint256 saltedRng = uint256(
   427                              keccak256(
   428                                  abi.encodePacked(
   429                                      rngWord,
   430                                      keccak256("BONUS_TRAITS")
   431                                  )
   432                              )
   433                          );
   434                          _payDailyCoinJackpot(1, saltedRng, 2, 5);
   435                      } else {
   436                          payDailyJackpot(false, purchaseLevel, rngWord);
   437                          _payDailyCoinJackpot(
   438                              purchaseLevel,
   439                              rngWord,
   440                              purchaseLevel + 1,
   441                              purchaseLevel + 4
   442                          );
   443                      }
   444                      // FLAG-02: combined target + game-over check (shares SLOADs when flag is set)
   445                      bool targetMet = gameOverPossible
   446                          ? _evaluateGameOverAndTarget(lvl, psd, day)
   447                          : _getNextPrizePool() >=
   448                              levelPrizePool[purchaseLevel - 1];
   449                      if (targetMet) {
   450                          lastPurchaseDay = true;
   451                          if (day - psd <= 3) {
   452                              compressedJackpotFlag = 1;
   453                          }
   454                      }
   455                      _unlockRng(day);
   456                      stage = STAGE_PURCHASE_DAILY;
   457                      break;
   458                  }
   459  
   460                  // Activate next-level tickets before jackpot phase
   461                  {
   462                      uint24 nextLevel = purchaseLevel + 1;
   463                      (
   464                          bool futureWorked,
   465                          bool futureFinished,
   466  
   467                      ) = _processFutureTicketBatch(nextLevel, rngWord);
   468                      if (futureWorked || !futureFinished) {
   469                          stage = STAGE_FUTURE_TICKETS_WORKING;
   470                          break;
   471                      }
   472                  }
   473  
   474                  // Consolidate prize pools for level transition
   475                  levelPrizePool[purchaseLevel] = _getNextPrizePool();
   476                  _distributeYieldSurplus(rngWord);
   477                  _consolidatePoolsAndRewardJackpots(
   478                      lvl,
   479                      purchaseLevel,
   480                      day,
   481                      rngWord,
   482                      psd
   483                  );
   484  
   485                  if (lvl >= 3 && _psRead(PS_ACTIVE_SHIFT, PS_ACTIVE_MASK) != 0) {
   486                      _psWrite(PS_ACTIVE_SHIFT, PS_ACTIVE_MASK, 0);
   487                  }
   488  
   489                  // Transition to jackpot phase
   490                  jackpotPhaseFlag = true;
   491  
   492                  lastPurchaseDay = false;
   493  
   494                  // Roll level quest at level transition so it's active during jackpot phase
   495                  quests.rollLevelQuest(rngWord);
   496  
   497                  // Do not unlock here: allows day-1 jackpot processing to run on
   498                  // the same day as the transition day.
   499                  stage = STAGE_ENTERED_JACKPOT;
   500                  break;
   501              }
   502  
   503              // === JACKPOT PHASE ===
   504  
   505              // Complete coin+ticket distribution
   506              if (dailyJackpotCoinTicketsPending) {
   507                  payDailyJackpotCoinAndTickets(rngWord);
   508                  if (jackpotCounter >= JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP) {
   509                      _endPhase();
   510                      stage = STAGE_JACKPOT_PHASE_ENDED;
   511                      break;
   512                  }
   513                  _unlockRng(day);
   514                  stage = STAGE_JACKPOT_COIN_TICKETS;
   515                  break;
   516              }
   517  
   518              // Fresh daily jackpot
   519              payDailyJackpot(true, lvl, rngWord);
   520              stage = STAGE_JACKPOT_DAILY_STARTED;
   521          } while (false);
   522  
   523          // New-day advance leg: `mult` already holds the day-epoch stall ladder (1/2/4/6)
   524          // the router scales the re-homed bounty by.
   525          emit Advance(stage, lvl);
   526      }
   527  
   528      /*+========================================================================================+
   529        |                    ADMIN VRF FUNCTIONS                                                 |
   530        +========================================================================================+
   531        |  Deploy-only VRF setup called from the ContractAddresses.ADMIN constructor.            |
   532        |  Post-deploy VRF changes use updateVrfCoordinatorAndSub (emergency rotation).          |
   533        +========================================================================================+*/
   534  
   535      /// @notice Wire VRF config, called once from the ADMIN constructor during deployment.
   536      /// @dev Access: ContractAddresses.ADMIN only. No post-deploy caller exists on ADMIN;
   537      ///      emergency VRF rotation uses updateVrfCoordinatorAndSub instead.
   538      /// @param coordinator_ Chainlink VRF V2.5 coordinator address.
   539      /// @param subId VRF subscription ID for LINK billing.
   540      /// @param keyHash_ VRF key hash for gas lane selection.
   541      function wireVrf(
   542          address coordinator_,
   543          uint256 subId,
   544          bytes32 keyHash_
   545      ) external {
   546          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.ADMIN) revert E();
   547  
   548          address current = address(vrfCoordinator);
   549          _setVrfConfig(coordinator_, subId, keyHash_);
   550          lastVrfProcessedTimestamp = uint48(block.timestamp);
   551          emit VrfCoordinatorUpdated(current, coordinator_);
   552      }
   553  
   554      /*+======================================================================+
   555        |                    GAMEOVER / LIVENESS GUARDS                        |
   556        +======================================================================+*/
   557  
   558      /// @dev Handles gameover state and liveness guard checks.
   559      ///      Returns (shouldReturn, stage). shouldReturn=true means advanceGame
   560      ///      should emit `stage` and exit. Stages used:
   561      ///         STAGE_GAMEOVER -- normal game-over completion or final sweep
   562      ///         STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING -- partial best-effort drain; caller retries
   563      function _handleGameOverPath(
   564          uint24 day,
   565          uint24 lvl,
   566          uint24 psd
   567      ) private returns (bool shouldReturn, uint8 stage) {
   568          // Liveness guard: prevent permanent lockup if game is abandoned.
   569          // Uses the shared _livenessTriggered() helper so purchase paths (in
   570          // DegenerusGameMintModule) can reuse the same predicate to block new
   571          // purchases during the multi-tx game-over drain sequence.
   572          psd; // silence unused-param warning after refactor to shared helper
   573          day;
   574          bool ok;
   575          bytes memory data;
   576  
   577          // gameOver check precedes liveness so the post-gameover final-sweep path
   578          // stays reachable after the VRF-dead path latches gameOver with day-math
   579          // still below the 120/365 threshold (e.g., VRF breaks on day 14).
   580          if (gameOver) {
   581              // Post-gameover: check for final sweep (1 month after gameover)
   582              (ok, data) = ContractAddresses.GAME_GAMEOVER_MODULE.delegatecall(
   583                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
   584                      IDegenerusGameGameOverModule.handleFinalSweep.selector
   585                  )
   586              );
   587              if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
   588              return (true, STAGE_GAMEOVER);
   589          }
   590  
   591          if (!_livenessTriggered()) return (false, 0);
   592  
   593          // Safety: don't activate game over if nextPool requirement is already met
   594          if (lvl != 0 && _getNextPrizePool() >= levelPrizePool[lvl]) {
   595              return (false, 0);
   596          }
   597  
   598          // Pre-gameover: acquire RNG, drain, then unlock
   599          if (rngWordByDay[day] == 0) {
   600              uint256 rngWord = _gameOverEntropy(
   601                  uint48(block.timestamp),
   602                  day,
   603                  lvl,
   604                  lastPurchaseDay
   605              );
   606              if (rngWord == 1 || rngWord == 0) return (true, STAGE_GAMEOVER);
   607          }
   608  
   609          // Best-effort dual-round drain of queued tickets so every purchased
   610          // ticket is eligible for the terminal jackpot trait-bucket share.
   611          // Round 1: drain the current read slot under the now-populated lootbox
   612          //          RNG slot.
   613          // Round 2: after round 1 fully finishes, swap the write slot into the
   614          //          read position and drain it too (covers tickets purchased
   615          //          after the most recent swap).
   616          //
   617          // Partial rounds (succeeded but unfinished) break out with
   618          // STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING so the caller can retry until the queue is
   619          // exhausted -- mirrors the do-while stage/break pattern.
   620          //
   621          // Catastrophic delegatecall reverts (e.g., queue exceeds the block
   622          // gas limit) are swallowed so game-over continues to terminal jackpot
   623          // distribution; undrained tickets forfeit trait-bucket eligibility but
   624          // fund release is never blocked.
   625          if (!ticketsFullyProcessed) {
   626              (bool d1Ok, bytes memory d1Data) = ContractAddresses
   627                  .GAME_MINT_MODULE
   628                  .delegatecall(
   629                      abi.encodeWithSelector(
   630                          IDegenerusGameMintModule.processTicketBatch.selector,
   631                          lvl + 1
   632                      )
   633                  );
   634              if (d1Ok && d1Data.length >= 32) {
   635                  bool d1Finished = abi.decode(d1Data, (bool));
   636                  if (!d1Finished) {
   637                      return (true, STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING);
   638                  }
   639                  // Round 1 completed: read slot drained. Swap write->read
   640                  // (safe because queue is now empty) and run round 2 so
   641                  // write-slot tickets also get their traits.
   642                  _swapTicketSlot(lvl + 1);
   643                  (bool d2Ok, bytes memory d2Data) = ContractAddresses
   644                      .GAME_MINT_MODULE
   645                      .delegatecall(
   646                          abi.encodeWithSelector(
   647                              IDegenerusGameMintModule
   648                                  .processTicketBatch
   649                                  .selector,
   650                              lvl + 1
   651                          )
   652                      );
   653                  if (d2Ok && d2Data.length >= 32) {
   654                      bool d2Finished = abi.decode(d2Data, (bool));
   655                      if (!d2Finished) {
   656                          return (true, STAGE_TICKETS_WORKING);
   657                      }
   658                      ticketsFullyProcessed = true;
   659                  }
   660                  // d2Ok=false -> swallow, fall through to handleGameOverDrain
   661              }
   662              // d1Ok=false -> swallow, fall through to handleGameOverDrain
   663          }
   664  
   665          (ok, data) = ContractAddresses.GAME_GAMEOVER_MODULE.delegatecall(
   666              abi.encodeWithSelector(
   667                  IDegenerusGameGameOverModule.handleGameOverDrain.selector,
   668                  day
   669              )
   670          );
   671          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
   672          _unlockRng(day);
   673          return (true, STAGE_GAMEOVER);
   674      }
   675  
   676      /*+======================================================================+
   677        |                           LEVEL END                                 |
   678        +======================================================================+*/
   679      function _endPhase() private {
   680          uint24 lvl = level;
   681          phaseTransitionActive = true;
   682          if (lvl % 100 == 0) {
   683              levelPrizePool[lvl] = _getFuturePrizePool() / 3;
   684          }
   685          jackpotCounter = 0;
   686          compressedJackpotFlag = 0;
   687      }
   688  
   689      /*+================================================================================================================+
   690        |                    DELEGATE MODULE HELPERS                                                                     |
   691        +================================================================================================================+
   692        |  Internal functions that delegatecall into specialized modules.                                                |
   693        |  All modules MUST inherit DegenerusGameStorage for slot alignment.                                             |
   694        |                                                                                                                |
   695        |  Modules:                                                                                                      |
   696        |  • ContractAddresses.GAME_DECIMATOR_MODULE - Decimator claim credits and lootbox payouts                       |
   697        |  • ContractAddresses.GAME_MINT_MODULE     - Mint data recording, airdrop multipliers                           |
   698        |  • ContractAddresses.GAME_WHALE_MODULE    - Whale bundle purchases and whale pass claims                       |
   699        |  • ContractAddresses.GAME_JACKPOT_MODULE  - Jackpot calculations and payouts                                   |
   700        |                                                                                                                |
   701        |  SECURITY: delegatecall executes module code in this contract's                                                |
   702        |  context, with access to all storage. Modules are constant.                                                    |
   703        +================================================================================================================+*/
   704  
   705      /// @dev Reward the top affiliate for a level and segregate per-level DGNRS allocation.
   706      ///      After the 1% top-affiliate draw, snapshots 5% of the remaining affiliate
   707      ///      pool into levelDgnrsAllocation[lvl]. Affiliate scores always route to
   708      ///      level + 1 during gameplay, so at transition time (when level becomes lvl),
   709      ///      all scores at index lvl are frozen — new scores go to lvl + 1.
   710      ///      Claims read levelDgnrsAllocation[currLevel] directly.
   711      ///      Unclaimed tokens are never physically moved — they remain in the pool
   712      ///      and naturally roll into the next level's snapshot.
   713      function _rewardTopAffiliate(uint24 lvl) private {
   714          (address top, ) = affiliate.affiliateTop(lvl);
   715  
   716          if (top != address(0)) {
   717              uint256 poolBalance = dgnrs.poolBalance(
   718                  IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate
   719              );
   720              uint256 dgnrsReward = (poolBalance * AFFILIATE_POOL_REWARD_BPS) /
   721                  10_000;
   722              uint256 paid = dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   723                  IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate,
   724                  top,
   725                  dgnrsReward
   726              );
   727              emit AffiliateDgnrsReward(top, lvl, paid);
   728          }
   729  
   730          // Segregate 5% of remaining affiliate pool for per-affiliate claims.
   731          // Scores at index lvl are frozen (new scores go to lvl + 1).
   732          uint256 remainingPool = dgnrs.poolBalance(
   733              IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate
   734          );
   735          levelDgnrsAllocation[lvl] =
   736              (remainingPool * AFFILIATE_DGNRS_LEVEL_BPS) /
   737              10_000;
   738      }
   739  
   740      /// @dev Distribute yield surplus via JackpotModule delegatecall.
   741      ///      Runs while frozen, before pool consolidation. The obligations sum
   742      ///      includes both live pools and the pending buffer, so freeze-window
   743      ///      revenue (which routes to pending) is never misread as yield surplus.
   744      function _distributeYieldSurplus(uint256 rngWord) private {
   745          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
   746              .GAME_JACKPOT_MODULE
   747              .delegatecall(
   748                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
   749                      IDegenerusGameJackpotModule.distributeYieldSurplus.selector,
   750                      rngWord
   751                  )
   752              );
   753          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
   754      }
   755  
   756      /// @dev Drive one chunk of the afking process STAGE via GAME_AFKING_MODULE
   757      ///      delegatecall (the module operates on this contract's storage in-context —
   758      ///      the subscriber set / cursors / Sub stamps all live in
   759      ///      DegenerusGameStorage). For each funded sub the callee STAMPS the per-sub box
   760      ///      fields (lootbox mode) or QUEUES whole tickets via purchaseWith (ticket mode),
   761      ///      sets the lastAutoBoughtDay marker, debits afkingFunding (claimablePool in
   762      ///      tandem, fail loud — D-348-04 no-valve), and advances _subCursor until the
   763      ///      accumulated gas-weight reaches SUB_STAGE_WEIGHT_BUDGET; it persists _subCursor
   764      ///      itself. The STAGE caller decides drained-vs-partial by re-reading _subCursor against
   765      ///      _subscribers.length. No per-day epoch is written — the box reads the LIVE level +
   766      ///      rngWordByDay[day] at open.
   767      /// @param processDay The boundary-pinned process day (seeds the open, FREEZE-03).
   768      function _runSubscriberStage(uint24 processDay) private {
   769          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
   770              .GAME_AFKING_MODULE
   771              .delegatecall(
   772                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
   773                      IGameAfkingModule.processSubscriberStage.selector,
   774                      processDay,
   775                      SUB_STAGE_WEIGHT_BUDGET
   776                  )
   777              );
   778          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
   779      }
   780  
   781      /// @dev Bubble up revert reason from delegatecall failure.
   782      ///      Uses assembly to preserve original error data.
   783      /// @param reason The error bytes from failed delegatecall.
   784      function _revertDelegate(bytes memory reason) private pure {
   785          if (reason.length == 0) revert E();
   786          assembly ("memory-safe") {
   787              revert(add(32, reason), mload(reason))
   788          }
   789      }
   790  
   791      /// @dev All pool transition logic: time-based future take, pool consolidation,
   792      ///      coinflip credit, reward jackpots (BAF/Decimator), and future→next drawdown.
   793      ///      All intermediate pool values computed in memory; storage written in batches.
   794      function _consolidatePoolsAndRewardJackpots(
   795          uint24 lvl,
   796          uint24 purchaseLevel,
   797          uint24 day,
   798          uint256 rngWord,
   799          uint24 psd
   800      ) private {
   801          uint256 memFuture = _getFuturePrizePool();
   802          uint256 memCurrent = _getCurrentPrizePool();
   803          uint256 memNext = _getNextPrizePool();
   804          uint256 memYieldAcc = yieldAccumulator;
   805  
   806          // --- Time-based future take (batched) ---
   807          {
   808              uint32 start = psd + 7;
   809              uint32 elapsed = day > start ? day - start : 0;
   810  
   811              uint256 bps = _nextToFutureBps(elapsed, purchaseLevel);
   812              if (purchaseLevel % 10 == 9) bps += NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_X9_BONUS;
   813  
   814              uint256 lastPool = levelPrizePool[purchaseLevel - 1];
   815  
   816              // Ratio adjust: ±4% based on future/next ratio (target 2:1)
   817              uint256 ratioPct = (memFuture * 100) / memNext;
   818              if (ratioPct < 200) {
   819                  bps += (200 - ratioPct) * 2;
   820              } else {
   821                  uint256 penalty = ratioPct - 200;
   822                  penalty = penalty > 400 ? 400 : penalty;
   823                  bps = penalty >= bps ? 0 : bps - penalty;
   824              }
   825  
   826              // Overshoot surcharge
   827              if (lastPool != 0) {
   828                  uint256 rBps = (memNext * 10_000) / lastPool;
   829                  if (rBps > OVERSHOOT_THRESHOLD_BPS) {
   830                      uint256 excess = rBps - OVERSHOOT_THRESHOLD_BPS;
   831                      uint256 surcharge = (excess * OVERSHOOT_COEFF) /
   832                          (excess + 10_000);
   833                      if (surcharge > OVERSHOOT_CAP_BPS)
   834                          surcharge = OVERSHOOT_CAP_BPS;
   835                      bps += surcharge;
   836                  }
   837              }
   838  
   839              // Additive random 0–10%
   840              bps += rngWord % (ADDITIVE_RANDOM_BPS + 1);
   841  
   842              // Compute take
   843              uint256 take = (memNext * bps) / 10_000;
   844  
   845              // ±25% multiplicative variance (triangular: avg of two uniform VRF rolls)
   846              if (take != 0) {
   847                  uint256 halfWidth = (take * NEXT_SKIM_VARIANCE_BPS) / 10_000;
   848                  uint256 minWidth = (memNext * NEXT_SKIM_VARIANCE_MIN_BPS) /
   849                      10_000;
   850                  if (halfWidth < minWidth) halfWidth = minWidth;
   851                  if (halfWidth > take) halfWidth = take;
   852  
   853                  uint256 range = halfWidth * 2 + 1;
   854                  uint256 roll1 = (rngWord >> 64) % range;
   855                  uint256 roll2 = (rngWord >> 192) % range;
   856                  uint256 combined = (roll1 + roll2) / 2;
   857  
   858                  if (combined >= halfWidth) {
   859                      take += combined - halfWidth;
   860                  } else {
   861                      take -= halfWidth - combined;
   862                  }
   863              }
   864  
   865              // Cap at 80%
   866              uint256 maxTake = (memNext * NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_MAX) / 10_000;
   867              if (take > maxTake) take = maxTake;
   868  
   869              uint256 insuranceSkim = (memNext * INSURANCE_SKIM_BPS) / 10_000;
   870              memNext -= take + insuranceSkim;
   871              memFuture += take;
   872              memYieldAcc += insuranceSkim;
   873          }
   874  
   875          // --- x00 yield accumulator dump: 50% into futurePool (memory) ---
   876          if ((lvl % 100) == 0) {
   877              uint256 half = memYieldAcc >> 1;
   878              memFuture += half;
   879              memYieldAcc -= half;
   880          }
   881  
   882          // --- BAF + Decimator x00: draw from futurePool BEFORE keep roll ---
   883          uint256 baseMemFuture = memFuture;
   884          uint24 prevMod10 = lvl % 10;
   885          uint24 prevMod100 = lvl % 100;
   886          uint256 claimableDelta;
   887  
   888          // BAF Jackpot (every 10 levels) — only if the daily flip won (bit 0 of
   889          // rngWord = 1). On a losing flip the bracket is marked skipped, the pool
   890          // stays in futurePool, and pre-skip winning-flip credit is filtered out
   891          // of future claims via the lastBafResolvedDay bump.
   892          if (prevMod10 == 0) {
   893              if ((rngWord & 1) == 1) {
   894                  uint256 bafPct = prevMod100 == 0 ? 20 : (lvl == 50 ? 20 : 10);
   895                  uint256 bafPoolWei = (baseMemFuture * bafPct) / 100;
   896  
   897                  uint256 claimed = IDegenerusGame(address(this)).runBafJackpot(
   898                      bafPoolWei,
   899                      lvl,
   900                      rngWord
   901                  );
   902                  memFuture -= claimed;
   903                  claimableDelta += claimed;
   904              } else {
   905                  jackpots.markBafSkipped(lvl);
   906              }
   907          }
   908  
   909          // Decimator jackpot fires at the window-close bump.
   910          // x00 draws 30% from pre-jackpot future; x5 (non-x95) draws 10% from current.
   911          uint256 decPoolWei;
   912          if (prevMod100 == 0) {
   913              decPoolWei = (baseMemFuture * 30) / 100;
   914          } else if (prevMod10 == 5 && prevMod100 != 95) {
   915              decPoolWei = (memFuture * 10) / 100;
   916          }
   917  
   918          if (decPoolWei != 0) {
   919              uint256 returnWei = IDegenerusGame(address(this))
   920                  .runDecimatorJackpot(decPoolWei, lvl, rngWord);
   921              uint256 spend = decPoolWei - returnWei;
   922              memFuture -= spend;
   923              claimableDelta += spend;
   924          }
   925  
   926          // --- x00 keep roll (5d4 dice: 30-65% keep, avg ~47.5%) ---
   927          // Operates on post-jackpot memFuture — all reward jackpots drew first.
   928          if ((lvl % 100) == 0) {
   929              uint256 seed = uint256(
   930                  keccak256(abi.encodePacked(rngWord, FUTURE_KEEP_TAG))
   931              );
   932              uint256 total;
   933              unchecked {
   934                  total =
   935                      (seed % 4) +
   936                      ((seed >> 16) % 4) +
   937                      ((seed >> 32) % 4) +
   938                      ((seed >> 48) % 4) +
   939                      ((seed >> 64) % 4);
   940              }
   941              uint256 keepBps = 3000 + (total * 3500) / 15;
   942              if (keepBps < 10_000) {
   943                  uint256 moveWei = memFuture - (memFuture * keepBps) / 10_000;
   944                  memFuture -= moveWei;
   945                  memCurrent += moveWei;
   946              }
   947          }
   948  
   949          // --- Merge next → current ---
   950          memCurrent += memNext;
   951          memNext = 0;
   952  
   953          // --- Coinflip credit ---
   954          coinflip.creditFlip(
   955              ContractAddresses.SDGNRS,
   956              (memCurrent * PRICE_COIN_UNIT) /
   957                  (PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(level) * 20)
   958          );
   959  
   960          // --- Future→next drawdown (15% on non-x00 levels) ---
   961          if ((lvl % 100) != 0) {
   962              uint256 reserved = (memFuture * 15) / 100;
   963              memFuture -= reserved;
   964              memNext = reserved;
   965          }
   966  
   967          // --- Single SSTORE batch: all pool values ---
   968          _setPrizePools(uint128(memNext), uint128(memFuture));
   969          currentPrizePool = uint128(memCurrent);
   970          yieldAccumulator = memYieldAcc;
   971          if (claimableDelta != 0) {
   972              claimablePool += uint128(claimableDelta); // Safe: claimableDelta bounded by futurePool which fits uint128
   973          }
   974          emit RewardJackpotsSettled(lvl, memFuture, claimableDelta);
   975      }
   976  
   977      /// @dev Pay daily jackpot via jackpot module delegatecall.
   978      ///      Called each day during purchase phase and jackpot phase.
   979      /// @param isJackpotPhase True for jackpot phase dailies, false for purchase phase jackpot.
   980      /// @param lvl Current level.
   981      /// @param randWord VRF random word for winner selection.
   982      function payDailyJackpot(
   983          bool isJackpotPhase,
   984          uint24 lvl,
   985          uint256 randWord
   986      ) internal {
   987          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
   988              .GAME_JACKPOT_MODULE
   989              .delegatecall(
   990                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
   991                      IDegenerusGameJackpotModule.payDailyJackpot.selector,
   992                      isJackpotPhase,
   993                      lvl,
   994                      randWord
   995                  )
   996              );
   997          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
   998      }
   999  
  1000      /// @dev Pay coin+ticket portion of daily jackpot via jackpot module delegatecall.
  1001      ///      Called when dailyJackpotCoinTicketsPending is true to complete the split
  1002      ///      daily jackpot (gas optimization to stay under 15M block limit).
  1003      /// @param randWord VRF random word for winner selection.
  1004      function payDailyJackpotCoinAndTickets(uint256 randWord) internal {
  1005          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
  1006              .GAME_JACKPOT_MODULE
  1007              .delegatecall(
  1008                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
  1009                      IDegenerusGameJackpotModule
  1010                          .payDailyJackpotCoinAndTickets
  1011                          .selector,
  1012                      randWord
  1013                  )
  1014              );
  1015          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
  1016      }
  1017  
  1018      /// @dev Pay daily BURNIE jackpot via jackpot module delegatecall.
  1019      ///      Called each day during purchase phase in its own transaction.
  1020      ///      Awards 0.5% of prize pool target in BURNIE to trait-matched winners in [minLevel, maxLevel].
  1021      /// @param lvl Current level.
  1022      /// @param randWord VRF random word for winner selection.
  1023      /// @param minLevel Minimum target level for near-future coin distribution (inclusive).
  1024      /// @param maxLevel Maximum target level for near-future coin distribution (inclusive).
  1025      function _payDailyCoinJackpot(
  1026          uint24 lvl,
  1027          uint256 randWord,

  1029          uint24 maxLevel
  1030      ) private {

  1036                      lvl,
  1037                      randWord,
  1038                      minLevel,
  1039                      maxLevel
  1040                  )
  1041              );
  1042          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
  1043      }
  1044  
  1045      /// @dev Emit DailyWinningTraits via self-call into GAME, which delegatecalls JackpotModule.
  1046      ///      Used at purchaseLevel==1 where payDailyJackpot is skipped.
  1047      ///      Self-call preserves msg.sender == address(this) across the delegatecall so the
  1048      ///      JackpotModule's OnlyGame check passes.
  1049      function _emitDailyWinningTraits(
  1050          uint24 lvl,
  1051          uint256 randWord,
  1052          uint24 bonusTargetLevel
  1053      ) private {
