  1055              lvl,
  1056              randWord,
  1057              bonusTargetLevel
  1058          );
  1059      }
  1060  
  1061      /// @notice Request lootbox RNG when activity threshold is met.
  1062      /// @dev Standalone function for mid-day lootbox RNG requests.
  1063      ///      Cannot be called while daily RNG is locked (jackpot resolution).
  1064      ///      VRF callback handles finalization directly - no advanceGame needed.
  1065      function requestLootboxRng() external {
  1066          if (rngLockedFlag) revert RngLocked();
  1067          // Block while mid-day ticket processing is active — prevents entropy reroll
  1068          // by requesting a new VRF word after inspecting the current one.
  1069          if (_lrRead(LR_MID_DAY_SHIFT, LR_MID_DAY_MASK) != 0) revert E();
  1070          uint48 nowTs = uint48(block.timestamp);
  1071          uint24 currentDay = _simulatedDayIndexAt(nowTs);
  1072  
  1073          // Block in the 15-minute pre-reset window to avoid competing with daily jackpot RNG flow.
  1074          if ((nowTs - 82620) % 1 days >= 1 days - 15 minutes) revert E();
  1075          // Block until today's daily RNG has been consumed and recorded.
  1076          if (rngWordByDay[currentDay] == 0) revert E();
  1077  
  1078          if (rngRequestTime != 0) revert E();
  1079  
  1080          // LINK balance check
  1081          (uint96 linkBal, , , , ) = vrfCoordinator.getSubscription(
  1082              vrfSubscriptionId
  1083          );
  1084          if (linkBal < MIN_LINK_FOR_LOOTBOX_RNG) revert E();
  1085  
  1086          // Threshold check
  1087          uint256 pendingEth = _unpackMilliEthToWei(
  1088              uint64(_lrRead(LR_PENDING_ETH_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_ETH_MASK))
  1089          );
  1090          uint256 pendingBurnie = _unpackWholeBurnieToWei(
  1091              uint40(_lrRead(LR_PENDING_BURNIE_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_BURNIE_MASK))
  1092          );
  1093          if (pendingEth == 0 && pendingBurnie == 0) revert E();
  1094          if (pendingBurnie < BURNIE_RNG_TRIGGER) {
  1095              uint256 totalEthEquivalent = pendingEth;
  1096              if (pendingBurnie != 0) {
  1097                  uint256 priceWei = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(level);
  1098                  if (priceWei != 0) {
  1099                      totalEthEquivalent +=
  1100                          (pendingBurnie * priceWei) /
  1101                          PRICE_COIN_UNIT;
  1102                  }
  1103              }
  1104              uint256 threshold = _unpackMilliEthToWei(
  1105                  uint64(_lrRead(LR_THRESHOLD_SHIFT, LR_THRESHOLD_MASK))
  1106              );
  1107              if (threshold != 0 && totalEthEquivalent < threshold) revert E();
  1108          }
  1109  
  1110          // Freeze ticket buffer: swap write→read so tickets purchased after
  1111          // VRF delivery can't be resolved by this word.
  1112          {
  1113              uint24 purchaseLevel_ = level + 1;
  1114              uint24 wk = _tqWriteKey(purchaseLevel_);
  1115              if (ticketQueue[wk].length > 0 && ticketsFullyProcessed) {
  1116                  _swapTicketSlot(purchaseLevel_);
  1117                  _lrWrite(LR_MID_DAY_SHIFT, LR_MID_DAY_MASK, 1);
  1118              }
  1119          }
  1120  
  1121          // VRF request (reverts on failure)
  1122          uint256 id = vrfCoordinator.requestRandomWords(
  1123              VRFRandomWordsRequest({
  1124                  keyHash: vrfKeyHash,
  1125                  subId: vrfSubscriptionId,
  1126                  requestConfirmations: VRF_MIDDAY_CONFIRMATIONS,
  1127                  callbackGasLimit: VRF_CALLBACK_GAS_LIMIT,
  1128                  numWords: 1,
  1129                  extraArgs: hex""
  1130              })
  1131          );
  1132  
  1133          // Advance lootbox index so new purchases target the NEXT RNG
  1134          _lrWrite(
  1135              LR_INDEX_SHIFT,
  1136              LR_INDEX_MASK,
  1137              _lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK) + 1
  1138          );
  1139          _lrWrite(LR_PENDING_ETH_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_ETH_MASK, 0);
  1140          _lrWrite(LR_PENDING_BURNIE_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_BURNIE_MASK, 0);
  1141          vrfRequestId = id;
  1142          rngWordCurrent = 0;
  1143          rngRequestTime = uint48(block.timestamp);
  1144      }
  1145  
  1146      /// @notice Retry a stalled mid-day lootbox RNG request after MIDDAY_RNG_RETRY_TIMEOUT.
  1147      /// @dev Permissionless. Only reachable when the original mid-day request committed
  1148      ///      a buffer swap (LR_MID_DAY = 1) and the VRF callback has not delivered.
  1149      ///      Re-fires VRF with the same parameters; the stalled requestId is auto-rejected
  1150      ///      by the requestId match in rawFulfillRandomWords. Buffer state and the
  1151      ///      pre-advanced lootboxRngIndex are preserved so the new word lands in the
  1152      ///      same bucket the original was bound to.
  1153      function retryLootboxRng() external {
  1154          if (_lrRead(LR_MID_DAY_SHIFT, LR_MID_DAY_MASK) == 0) revert E();
  1155          if (rngRequestTime == 0) revert E();
  1156          if (uint48(block.timestamp) < rngRequestTime + MIDDAY_RNG_RETRY_TIMEOUT) revert E();
  1157  
  1158          (uint96 linkBal, , , , ) = vrfCoordinator.getSubscription(
  1159              vrfSubscriptionId
  1160          );
  1161          if (linkBal < MIN_LINK_FOR_LOOTBOX_RNG) revert E();
  1162  
  1163          uint256 id = vrfCoordinator.requestRandomWords(
  1164              VRFRandomWordsRequest({
  1165                  keyHash: vrfKeyHash,
  1166                  subId: vrfSubscriptionId,
  1167                  requestConfirmations: VRF_MIDDAY_CONFIRMATIONS,
  1168                  callbackGasLimit: VRF_CALLBACK_GAS_LIMIT,
  1169                  numWords: 1,
  1170                  extraArgs: hex""
  1171              })
  1172          );
  1173  
  1174          vrfRequestId = id;
  1175          rngRequestTime = uint48(block.timestamp);
  1176      }
  1177  
  1178      // BIT ALLOCATION MAP for VRF random word (currentWord after _applyDailyRng):
  1179      //
  1180      // Bit(s)   Consumer                    Operation                         Location
  1181      // ------   --------                    ---------                         --------
  1182      // 0        Coinflip win/loss           rngWord & 1                       BurnieCoinflip._resolveDay
  1183      // 0        BAF fire gate               rngWord & 1                       AdvanceModule._consolidatePoolsAndRewardJackpots
  1184      // 8+       Redemption roll             (currentWord >> 8) % 151 + 25     AdvanceModule.rngGate
  1185      // full     Coinflip reward percent     keccak256(rngWord, epoch) % 20    BurnieCoinflip._resolveDay
  1186      // full     Jackpot winner selection    via delegatecall (full word)      JackpotModule (payDailyJackpot)
  1187      // full     Coin jackpot                via delegatecall (full word)      JackpotModule (_payDailyCoinJackpot)
  1188      // full     Lootbox RNG                 stored as lootboxRngWordByIndex   AdvanceModule._applyDailyRng
  1189      // full     Future take variance        rngWord % (variance * 2 + 1)      AdvanceModule._takeFuturePrizePoolSlice
  1190      // full     Prize pool consolidation    via delegatecall (full word)      JackpotModule (consolidatePrizePools)
  1191      // full     Reward jackpots             via delegatecall (full word)      JackpotModule (_runRewardJackpots)
  1192      //
  1193      // NOTE: Bits 0 and 8+ are the only direct bit-level consumers.
  1194      //       All "full" consumers use modular arithmetic or keccak mixing,
  1195      //       so bit overlap with bits 0 and 8+ is not a collision concern.
  1196  
  1197      /// @dev Daily RNG processing gate called during advanceGame. Applies VRF word,
  1198      ///      processes coinflip payouts, rolls daily quest, resolves pending gambling
  1199      ///      burn redemptions, stores lootbox RNG, and handles VRF timeout retries (12h).
  1200      function rngGate(
  1201          uint48 ts,
  1202          uint24 day,
  1203          uint24 lvl,
  1204          bool isTicketJackpotDay,
  1205          bool bonusFlip
  1206      ) internal returns (uint256 word, uint32 gapDays) {
  1207          // Already recorded for today
  1208          if (rngWordByDay[day] != 0) return (rngWordByDay[day], 0);
  1209  
  1210          uint256 currentWord = rngWordCurrent;
  1211  
  1212          // Have a fresh VRF word ready
  1213          if (currentWord != 0 && rngRequestTime != 0) {
  1214              // Backfill gap days from VRF stall before processing current day.
  1215              // Gated on rngWordByDay[idx + 1] == 0 so the backfill runs at
  1216              // most once per lock window: dailyIdx is only updated by
  1217              // _unlockRng, so a multi-day drain would otherwise re-enter
  1218              // this branch on each new wall-clock day and re-process the
  1219              // same gap range, doubling purchaseStartDay and re-running
  1220              // coinflip payouts for already-resolved days.
  1221              uint24 idx = dailyIdx;
  1222              if (day > idx + 1 && rngWordByDay[idx + 1] == 0) {
  1223                  uint24 gapCount = day - idx - 1;
  1224                  _backfillGapDays(currentWord, idx + 1, day, bonusFlip);
  1225  
  1226                  // Backfill any lootbox indices that never got a VRF word (orphaned by stall).
  1227                  // Uses fresh VRF entropy, not predictable on-chain state.
  1228                  _backfillOrphanedLootboxIndices(currentWord);
  1229  
  1230                  // Extend death clock by the stall duration -- gap days don't count toward
  1231                  // the 120-day inactivity timeout since the game was stalled, not abandoned.
  1232                  purchaseStartDay += gapCount;
  1233                  gapDays = gapCount;
  1234              }
  1235  
  1236              // Normal daily RNG processing (request from current day)
  1237              currentWord = _applyDailyRng(day, currentWord);
  1238              coinflip.processCoinflipPayouts(bonusFlip, currentWord, day);
  1239              quests.rollDailyQuest(day, currentWord);
  1240  
  1241              // Resolve the sentinel-stamped gambling-burn pool if any (INV-13). Reading the
  1242              // sentinel rather than deriving `day - 1` makes multi-day RNG stalls correct by
  1243              // construction: the sentinel always names the (at most one) unresolved day, so a
  1244              // single resolve call after the stall recovers covers the stuck pool exactly.
  1245              {
  1246                  IStakedDegenerusStonk sdgnrs = IStakedDegenerusStonk(
  1247                      ContractAddresses.SDGNRS
  1248                  );
  1249                  uint24 toResolve = sdgnrs.pendingResolveDay();
  1250                  if (toResolve != 0) {
  1251                      uint16 redemptionRoll = uint16(
  1252                          ((currentWord >> 8) % 151) + 25
  1253                      );
  1254                      sdgnrs.resolveRedemptionPeriod(redemptionRoll, toResolve);
  1255                  }
  1256              }
  1257  
  1258              _finalizeLootboxRng(currentWord);
  1259              return (currentWord, gapDays);
  1260          }
  1261  
  1262          // Waiting for VRF - check for timeout retry
  1263          if (rngRequestTime != 0) {
  1264              uint48 elapsed = ts - rngRequestTime;
  1265              if (elapsed >= 12 hours) {
  1266                  _requestRng(isTicketJackpotDay, lvl);
  1267                  return (1, 0);
  1268              }
  1269              revert RngNotReady();
  1270          }
  1271  
  1272          // Need fresh RNG
  1273          _requestRng(isTicketJackpotDay, lvl);
  1274          return (1, 0);
  1275      }
  1276  
  1277      function _finalizeLootboxRng(uint256 rngWord) private {
  1278          uint48 index = uint48(_lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK)) - 1;
  1279          if (lootboxRngWordByIndex[index] != 0) return;
  1280          lootboxRngWordByIndex[index] = rngWord;
  1281          emit LootboxRngApplied(index, rngWord, vrfRequestId);
  1282      }
  1283  
  1284      /// @dev Game-over RNG gate with fallback for stalled VRF.
  1285      ///      After 3-day timeout, uses earliest historical VRF word as fallback (more secure
  1286      ///      than blockhash since it's already verified on-chain and cannot be manipulated).
  1287      ///      Also resolves any pending gambling burn redemptions (mirrors rngGate behavior, CP-06 fix).
  1288      /// @return word RNG word, 1 if request sent, or 0 if waiting on fallback.
  1289      function _gameOverEntropy(
  1290          uint48 ts,
  1291          uint24 day,
  1292          uint24 lvl,
  1293          bool isTicketJackpotDay
  1294      ) private returns (uint256 word) {
  1295          if (rngWordByDay[day] != 0) return rngWordByDay[day];
  1296  
  1297          uint256 currentWord = rngWordCurrent;
  1298          if (currentWord != 0 && rngRequestTime != 0) {
  1299              currentWord = _applyDailyRng(day, currentWord);
  1300              if (lvl != 0) {
  1301                  coinflip.processCoinflipPayouts(
  1302                      isTicketJackpotDay,
  1303                      currentWord,
  1304                      day
  1305                  );
  1306              }
  1307              // Resolve the sentinel-stamped gambling-burn pool if any (INV-13). Same shape as the
  1308              // rngGate redemption resolution path — sentinel-keyed so multi-day stalls resolve
  1309              // by construction.
  1310              {
  1311                  IStakedDegenerusStonk sdgnrs = IStakedDegenerusStonk(
  1312                      ContractAddresses.SDGNRS
  1313                  );
  1314                  uint24 toResolve = sdgnrs.pendingResolveDay();
  1315                  if (toResolve != 0) {
  1316                      uint16 redemptionRoll = uint16(
  1317                          ((currentWord >> 8) % 151) + 25
  1318                      );
  1319                      sdgnrs.resolveRedemptionPeriod(redemptionRoll, toResolve);
  1320                  }
  1321              }
  1322              _finalizeLootboxRng(currentWord);
  1323              return currentWord;
  1324          }
  1325  
  1326          if (rngRequestTime != 0) {
  1327              uint48 elapsed = ts - rngRequestTime;
  1328              if (elapsed >= GAMEOVER_RNG_FALLBACK_DELAY) {
  1329                  // Use earliest historical VRF word as fallback (more secure than blockhash)
  1330                  uint256 fallbackWord = _getHistoricalRngFallback(day);
  1331                  fallbackWord = _applyDailyRng(day, fallbackWord);
  1332                  if (lvl != 0) {
  1333                      coinflip.processCoinflipPayouts(
  1334                          isTicketJackpotDay,
  1335                          fallbackWord,
  1336                          day
  1337                      );
  1338                  }
  1339                  // Resolve the sentinel-stamped gambling-burn pool if any (INV-13). Fallback path
  1340                  // uses fallbackWord for the roll; sentinel still names the stuck day so resolves
  1341                  // are correct even after a 3-day GAMEOVER_RNG_FALLBACK_DELAY stall.
  1342                  {
  1343                      IStakedDegenerusStonk sdgnrs = IStakedDegenerusStonk(
  1344                          ContractAddresses.SDGNRS
  1345                      );
  1346                      uint24 toResolve = sdgnrs.pendingResolveDay();
  1347                      if (toResolve != 0) {
  1348                          uint16 redemptionRoll = uint16(
  1349                              ((fallbackWord >> 8) % 151) + 25
  1350                          );
  1351                          sdgnrs.resolveRedemptionPeriod(redemptionRoll, toResolve);
  1352                      }
  1353                  }
  1354                  _finalizeLootboxRng(fallbackWord);
  1355                  // Release the stall lock once fallback has committed; liveness now reads
  1356                  // from day math alone instead of short-circuiting on a stale VRF timer.
  1357                  rngRequestTime = 0;
  1358                  return fallbackWord;
  1359              }
  1360              revert RngNotReady();
  1361          }
  1362  
  1363          if (_tryRequestRng(isTicketJackpotDay, lvl)) {
  1364              return 1;
  1365          }
  1366  
  1367          // VRF request failed; start fallback timer (rngRequestTime != 0 acts as lock).
  1368          rngWordCurrent = 0;
  1369          rngRequestTime = ts;
  1370          return 0;
  1371      }
  1372  
  1373      /// @dev Get historical VRF fallback entropy for gameover RNG.
  1374      ///      Collects up to 5 early historical VRF words and hashes them together
  1375      ///      with currentDay and block.prevrandao. Historical words are committed VRF
  1376      ///      (non-manipulable), prevrandao adds unpredictability at the cost of 1-bit
  1377      ///      validator manipulation (propose or skip). Acceptable trade-off for a
  1378      ///      gameover-only fallback path when VRF is dead.
  1379      ///      If no historical words exist, falls through to prevrandao-only
  1380      ///      entropy. This can only happen at level 0 (zero VRF history means
  1381      ///      zero completed advances), so the 1-bit validator bias is irrelevant.
  1382      /// @param currentDay Current day index.
  1383      /// @return word Combined historical entropy.
  1384      function _getHistoricalRngFallback(
  1385          uint24 currentDay
  1386      ) private view returns (uint256 word) {
  1387          uint256 found;
  1388          uint256 combined;
  1389          uint24 searchLimit = currentDay > 30 ? 30 : currentDay;
  1390          for (uint24 searchDay = 1; searchDay < searchLimit; ) {
  1391              uint256 w = rngWordByDay[searchDay];
  1392              if (w != 0) {
  1393                  combined = uint256(keccak256(abi.encodePacked(combined, w)));
  1394                  unchecked {
  1395                      ++found;
  1396                  }
  1397                  if (found == 5) break;
  1398              }
  1399              unchecked {
  1400                  ++searchDay;
  1401              }
  1402          }
  1403  
  1404          word = uint256(
  1405              keccak256(abi.encodePacked(combined, currentDay, block.prevrandao))
  1406          );
  1407          if (word == 0) word = 1;
  1408      }
  1409  
  1410      /*+======================================================================+
  1411        |                    FUTURE PRIZE POOL DRAW                           |
  1412        +======================================================================+
  1413        |  Release a portion of the future prize pool once per level.         |
  1414        |  Normal levels draw 15%, x00 levels skip the draw.                   |
  1415        +======================================================================+*/
  1416  
  1417      function _nextToFutureBps(
  1418          uint32 elapsed,
  1419          uint24 lvl
  1420      ) internal pure returns (uint16) {
  1421          uint256 lvlBonus = (uint256(lvl % 100) / 10) * 100; // +1% per 10 levels within cycle
  1422          uint256 bps;
  1423          if (elapsed <= 1) {
  1424              bps = NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_FAST + lvlBonus;
  1425          } else if (elapsed <= 14) {
  1426              uint256 elapsedAfterDay = elapsed - 1;
  1427              uint256 delta = NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_FAST +
  1428                  lvlBonus -
  1429                  NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_MIN;
  1430              bps =
  1431                  NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_FAST +
  1432                  lvlBonus -
  1433                  (delta * elapsedAfterDay) /
  1434                  13;
  1435          } else if (elapsed <= 28) {
  1436              uint256 elapsedAfterMin = elapsed - 14;
  1437              uint256 delta = NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_FAST +
  1438                  lvlBonus -
  1439                  NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_MIN;
  1440              bps = NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_MIN + (delta * elapsedAfterMin) / 14;
  1441          } else {
  1442              bps =
  1443                  NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_FAST +
  1444                  lvlBonus +
  1445                  (elapsed - 28) *
  1446                  NEXT_TO_FUTURE_BPS_DAY_STEP;
  1447          }
  1448          return uint16(bps > 10_000 ? 10_000 : bps);
  1449      }
  1450  
  1451      /*+======================================================================+
  1452        |                    FUTURE TICKET ACTIVATION                         |
  1453        +======================================================================+
  1454        |  Future ticket rewards are staged per level and activated at the     |
  1455        |  start of the PREVIOUS level's jackpot phase (making them eligible    |
  1456        |  for daily jackpots and purchase phase rewards).                     |
  1457        +======================================================================+*/
  1458  
  1459      /// @dev Process a batch of future ticket rewards for the specified level.
  1460      ///      Called during jackpot phase of level N-1 to activate tickets for level N.
  1461      /// @param lvl Target level to activate (typically current level + 1).
  1462      /// @param entropy Today's daily RNG word (from rngGate) used for rarity rolls.
  1463      /// @return worked True if any queued entries were processed.
  1464      /// @return finished True if all queued entries for this level are processed.
  1465      /// @return writesUsed Number of SSTORE operations used in this batch.
  1466      function _processFutureTicketBatch(
  1467          uint24 lvl,
  1468          uint256 entropy
  1469      ) private returns (bool worked, bool finished, uint32 writesUsed) {
  1470          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
  1471              .GAME_MINT_MODULE
  1472              .delegatecall(
  1473                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
  1474                      IDegenerusGameMintModule.processFutureTicketBatch.selector,
  1475                      lvl,
  1476                      entropy
  1477                  )
  1478              );
  1479          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
  1480          if (data.length == 0) revert E();
  1481          return abi.decode(data, (bool, bool, uint32));
  1482      }
  1483  
  1484      /// @dev Before daily draws, process near-future ticket read queues.
  1485      ///      Caller passes level during jackpot phase (range lvl+1..lvl+4) or
  1486      ///      purchaseLevel during purchase phase (range lvl+2..lvl+5).
  1487      ///      FF promotion is handled separately at phase transition time.
  1488      /// @param lvl Base level (level during jackpot, purchaseLevel during purchase).
  1489      /// @param entropy Today's daily RNG word (from rngGate) threaded to ticket rarity rolls.
  1490      /// @return finished True when all target future levels are fully processed.
  1491      function _prepareFutureTickets(
  1492          uint24 lvl,
  1493          uint256 entropy
  1494      ) private returns (bool finished) {
  1495          uint24 startLevel = lvl + 1;
  1496          uint24 endLevel = lvl + 4;
  1497          uint24 resumeLevel = ticketLevel;
  1498  
  1499          // Continue an in-flight future level first to preserve progress.
  1500          if (resumeLevel >= startLevel && resumeLevel <= endLevel) {
  1501              (bool worked, bool levelFinished, ) = _processFutureTicketBatch(
  1502                  resumeLevel,
  1503                  entropy
  1504              );
  1505              if (worked || !levelFinished) return false;
  1506          }
  1507  
  1508          // Then probe remaining target levels in order.
  1509          for (uint24 target = startLevel; target <= endLevel; ) {
  1510              if (target != resumeLevel) {
  1511                  (bool worked, bool levelFinished, ) = _processFutureTicketBatch(
  1512                      target,
  1513                      entropy
  1514                  );
  1515                  if (worked || !levelFinished) return false;
  1516              }
  1517              unchecked {
  1518                  ++target;
  1519              }
  1520          }
  1521          return true;
  1522      }
  1523  
  1524      /*+======================================================================+
  1525        |                    TICKET / TOKEN AIRDROP BATCHING                         |
  1526        +======================================================================+
  1527        |  Ticket entries are processed in batches to prevent gas exhaustion.  |
  1528        |  Large purchases are queued and processed across multiple txs.       |
  1529        +======================================================================+*/
  1530  
  1531      /// @dev Process a batch of current level tickets via mint module delegatecall.
  1532      /// @param lvl Current level.
  1533      /// @return worked True if any tickets were processed.
  1534      /// @return finished True if all tickets for this level have been fully processed.
  1535      function _runProcessTicketBatch(
  1536          uint24 lvl
  1537      ) private returns (bool worked, bool finished) {
  1538          uint32 prevCursor = ticketCursor;
  1539          uint24 prevLevel = ticketLevel;
  1540          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
  1541              .GAME_MINT_MODULE
  1542              .delegatecall(
  1543                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
  1544                      IDegenerusGameMintModule.processTicketBatch.selector,
  1545                      lvl
  1546                  )
  1547              );
  1548          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
  1549          if (data.length == 0) revert E();
  1550          finished = abi.decode(data, (bool));
  1551          worked = (ticketCursor != prevCursor) || (ticketLevel != prevLevel);
  1552      }
  1553  
  1554      /// @dev Process jackpot→purchase transition housekeeping (vault perpetual tickets + auto-stake).
  1555      ///      Vault addresses (SDGNRS, VAULT) get generic queued tickets.
  1556      /// @param purchaseLevel Current purchase level (level + 1).
  1557      /// @return finished True if all transition work completed this call.
  1558      function _processPhaseTransition(
  1559          uint24 purchaseLevel
  1560      ) private returns (bool finished) {
  1561          // Vault perpetual tickets: 16 generic tickets per level for DGNRS and VAULT
  1562          uint24 targetLevel = purchaseLevel + 99;
  1563          _queueTickets(
  1564              ContractAddresses.SDGNRS,
  1565              targetLevel,
  1566              VAULT_PERPETUAL_TICKETS,
  1567              true
  1568          );
  1569          _queueTickets(
  1570              ContractAddresses.VAULT,
  1571              targetLevel,
  1572              VAULT_PERPETUAL_TICKETS,
  1573              true
  1574          );
  1575  
  1576          // Auto-stake all non-claimable ETH into stETH for yield generation.
  1577          // Non-blocking: if stETH contract fails, game continues normally.
  1578          _autoStakeExcessEth();
  1579  
  1580          return true;
  1581      }
  1582  
  1583      /// @dev Stake all ETH above claimablePool into stETH via Lido.
  1584      ///      Uses try/catch so stETH is never a hard dependency — game
  1585      ///      continues even if Lido is paused or the call reverts.
  1586      function _autoStakeExcessEth() private {
  1587          uint256 ethBal = address(this).balance;
  1588          uint256 reserve = claimablePool;
  1589          if (ethBal <= reserve) return;
  1590          uint256 stakeable = ethBal - reserve;
  1591          try steth.submit{value: stakeable}(address(0)) returns (
  1592              uint256
  1593          ) {} catch {
  1594              emit StEthStakeFailed(stakeable);
  1595          }
  1596      }
  1597  
  1598      /// @dev Request new VRF random word from Chainlink.
  1599      ///      Sets RNG lock to prevent manipulation during pending window.
  1600      /// @param isTicketJackpotDay True if this is the last purchase day.
  1601      /// @param lvl Current level.
  1602      function _requestRng(bool isTicketJackpotDay, uint24 lvl) private {
  1603          // Hard revert if Chainlink request fails; this intentionally halts game progress until VRF funding/config is fixed.
  1604          uint256 id = vrfCoordinator.requestRandomWords(
  1605              VRFRandomWordsRequest({
  1606                  keyHash: vrfKeyHash,
  1607                  subId: vrfSubscriptionId,
  1608                  requestConfirmations: VRF_REQUEST_CONFIRMATIONS,
  1609                  callbackGasLimit: VRF_CALLBACK_GAS_LIMIT,
  1610                  numWords: 1,
  1611                  extraArgs: hex"" // Empty for LINK payment (default)
  1612              })
  1613          );
  1614          _finalizeRngRequest(isTicketJackpotDay, lvl, id);
  1615      }
  1616  
  1617      function _tryRequestRng(
  1618          bool isTicketJackpotDay,
  1619          uint24 lvl
  1620      ) private returns (bool requested) {
  1621          try
  1622              vrfCoordinator.requestRandomWords(
  1623                  VRFRandomWordsRequest({
  1624                      keyHash: vrfKeyHash,
  1625                      subId: vrfSubscriptionId,
  1626                      requestConfirmations: VRF_REQUEST_CONFIRMATIONS,
  1627                      callbackGasLimit: VRF_CALLBACK_GAS_LIMIT,
  1628                      numWords: 1,
  1629                      extraArgs: hex"" // Empty for LINK payment (default)
  1630                  })
  1631              )
  1632          returns (uint256 id) {
  1633              _finalizeRngRequest(isTicketJackpotDay, lvl, id);
  1634              requested = true;
  1635          } catch {}
  1636      }
  1637  
  1638      /// @dev Submit a single-word VRF request on the current coordinator.
  1639      /// @param confirmations Block confirmations for this request's gas lane.
  1640      /// @return id The Chainlink request ID.
  1641      function _requestVrfWord(uint16 confirmations) private returns (uint256 id) {
  1642          id = vrfCoordinator.requestRandomWords(
  1643              VRFRandomWordsRequest({
  1644                  keyHash: vrfKeyHash,
  1645                  subId: vrfSubscriptionId,
  1646                  requestConfirmations: confirmations,
  1647                  callbackGasLimit: VRF_CALLBACK_GAS_LIMIT,
  1648                  numWords: 1,
  1649                  extraArgs: hex""
  1650              })
  1651          );
  1652      }
  1653  
  1654      /// @dev Write the VRF coordinator, subscription, and key hash together.
  1655      /// @param coord VRF coordinator address.
  1656      /// @param sub VRF subscription ID for LINK billing.
  1657      /// @param key VRF key hash for gas lane selection.
  1658      function _setVrfConfig(address coord, uint256 sub, bytes32 key) internal {
  1659          vrfCoordinator = IVRFCoordinator(coord);
  1660          vrfSubscriptionId = sub;
  1661          vrfKeyHash = key;
  1662      }
  1663  
  1664      function _finalizeRngRequest(
  1665          bool isTicketJackpotDay,
  1666          uint24 lvl,
  1667          uint256 requestId
  1668      ) private {
  1669          bool isRetry = vrfRequestId != 0 &&
  1670              rngRequestTime != 0 &&
  1671              rngWordCurrent == 0;
  1672          if (!isRetry) {
  1673              // Fresh request: advance lootbox index so new purchases target the NEXT RNG.
  1674              _lrWrite(
  1675                  LR_INDEX_SHIFT,
  1676                  LR_INDEX_MASK,
  1677                  _lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK) + 1
  1678              );
  1679              _lrWrite(LR_PENDING_ETH_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_ETH_MASK, 0);
  1680              _lrWrite(LR_PENDING_BURNIE_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_BURNIE_MASK, 0);
  1681          }
  1682          // Retry: index already advanced from the original request. No action needed —
  1683          // lootboxRngIndex - 1 still points to the pending index regardless of request ID.
  1684  
  1685          vrfRequestId = requestId;
  1686          rngWordCurrent = 0;
  1687          rngRequestTime = uint48(block.timestamp);
  1688          rngLockedFlag = true;
  1689  
  1690          // Increment level at RNG request time when lastPurchaseDay = true.
  1691          // lvl is already purchaseLevel (= level + 1), so set directly.
  1692          // Only on fresh request - retry would double-increment.
  1693          if (isTicketJackpotDay && !isRetry) {
  1694              // Snapshot affiliate reward before level increment.
  1695              // Scores routed to lvl (= level + 1) during the purchase phase just ended.
  1696              _rewardTopAffiliate(lvl);
  1697              level = lvl;
  1698  
  1699              // Decimator window: open at x4/x99, close at x5/x00
  1700              uint24 mod100 = lvl % 100;
  1701              uint24 mod10 = lvl % 10;
  1702              if ((mod10 == 4 && mod100 != 94) || mod100 == 99) {
  1703                  decWindowOpen = true;
  1704              } else if (
  1705                  decWindowOpen && ((mod10 == 5 && mod100 != 95) || mod100 == 0)
  1706              ) {
  1707                  decWindowOpen = false;
  1708              }
  1709  
  1710              // Resolve charity governance for the completed level.
  1711              // lvl is the NEW level (old level + 1). CHARITY.currentLevel tracks
  1712              // the CURRENT governance level (starts at 0, incremented by pickCharity).
  1713              // The game's level 0->1 transition means level 0 gameplay is complete,
  1714              // so we resolve governance for level 0 = lvl - 1.
  1715              charityResolve.pickCharity(lvl - 1);
  1716          }
  1717      }
  1718  
  1719      /// @notice Emergency VRF coordinator rotation (governance-gated).
  1720      /// @dev Access: ContractAddresses.ADMIN only. The Admin contract enforces
  1721      ///      stall duration via sDGNRS-holder governance (propose/vote/execute).
  1722      /// @param newCoordinator New VRF coordinator address.
  1723      /// @param newSubId New subscription ID.
  1724      /// @param newKeyHash New key hash for the gas lane.
  1725      function updateVrfCoordinatorAndSub(
  1726          address newCoordinator,
  1727          uint256 newSubId,
  1728          bytes32 newKeyHash
  1729      ) external {
  1730          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.ADMIN) revert E();
  1731  
  1732          address current = address(vrfCoordinator);
  1733          _setVrfConfig(newCoordinator, newSubId, newKeyHash);
  1734  
  1735          // Detect what is in flight and re-issue on the new coordinator (D-01/D-02).
  1736          // The request is accepted before the new subscription is LINK-funded; DegenerusAdmin
  1737          // funds it in the same _executeSwap transaction (transferAndCall), and the VRF node
  1738          // fulfills once funded. retryLootboxRng is the failsafe if the new coordinator stalls.
  1739          if (_lrRead(LR_MID_DAY_SHIFT, LR_MID_DAY_MASK) != 0) {
  1740              // Mid-day in flight: KEEP LR_MID_DAY=1; LR_INDEX preserved so the new word lands
  1741              // in the same reserved slot [N] via the mid-day fulfillment branch (:1772).
  1742              vrfRequestId = _requestVrfWord(VRF_MIDDAY_CONFIRMATIONS);
  1743              rngRequestTime = uint48(block.timestamp);
  1744          } else if (rngLockedFlag) {
  1745              // Daily in flight: KEEP rngLockedFlag=true.
  1746              if (rngWordCurrent == 0) {
  1747                  // Daily word not yet delivered: re-request on the new coordinator (-> :1768).
  1748                  vrfRequestId = _requestVrfWord(VRF_REQUEST_CONFIRMATIONS);
  1749                  rngRequestTime = uint48(block.timestamp);
  1750              }
  1751              // else: daily word already delivered and valid -> preserve it; no re-issue
  1752              // (a fresh callback would be rejected by the :1761 rngWordCurrent!=0 guard).
  1753          }
  1754          // else: nothing in flight -> config repoint only; no re-issue, no flag change.
  1755  
  1756          // Intentional: totalFlipReversals is NOT reset here. Nudges were purchased
  1757          // with irreversible BURNIE burns before or during the stall. They carry over
  1758          // and apply to the first post-swap VRF word via _applyDailyRng. Resetting
  1759          // would steal user value (burned BURNIE for zero effect).
  1760  
  1761          emit VrfCoordinatorUpdated(current, newCoordinator);
  1762      }
  1763  
  1764      /// @dev Unlock RNG after processing is complete for the day.
  1765      ///      Resets VRF state and re-enables RNG usage.
  1766      /// @param day Current day index to record.
  1767      function _unlockRng(uint24 day) private {
  1768          dailyIdx = day;
  1769          rngLockedFlag = false;
  1770          rngWordCurrent = 0;
  1771          vrfRequestId = 0;
  1772          rngRequestTime = 0;
  1773          _unfreezePool();
  1774      }
  1775  
  1776      /// @notice Chainlink VRF callback for random word fulfillment.
  1777      /// @dev Access: VRF coordinator only.
  1778      ///      Daily RNG: stores word for advanceGame processing (nudges applied there).
  1779      ///      Mid-day RNG: directly finalizes lootbox RNG, no advanceGame needed.
  1780      ///      SECURITY: Validates requestId and coordinator address.
  1781      /// @param requestId The request ID to match.
  1782      /// @param randomWords Array containing the random word (length 1).
  1783      function rawFulfillRandomWords(
  1784          uint256 requestId,
  1785          uint256[] calldata randomWords
  1786      ) external {
  1787          if (msg.sender != address(vrfCoordinator)) revert E();
  1788          if (requestId != vrfRequestId || rngWordCurrent != 0) return;
  1789  
  1790          uint256 word = randomWords[0];
  1791          if (word == 0) word = 1;
  1792  
  1793          if (rngLockedFlag) {
  1794              // Daily RNG: store for advanceGame processing (nudges applied there)
  1795              rngWordCurrent = word;
  1796          } else {
  1797              // Mid-day RNG: directly finalize lootbox and clear state
  1798              uint48 index = uint48(_lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK)) - 1;
  1799              lootboxRngWordByIndex[index] = word;
  1800              emit LootboxRngApplied(index, word, requestId);
  1801              vrfRequestId = 0;
  1802              rngRequestTime = 0;
  1803          }
  1804      }
  1805  
  1806      /// @dev Backfill rngWordByDay and process coinflip payouts for gap days
  1807      ///      caused by VRF stall. Derives deterministic words from the first
  1808      ///      post-gap VRF word via keccak256(vrfWord, gapDay).
  1809      ///      NOTE: Gap days get zero nudges (totalFlipReversals not consumed).
  1810      ///      NOTE: resolveRedemptionPeriod is NOT called for backfilled gap days —
  1811      ///      the redemption timer continued ticking in real time during the stall;
  1812      ///      it resolves only on the current day via the normal rngGate path.
  1813      /// @param vrfWord The first post-gap VRF random word.
  1814      /// @param startDay First gap day (dailyIdx + 1).
  1815      /// @param endDay Current day (exclusive — not backfilled, handled by normal path).
  1816      /// @param bonusFlip Whether presale bonus applies to coinflip resolution.
  1817      function _backfillGapDays(
  1818          uint256 vrfWord,
  1819          uint24 startDay,
  1820          uint24 endDay,
  1821          bool bonusFlip
  1822      ) private {
  1823          // Cap at 120 gap days to stay within block gas limit (~9M gas).
  1824          // Backfills oldest days first (most likely to have active coinflips).
  1825          if (endDay - startDay > 120) endDay = startDay + 120;
  1826          for (uint24 gapDay = startDay; gapDay < endDay; ) {
  1827              uint256 derivedWord = uint256(
  1828                  keccak256(abi.encodePacked(vrfWord, gapDay))
  1829              );
  1830              if (derivedWord == 0) derivedWord = 1;
  1831              rngWordByDay[gapDay] = derivedWord;
  1832              coinflip.processCoinflipPayouts(bonusFlip, derivedWord, gapDay);
  1833              emit DailyRngApplied(gapDay, derivedWord, 0, derivedWord);
  1834              unchecked {
  1835                  ++gapDay;
  1836              }
  1837          }
  1838      }
  1839  
  1840      /// @dev Backfill any lootbox RNG indices that never received a VRF word.
  1841      ///      Scans backwards from lootboxRngIndex - 1 until hitting a filled index.
  1842      ///      Uses VRF-derived entropy so lootbox outcomes cannot be front-run.
  1843      /// @param vrfWord Fresh VRF word from the post-gap callback.
  1844      function _backfillOrphanedLootboxIndices(uint256 vrfWord) private {
  1845          uint48 idx = uint48(_lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK));
  1846          if (idx <= 1) return; // nothing reserved yet
  1847  
  1848          // Scan backwards from the most recent reserved index
  1849          for (uint48 i = idx - 1; i >= 1; ) {
  1850              if (lootboxRngWordByIndex[i] != 0) break; // hit a filled index, done
  1851  
  1852              uint256 fallbackWord = uint256(
  1853                  keccak256(abi.encodePacked(vrfWord, i))
  1854              );
  1855              if (fallbackWord == 0) fallbackWord = 1;
  1856              lootboxRngWordByIndex[i] = fallbackWord;
  1857              emit LootboxRngApplied(i, fallbackWord, 0);
  1858  
  1859              unchecked {
  1860                  --i;
  1861              }
  1862          }
  1863      }
  1864  
  1865      /// @dev Apply daily RNG nudges, record the word, and emit the finalized word.
  1866      function _applyDailyRng(
  1867          uint24 day,
  1868          uint256 rawWord
  1869      ) private returns (uint256 finalWord) {
  1870          uint256 nudges = totalFlipReversals;
  1871          finalWord = rawWord;
  1872          if (nudges != 0) {
  1873              unchecked {
  1874                  finalWord += nudges;
  1875              }
  1876              totalFlipReversals = 0;
  1877          }
  1878          rngWordCurrent = finalWord;
  1879          rngWordByDay[day] = finalWord;
  1880          lastVrfProcessedTimestamp = uint48(block.timestamp);
  1881          emit DailyRngApplied(day, rawWord, nudges, finalWord);
  1882      }
  1883  
  1884      /*+======================================================================+
  1885        |                    DRIP PROJECTION MATH                             |
  1886        +======================================================================+*/
  1887  
  1888      /// @dev Compute base^exp in 1e18 scale via repeated squaring.
  1889      ///      Max 7 iterations for exp <= 120. ~700 gas.
  1890      function _wadPow(uint256 base, uint256 exp) private pure returns (uint256) {
  1891          uint256 result = 1 ether;
  1892          while (exp > 0) {
  1893              if (exp & 1 == 1) {
  1894                  result = (result * base) / 1 ether;
  1895              }
  1896              base = (base * base) / 1 ether;
  1897              exp >>= 1;
  1898          }
  1899          return result;
  1900      }
  1901  
  1902      /// @dev Projected total drip from futurePool over n remaining days.
  1903      ///      Closed-form geometric series: futurePool * (1 - 0.9925^n).
  1904      function _projectedDrip(
  1905          uint256 futurePool,
  1906          uint256 daysRemaining
  1907      ) private pure returns (uint256) {
  1908          if (daysRemaining == 0) return 0;
  1909          uint256 decayN = _wadPow(DECAY_RATE, daysRemaining);
  1910          return (futurePool * (1 ether - decayN)) / 1 ether;
  1911      }
  1912  
  1913      /// @dev Set or clear gameOverPossible based on drip projection vs nextPool deficit.
  1914      /// @dev Evaluates gameOverPossible flag and returns whether nextPool >= target.
  1915      ///      At L10+: flag is set if projected drip cannot cover the gap.
  1916      ///      Below L10: flag is always cleared.
  1917      function _evaluateGameOverAndTarget(
  1918          uint24 lvl,
  1919          uint24 psd,
  1920          uint24 day
  1921      ) private returns (bool targetMet) {
  1922          uint256 nextPool = _getNextPrizePool();
  1923          uint256 target = levelPrizePool[lvl];
  1924          targetMet = nextPool >= target;
  1925          if (lvl < 10 || targetMet) {
  1926              gameOverPossible = false;
  1927              return targetMet;
  1928          }
  1929          uint256 deficit = target - nextPool;
  1930          uint256 daysRemaining = psd + 120 > day ? psd + 120 - day : 0;
  1931          gameOverPossible =
  1932              _projectedDrip(_getFuturePrizePool(), daysRemaining) < deficit;
  1933      }
  1934  }

    92      /// @dev Bubbles up revert reason from delegatecall failure.
    93      /// @param reason The revert data from the failed delegatecall.
    94      function _revertDelegate(bytes memory reason) private pure {
    95          if (reason.length == 0) revert E();
    96          assembly ("memory-safe") {
    97              revert(add(32, reason), mload(reason))
    98          }
    99      }
   100  
   101      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   102      // Constants
   103      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   104  
   105      /// @dev Basis points denominator (10000 = 100%).
   106      uint16 private constant BPS_DENOMINATOR = 10_000;
   107  
   108      /// @dev Multiplier cap for Decimator burns (200 mints worth).
   109      uint256 private constant DECIMATOR_MULTIPLIER_CAP = 200 * PRICE_COIN_UNIT;
   110  
   111      /// @dev Maximum denominator for Decimator buckets (2-12 inclusive).
   112      uint8 private constant DECIMATOR_MAX_DENOM = 12;
   113  
   114      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   115      // External Entry Points (delegatecall targets)
   116      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   117  
   118      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   119      // Decimator Burn Tracking
   120      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   121  
   122      /// @notice Record a Decimator burn for jackpot eligibility.
   123      /// @dev Called by coin contract on every Decimator burn.
   124      ///      First burn sets player's bucket (denominator) choice.
   125      ///      Subbucket is deterministically assigned from hash(player, lvl, bucket).
   126      ///      Subsequent burns accumulate in that bucket unless a strictly better
   127      ///      bucket (lower denominator) is provided. On improvement, previous burn
   128      ///      is removed from old aggregate, carried over to the new bucket, and entry migrates.
   129      ///      Burn amount capped at uint192.max with saturation.
   130      /// @param player Address of the player.
   131      /// @param lvl Current game level.
   132      /// @param bucket Player's chosen denominator (2-12).
   133      /// @param baseAmount Burn amount before multiplier.
   134      /// @param multBps Player bonus multiplier in basis points (10000 = 1x).
   135      /// @return bucketUsed The bucket actually used (may differ from requested if not an improvement).
   136      /// @custom:access Restricted to coin contract.
   137      function recordDecBurn(
   138          address player,
   139          uint24 lvl,
   140          uint8 bucket,
   141          uint256 baseAmount,
   142          uint256 multBps
   143      ) external returns (uint8 bucketUsed) {
   144          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.COIN) revert OnlyCoin();
   145  
   146          DecEntry storage e = decBurn[lvl][player];
   147          DecEntry memory m = e;
   148          uint192 prevBurn = m.burn;
   149  
   150          // First burn this level: set bucket and deterministic subbucket.
   151          if (m.bucket == 0) {
   152              m.bucket = bucket;
   153              m.subBucket = _decSubbucketFor(player, lvl, bucket);
   154          } else if (bucket != 0 && bucket < m.bucket) {
   155              // Better bucket selected: migrate burn to new subbucket.
   156              _decRemoveSubbucket(lvl, m.bucket, m.subBucket, prevBurn);
   157              m.bucket = bucket;
   158              m.subBucket = _decSubbucketFor(player, lvl, bucket);
   159              // Seed new subbucket with carried-over burn.
   160              if (prevBurn != 0) {
   161                  _decUpdateSubbucket(lvl, m.bucket, m.subBucket, prevBurn);
   162              }
   163          }
   164  
   165          bucketUsed = m.bucket;
   166  
   167          uint256 effectiveAmount = _decEffectiveAmount(
   168              uint256(prevBurn),
   169              baseAmount,
   170              multBps
   171          );
   172  
   173          // Accumulate burn with uint192 saturation
   174          uint256 updated = uint256(prevBurn) + effectiveAmount;
   175          if (updated > type(uint192).max) updated = type(uint192).max;
   176          uint192 newBurn = uint192(updated);
   177          e.burn = newBurn;
   178          e.bucket = m.bucket;
   179          e.subBucket = m.subBucket;
   180  
   181          // Update subbucket aggregate if burn increased
   182          uint192 delta = newBurn - prevBurn;
   183          if (delta != 0) {
   184              _decUpdateSubbucket(lvl, bucketUsed, m.subBucket, delta);
   185              emit DecBurnRecorded(
   186                  player,
   187                  lvl,
   188                  bucketUsed,
   189                  m.subBucket,
   190                  delta,
   191                  newBurn
   192              );
   193          }
   194  
   195          return bucketUsed;
   196      }
   197  
   198      /*+======================================================================+
   199        |                    DECIMATOR JACKPOT RESOLUTION                      |
   200        +======================================================================+
   201        |  Snapshots winning subbuckets for deferred claim distribution.       |
   202        +======================================================================+*/
   203  
   204      /// @notice Snapshot Decimator jackpot winners for deferred claims.
   205      /// @dev Selects winning subbucket per denominator and snapshots totals.
   206      ///      Actual distribution happens via claim functions.
   207      ///      Returns poolWei if level already snapshotted or no qualifying burns.
   208      /// @param poolWei Total ETH prize pool for this level.
   209      /// @param lvl Level number being resolved.
   210      /// @param rngWord VRF-derived randomness seed.
   211      /// @return returnAmountWei Amount to return (non-zero if no winners or already snapshotted).
   212      /// @custom:access Restricted to game contract.
   213      function runDecimatorJackpot(
   214          uint256 poolWei,
   215          uint24 lvl,
   216          uint256 rngWord
   217      ) external returns (uint256 returnAmountWei) {
   218          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.GAME) revert OnlyGame();
   219  
   220          // Prevent double-snapshotting: return pool if this level already snapshotted
   221          if (decClaimRounds[lvl].poolWei != 0) {
   222              return poolWei;
   223          }
   224  
   225          uint256 totalBurn;
   226          uint64 packedOffsets;
   227  
   228          // Select winning subbucket for each denominator (2-12)
   229          uint256 decSeed = rngWord;
   230          for (uint8 denom = 2; denom <= DECIMATOR_MAX_DENOM; ) {
   231              // Deterministically select winning subbucket from VRF
   232              uint8 winningSub = _decWinningSubbucket(decSeed, denom);
   233              packedOffsets = _packDecWinningSubbucket(
   234                  packedOffsets,
   235                  denom,
   236                  winningSub
   237              );
   238  
   239              // Accumulate burn total from winning subbucket
   240              uint256 subTotal = decBucketBurnTotal[lvl][denom][winningSub];
   241              if (subTotal != 0) {
   242                  totalBurn += subTotal;
   243              }
   244  
   245              unchecked {
   246                  ++denom;
   247              }
   248          }
   249  
   250          // No qualifying burns: return full pool
   251          if (totalBurn == 0) {
   252              return poolWei;
   253          }
   254  
   255          // Store packed winning subbuckets for claim validation
   256          decBucketOffsetPacked[lvl] = packedOffsets;
   257          emit DecimatorResolved(lvl, packedOffsets, poolWei, totalBurn);
   258  
   259          // Snapshot claim round for this level (persistent — no expiry)
   260          decClaimRounds[lvl].poolWei = poolWei;
   261          decClaimRounds[lvl].totalBurn = uint232(totalBurn);
   262          decClaimRounds[lvl].rngWord = rngWord;
   263  
   264          return 0; // All funds held for claims
   265      }
   266  
   267      /*+======================================================================+
   268        |                      DECIMATOR CLAIM FUNCTIONS                       |
   269        +======================================================================+*/
   270  
   271      /// @dev Internal claim validation and marking.
   272      ///      Validates eligibility and marks as claimed if successful.
   273      /// @param player Address claiming the jackpot.
   274      /// @param lvl Level to claim from.
   275      /// @return amountWei Pro-rata payout amount.
   276      /// @custom:reverts DecClaimInactive When no decimator snapshot exists for this level.
   277      /// @custom:reverts DecAlreadyClaimed When player has already claimed for this level.
   278      /// @custom:reverts DecNotWinner When player's subbucket did not win.
   279      function _consumeDecClaim(
   280          address player,
   281          uint24 lvl
   282      ) internal returns (uint256 amountWei) {
   283          DecClaimRound storage round = decClaimRounds[lvl];
   284          if (round.poolWei == 0) revert DecClaimInactive();
   285  
   286          DecEntry storage e = decBurn[lvl][player];
   287          if (e.claimed != 0) revert DecAlreadyClaimed();
   288  
   289          // Calculate pro-rata share if player's subbucket won
   290          uint64 packedOffsets = decBucketOffsetPacked[lvl];
   291          uint256 totalBurn = uint256(round.totalBurn);
   292          amountWei = _decClaimableFromEntry(
   293              round.poolWei,
   294              totalBurn,
   295              e,
   296              packedOffsets
   297          );
   298          if (amountWei == 0) revert DecNotWinner();
   299  
   300          // Mark as claimed to prevent double-claiming
   301          e.claimed = 1;
   302      }
   303  
   304      /// @notice Consume Decimator claim on behalf of player.
   305      /// @dev Used for game-initiated claims.
   306      /// @param player Address to claim for.
   307      /// @param lvl Level to claim from.
   308      /// @return amountWei Pro-rata payout amount.
   309      /// @custom:access Restricted to game contract.
   310      function consumeDecClaim(
   311          address player,
   312          uint24 lvl
   313      ) external returns (uint256 amountWei) {
   314          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.GAME) revert OnlyGame();
   315          return _consumeDecClaim(player, lvl);
   316      }
   317  
   318      /// @notice Claim Decimator jackpot for caller.
   319      /// @dev Public function for players to claim their own jackpot.
   320      ///      Credits payout to player's claimable balance.
   321      /// @param lvl Level to claim from.
   322      /// @custom:reverts DecClaimInactive When no decimator snapshot exists for this level.
   323      /// @custom:reverts DecAlreadyClaimed When caller has already claimed for this level.
   324      /// @custom:reverts DecNotWinner When caller's subbucket did not win.
   325      function claimDecimatorJackpot(uint24 lvl) external {
   326          // Block claims while prize pools are frozen (active during VRF window).
   327          // This path writes to futurePrizePool (lootbox portion) — allowing it
   328          // during freeze would corrupt the live pool that advanceGame operates on.
   329          if (prizePoolFrozen) revert E();
   330  
   331          // Capture the winning entry's bucket before the claim consumes it; the bucket encodes
   332          // the activity score sealed at decimator-burn time (see _minScoreForBucket), freezing
   333          // the lootbox EV multiplier instead of reading a live, post-word score at claim.
   334          uint8 winBucket = decBurn[lvl][msg.sender].bucket;
   335          uint256 amountWei = _consumeDecClaim(msg.sender, lvl);
   336  
   337          if (gameOver) {
   338              _creditClaimable(msg.sender, amountWei);
   339              emit DecimatorClaimed(msg.sender, lvl, amountWei, amountWei, 0);
   340              return;
   341          }
   342  
   343          uint256 lootboxPortion = _creditDecJackpotClaimCore(
   344              msg.sender,
   345              amountWei,
   346              decClaimRounds[lvl].rngWord,
   347              _minScoreForBucket(winBucket, lvl)
   348          );
   349          if (lootboxPortion != 0) {
   350              _setFuturePrizePool(_getFuturePrizePool() + lootboxPortion);
   351          }
   352          emit DecimatorClaimed(
   353              msg.sender,
   354              lvl,
   355              amountWei,
   356              amountWei - lootboxPortion,
   357              lootboxPortion
   358          );
   359      }
   360  
   361      /// @notice Check if player can claim Decimator jackpot for a level.
   362      /// @dev View function for UI to show claimable amounts.
   363      /// @param player Address to check.
   364      /// @param lvl Level to check.
   365      /// @return amountWei Claimable amount (0 if not winner or already claimed).
   366      /// @return winner True if player is a winner for this level.
   367      function decClaimable(
   368          address player,
   369          uint24 lvl
   370      ) external view returns (uint256 amountWei, bool winner) {
   371          DecClaimRound storage round = decClaimRounds[lvl];
   372          if (round.poolWei == 0) {
   373              return (0, false);
   374          }
   375          return _decClaimable(round, player, lvl);
   376      }
   377  
   378      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   379      // Decimator Helpers
   380      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   381  
   382      /// @dev Credits decimator claim in normal (non-gameover) mode.
   383      ///      Callers must ensure amount != 0 and account != address(0).
   384      /// @return lootboxPortion Amount routed to lootbox tickets.
   385      function _creditDecJackpotClaimCore(
   386          address account,
   387          uint256 amount,
   388          uint256 rngWord,
   389          uint16 evScore
   390      ) private returns (uint256 lootboxPortion) {
   391          // Split 50/50: half ETH, half lootbox tickets
   392          uint256 ethPortion = amount >> 1;
   393          lootboxPortion = amount - ethPortion;
   394  
   395          _creditClaimable(account, ethPortion);
   396  
   397          // Lootbox portion is no longer claimable ETH; remove from reserved pool.
   398          claimablePool -= uint128(lootboxPortion); // Safe: lootboxPortion is a fraction of claimablePool, fits uint128
   399          _awardDecimatorLootbox(account, lootboxPortion, rngWord, evScore);
   400      }
   401  
   402      /// @dev Apply multiplier until the cap is reached; extra amount is counted at 1x.
   403      /// @param prevBurn Previous accumulated burn amount.
   404      /// @param baseAmount New burn amount before multiplier.
   405      /// @param multBps Multiplier in basis points.
   406      /// @return effectiveAmount The effective burn amount after applying capped multiplier.
   407      function _decEffectiveAmount(
   408          uint256 prevBurn,
   409          uint256 baseAmount,
   410          uint256 multBps
   411      ) private pure returns (uint256 effectiveAmount) {
   412          if (baseAmount == 0) return 0;
   413          if (
   414              multBps <= BPS_DENOMINATOR || prevBurn >= DECIMATOR_MULTIPLIER_CAP
   415          ) {
   416              return baseAmount;
   417          }
   418  
   419          uint256 remaining = DECIMATOR_MULTIPLIER_CAP - prevBurn;
   420          uint256 fullEffective = (baseAmount * multBps) / BPS_DENOMINATOR;
   421          if (fullEffective <= remaining) return fullEffective;
   422  
   423          uint256 maxMultBase = (remaining * BPS_DENOMINATOR) / multBps;
   424          uint256 multiplied = (maxMultBase * multBps) / BPS_DENOMINATOR;
   425          effectiveAmount = multiplied + (baseAmount - maxMultBase);
   426      }
   427  
   428      /// @dev Deterministically select winning subbucket for a denominator.
   429      /// @param entropy VRF-derived randomness.
   430      /// @param denom Denominator (2-12).
   431      /// @return Winning subbucket index (0 to denom-1).
   432      function _decWinningSubbucket(
   433          uint256 entropy,
   434          uint8 denom
   435      ) private pure returns (uint8) {
   436          return
   437              uint8(uint256(keccak256(abi.encodePacked(entropy, denom))) % denom);
   438      }
   439  
   440      /// @dev Pack a winning subbucket into the packed uint64.
   441      ///      Layout: 4 bits per denom, starting at denom 2.
   442      /// @param packed Current packed value.
   443      /// @param denom Denominator to pack (2-12).
   444      /// @param sub Winning subbucket for this denom.
   445      /// @return Updated packed value.
   446      function _packDecWinningSubbucket(
   447          uint64 packed,
   448          uint8 denom,
   449          uint8 sub
   450      ) private pure returns (uint64) {
   451          uint8 shift = (denom - 2) << 2; // 4 bits per denom
   452          uint64 mask = uint64(0xF) << shift;
   453          return (packed & ~mask) | ((uint64(sub) & 0xF) << shift);
   454      }
   455  
   456      /// @dev Unpack a winning subbucket from the packed uint64.
   457      /// @param packed Packed winning subbuckets.
   458      /// @param denom Denominator to unpack (2-12).
   459      /// @return Winning subbucket for this denom.
   460      function _unpackDecWinningSubbucket(
   461          uint64 packed,
   462          uint8 denom
   463      ) private pure returns (uint8) {
   464          if (denom < 2) return 0;
   465          uint8 shift = (denom - 2) << 2;
   466          return uint8((packed >> shift) & 0xF);
   467      }
   468  
   469      /// @dev Calculate pro-rata claimable amount for a player's DecEntry.
   470      /// @param poolWei Total pool available for claims.
   471      /// @param totalBurn Total qualifying burn (denominator for pro-rata).
   472      /// @param e Player's DecEntry storage reference.
   473      /// @param packedOffsets Packed winning subbuckets.
   474      /// @return amountWei Player's pro-rata share (0 if not winner).
   475      function _decClaimableFromEntry(
   476          uint256 poolWei,
   477          uint256 totalBurn,
   478          DecEntry storage e,
   479          uint64 packedOffsets
   480      ) private view returns (uint256 amountWei) {
   481          if (totalBurn == 0) return 0;
   482  
   483          uint8 denom = e.bucket;
   484          uint8 sub = e.subBucket;
   485          uint192 entryBurn = e.burn;
   486  
   487          // No participation or zero burn
   488          if (denom == 0 || entryBurn == 0) return 0;
   489  
   490          // Check if player's subbucket matches winning subbucket
   491          uint8 winningSub = _unpackDecWinningSubbucket(packedOffsets, denom);
   492          if (sub != winningSub) return 0;
   493  
   494          // Pro-rata share: (pool × playerBurn) / totalBurn
   495          amountWei = (poolWei * uint256(entryBurn)) / totalBurn;
   496      }
   497  
   498      /// @dev Internal view helper for decClaimable.
   499      /// @param round DecClaimRound storage reference.
   500      /// @param player Address to check.
   501      /// @param lvl Level number.
   502      /// @return amountWei Claimable amount.
   503      /// @return winner True if player is a winner.
   504      function _decClaimable(
   505          DecClaimRound storage round,
   506          address player,
   507          uint24 lvl
   508      ) internal view returns (uint256 amountWei, bool winner) {
   509          uint256 totalBurn = uint256(round.totalBurn);
   510          if (totalBurn == 0) return (0, false);
   511  
   512          DecEntry storage e = decBurn[lvl][player];
   513          if (e.claimed != 0) return (0, false);
   514  
   515          uint64 packedOffsets = decBucketOffsetPacked[lvl];
   516          amountWei = _decClaimableFromEntry(
   517              round.poolWei,
   518              totalBurn,
   519              e,
   520              packedOffsets
   521          );
   522          winner = amountWei != 0;
   523      }
   524  
   525      /// @dev Update aggregated burn totals for a subbucket.
   526      /// @param lvl Level number.
   527      /// @param denom Denominator (bucket).
   528      /// @param sub Subbucket index.
   529      /// @param delta Burn amount to add.
   530      function _decUpdateSubbucket(
   531          uint24 lvl,
   532          uint8 denom,
   533          uint8 sub,
   534          uint192 delta
   535      ) internal {
   536          if (delta == 0 || denom == 0) return;
   537          decBucketBurnTotal[lvl][denom][sub] += uint256(delta);
   538      }
   539  
   540      /// @dev Remove aggregated burn totals for a subbucket.
   541      /// @param lvl Level number.
   542      /// @param denom Denominator (bucket).
   543      /// @param sub Subbucket index.
   544      /// @param delta Burn amount to remove.
   545      function _decRemoveSubbucket(
   546          uint24 lvl,
   547          uint8 denom,
   548          uint8 sub,
   549          uint192 delta
   550      ) internal {
   551          if (delta == 0 || denom == 0) return;
   552          uint256 slotTotal = decBucketBurnTotal[lvl][denom][sub];
   553          if (slotTotal < uint256(delta)) revert E();
   554          decBucketBurnTotal[lvl][denom][sub] = slotTotal - uint256(delta);
   555      }
   556  
   557      /// @dev Deterministically assign subbucket for a player.
   558      ///      Hash of (player, lvl, bucket) ensures consistent assignment.
   559      /// @param player Address.
   560      /// @param lvl Level number.
   561      /// @param bucket Denominator.
   562      /// @return Subbucket index (0 to bucket-1).
   563      function _decSubbucketFor(
   564          address player,
   565          uint24 lvl,
   566          uint8 bucket
   567      ) private pure returns (uint8) {
   568          if (bucket == 0) return 0;
   569          return
   570              uint8(
   571                  uint256(keccak256(abi.encodePacked(player, lvl, bucket))) %
   572                      bucket
   573              );
   574      }
   575  
   576      /// @dev Awards decimator lootbox rewards to a claimer.
   577      /// @param winner Address to receive tickets.
   578      /// @param amount Lootbox portion of decimator claim in wei.
   579      /// @param rngWord VRF random word for lootbox resolution.
   580      function _awardDecimatorLootbox(
   581          address winner,
   582          uint256 amount,
   583          uint256 rngWord,
   584          uint16 evScore
   585      ) private {
   586          if (winner == address(0) || amount == 0) return;
   587          if (amount > LOOTBOX_CLAIM_THRESHOLD) {
   588              uint256 fullHalfPasses = amount / HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE;
   589              uint256 remainder = amount - (fullHalfPasses * HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE);
   590              if (fullHalfPasses != 0) {
   591                  uint24 startLevel = level + 1;
   592                  _applyWhalePassStats(winner, startLevel);
   593                  _queueTicketRange(winner, startLevel, 100, uint32(fullHalfPasses), false);
   594              }
   595              if (remainder != 0) {
   596                  _creditClaimable(winner, remainder);
   597              }
   598              return;
   599          }
   600          // Resolve lootbox via delegatecall to open module
   601          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
   602              .GAME_LOOTBOX_MODULE
   603              .delegatecall(
   604                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
   605                      IDegenerusGameLootboxModule.resolveLootboxDirect.selector,
   606                      winner,
   607                      amount,
   608                      rngWord,
   609                      evScore
   610                  )
   611              );
   612          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
   613      }
   614  
   615      /// @dev Inverse of BurnieCoin._adjustDecimatorBucket: the minimum activity score (bps)
   616      ///      that lands a burn in `bucket`. The decimator-claim lootbox EV multiplier reads
   617      ///      this frozen value (sealed when the winning burn was bucketed) rather than a live
   618      ///      score. Mirrors BurnieCoin's bucket scale: base 12, floor 5 (or 2 on x100 levels),
   619      ///      activity cap 23500.
   620      function _minScoreForBucket(uint8 bucket, uint24 lvl) private pure returns (uint16) {
   621          if (bucket >= 12) return 0; // base bucket = score ~0 -> 80% EV floor
   622          uint256 cap = 23_500;
   623          uint256 floorBucket = (lvl % 100 == 0) ? 2 : 5;
   624          uint256 reduction = 12 - uint256(bucket);
   625          uint256 range = 12 - floorBucket;
   626          uint256 numer = reduction * cap - cap / 2; // reduction >= 1 here, so no underflow
   627          uint256 s = (numer + range - 1) / range;   // ceil: min score that produces this bucket
   628          if (s > cap) s = cap;
   629          return uint16(s);
   630      }
   631  
   632      /*+======================================================================+
   633        |                    TERMINAL DECIMATOR (DEATH BET)                    |
   634        +======================================================================+
   635        |  Burn for GAMEOVER (blocked within 7 days of death clock).           |
   636        |  Time multiplier rewards early                                       |
   637        |  conviction. 200k cap equalizes bankroll — timing differentiates.   |
   638        +======================================================================+*/
   639  
   640      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   641      // Terminal Decimator Events
   642      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   643  
   644      event TerminalDecBurnRecorded(
   645          address indexed player,
   646          uint24 indexed lvl,
   647          uint8 bucket,
   648          uint8 subBucket,
   649          uint256 effectiveAmount,
   650          uint256 weightedAmount,
   651          uint256 timeMultBps
   652      );
   653  
   654      /// @notice Emitted when a player claims the terminal decimator jackpot.
   655      /// @param player The claimer.
   656      /// @param lvl Terminal decimator level.
   657      /// @param amountWei Payout credited as ETH claimable.
   658      event TerminalDecimatorClaimed(
   659          address indexed player,
   660          uint24 indexed lvl,
   661          uint256 amountWei
   662      );
   663  
   664      /// @notice Emitted when a final-day streak boost scales (and possibly promotes)
   665      ///         a player's terminal decimator entry.
   666      /// @param player The boosted player.
   667      /// @param lvl Terminal decimator level.
   668      /// @param oldBucket Bucket before the boost.
   669      /// @param newBucket Bucket after the boost (lower = better; equal if no promotion).
   670      /// @param newWeightedBurn The post-boost weighted burn (saturated at uint88 max).
   671      event TerminalDecBoosted(
   672          address indexed player,
   673          uint24 indexed lvl,
   674          uint8 oldBucket,
   675          uint8 newBucket,
   676          uint256 newWeightedBurn
   677      );
   678  
   679      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   680      // Terminal Decimator Errors
   681      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   682  
   683      error TerminalDecCapped();
   684      error TerminalDecNotActive();
   685      error TerminalDecNotWinner();
   686      error TerminalDecDeadlinePassed();
   687      error TerminalDecNotBoostable();
   688      error TerminalDecAlreadyBoosted();
