   690      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   691      // Terminal Decimator Constants
   692      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   693  
   694      uint32 private constant TERMINAL_DEC_IDLE_TIMEOUT_DAYS = 365;
   695      uint32 private constant TERMINAL_DEC_DEATH_CLOCK_DAYS = 120;
   696  
   697      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   698      // Terminal Decimator Burn Tracking
   699      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   700  
   701      /// @dev Bucket base and min for terminal decimator (lvl 100 rules).
   702      uint8 private constant TERMINAL_DEC_BUCKET_BASE = 12;
   703      uint8 private constant TERMINAL_DEC_MIN_BUCKET = 2;
   704      uint16 private constant TERMINAL_DEC_ACTIVITY_CAP_BPS = 23_500;
   705  
   706      /// @notice Record a terminal decimator burn for GAMEOVER eligibility.
   707      /// @dev Called by coin contract. Bucket and multiplier computed internally
   708      ///      from player activity score (lvl 100 rules, min bucket 2).
   709      ///      Time multiplier computed from days remaining on death clock.
   710      ///      Burns blocked when <= 7 days remain (7-day cooldown before termination).
   711      /// @param player Address of the player.
   712      /// @param lvl Current game level.
   713      /// @param baseAmount Burn amount before multiplier.
   714      function recordTerminalDecBurn(
   715          address player,
   716          uint24 lvl,
   717          uint256 baseAmount
   718      ) external {
   719          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.COIN) revert OnlyCoin();
   720  
   721          uint256 daysRemaining = _terminalDecDaysRemaining();
   722          if (daysRemaining <= 7) revert TerminalDecDeadlinePassed();
   723  
   724          // Compute bucket and multiplier from activity score (self-call; runs via delegatecall so address(this) == game)
   725          uint256 bonusBps = IDegenerusGame(address(this)).playerActivityScore(
   726              player
   727          );
   728          if (bonusBps > TERMINAL_DEC_ACTIVITY_CAP_BPS)
   729              bonusBps = TERMINAL_DEC_ACTIVITY_CAP_BPS;
   730          uint8 bucket = _terminalDecBucket(bonusBps);
   731          uint256 multBps = bonusBps == 0
   732              ? BPS_DENOMINATOR
   733              : BPS_DENOMINATOR + (bonusBps / 3);
   734  
   735          TerminalDecEntry storage e = terminalDecEntries[player];
   736  
   737          // Lazy reset: if entry is from a previous level, zero it out
   738          if (e.burnLevel != uint48(lvl)) {
   739              e.totalBurn = 0;
   740              e.weightedBurn = 0;
   741              e.bucket = 0;
   742              e.subBucket = 0;
   743              e.burnLevel = uint48(lvl);
   744              e.boosted = false; // boost is one-time PER LEVEL; clear with the rest
   745          }
   746  
   747          // First burn this level: set bucket and subbucket
   748          if (e.bucket == 0) {
   749              e.bucket = bucket;
   750              e.subBucket = _decSubbucketFor(player, lvl, bucket);
   751          }
   752  
   753          // Apply activity multiplier and cap
   754          uint256 effectiveAmount = _decEffectiveAmount(
   755              uint256(e.totalBurn),
   756              baseAmount,
   757              multBps
   758          );
   759          if (effectiveAmount == 0) revert TerminalDecCapped();
   760  
   761          // Update pre-time-multiplier total (for cap enforcement)
   762          uint256 newTotal = uint256(e.totalBurn) + effectiveAmount;
   763          if (newTotal > type(uint80).max) newTotal = type(uint80).max;
   764          e.totalBurn = uint80(newTotal);
   765  
   766          // Apply time multiplier
   767          uint256 timeMultBps = _terminalDecMultiplierBps(daysRemaining);
   768          uint256 weightedAmount = (effectiveAmount * timeMultBps) /
   769              BPS_DENOMINATOR;
   770  
   771          // Update post-time-multiplier total (for claim share)
   772          uint256 newWeighted = uint256(e.weightedBurn) + weightedAmount;
   773          if (newWeighted > type(uint88).max) newWeighted = type(uint88).max;
   774          e.weightedBurn = uint88(newWeighted);
   775  
   776          // Update bucket aggregate (key includes lvl, so old-level entries are naturally stale)
   777          bytes32 bucketKey = keccak256(abi.encode(lvl, e.bucket, e.subBucket));
   778          terminalDecBucketBurnTotal[bucketKey] += weightedAmount;
   779  
   780          emit TerminalDecBurnRecorded(
   781              player,
   782              lvl,
   783              e.bucket,
   784              e.subBucket,
   785              effectiveAmount,
   786              weightedAmount,
   787              timeMultBps
   788          );
   789      }
   790  
   791      /// @notice Final-day streak boost: scales an existing terminal decimator
   792      ///         entry by the player's effective quest streak and, if the live
   793      ///         activity score now qualifies a better (lower) bucket, promotes it.
   794      /// @dev Weight-only — the ETH/BURNIE payout path is untouched. Gated by
   795      ///      `!_livenessTriggered()` (the death-clock predicate is day-constant),
   796      ///      so the boost and any promotion provably commit BEFORE the game-over
   797      ///      resolution word exists: the placement is deterministic from the
   798      ///      committed burn and a view-read streak, never from draw knowledge.
   799      ///      Admissible only on the deadline day itself (daysRemaining == 0,
   800      ///      still pre-liveness) — forcing the streak to be kept alive to the end.
   801      ///      On promotion the subBucket is re-derived for the new denominator and
   802      ///      the aggregate is re-keyed (remove from old key, add to new) so total
   803      ///      weight in `terminalDecBucketBurnTotal` is conserved. One-time per
   804      ///      level via the `boosted` bit.
   805      function boostTerminalDecimator() external {
   806          if (_livenessTriggered()) revert TerminalDecNotActive();
   807          if (_terminalDecDaysRemaining() != 0) revert TerminalDecNotBoostable();
   808  
   809          address player = msg.sender;
   810          uint24 lvl = level;
   811  
   812          TerminalDecEntry storage e = terminalDecEntries[player];
   813          // Scale committed weight — never buy an entry. A stale (prior-level) or
   814          // empty entry has no weight to boost.
   815          if (e.burnLevel != uint48(lvl) || e.bucket == 0) {
   816              revert TerminalDecNotBoostable();
   817          }
   818          if (e.boosted) revert TerminalDecAlreadyBoosted();
   819  
   820          uint256 effectiveStreak = uint256(
   821              IDegenerusQuests(ContractAddresses.QUESTS)
   822                  .getPlayerQuestView(player)
   823                  .baseStreak
   824          );
   825          if (effectiveStreak == 0) revert TerminalDecNotBoostable();
   826  
   827          uint256 oldWeighted = uint256(e.weightedBurn);
   828          if (oldWeighted == 0) revert TerminalDecNotBoostable();
   829  
   830          // Scale weight by the streak factor, saturating at uint88 max.
   831          uint256 factorBps = _terminalDecBoostFactorBps(effectiveStreak);
   832          uint256 newWeighted = (oldWeighted * factorBps) / BPS_DENOMINATOR;
   833          if (newWeighted > type(uint88).max) newWeighted = type(uint88).max;
   834  
   835          uint8 oldBucket = e.bucket;
   836          uint8 oldSub = e.subBucket;
   837  
   838          // Recompute the bucket from the LIVE activity score (which now reflects
   839          // the kept-alive streak). Promote only if strictly better (lower).
   840          uint256 bonusBps = IDegenerusGame(address(this)).playerActivityScore(
   841              player
   842          );
   843          if (bonusBps > TERMINAL_DEC_ACTIVITY_CAP_BPS) {
   844              bonusBps = TERMINAL_DEC_ACTIVITY_CAP_BPS;
   845          }
   846          uint8 liveBucket = _terminalDecBucket(bonusBps);
   847  
   848          uint8 newBucket = oldBucket;
   849          uint8 newSub = oldSub;
   850          if (liveBucket < oldBucket) {
   851              newBucket = liveBucket;
   852              newSub = _decSubbucketFor(player, lvl, liveBucket);
   853              e.bucket = newBucket;
   854              e.subBucket = newSub;
   855          }
   856  
   857          e.weightedBurn = uint88(newWeighted);
   858          e.boosted = true;
   859  
   860          // Re-key the aggregate: remove the player's pre-boost weight from the old
   861          // key and add the post-boost weight to the (possibly new) key. Total
   862          // weight is conserved on a same-key boost (remove oldWeighted, add
   863          // newWeighted to the SAME key nets to +delta) and on a promotion.
   864          bytes32 oldKey = keccak256(abi.encode(lvl, oldBucket, oldSub));
   865          bytes32 newKey = keccak256(abi.encode(lvl, newBucket, newSub));
   866          terminalDecBucketBurnTotal[oldKey] -= oldWeighted;
   867          terminalDecBucketBurnTotal[newKey] += newWeighted;
   868  
   869          emit TerminalDecBoosted(player, lvl, oldBucket, newBucket, newWeighted);
   870      }
   871  
   872      /// @dev Streak → weight multiplier in bps (1x floor at streak 0, 4x at 10,
   873      ///      20x at 100, capped at 20x). The quest streak itself caps at 100.
   874      function _terminalDecBoostFactorBps(
   875          uint256 streak
   876      ) private pure returns (uint256) {
   877          if (streak > 100) streak = 100;
   878          uint256 factorBps;
   879          if (streak <= 10) {
   880              factorBps = BPS_DENOMINATOR + streak * 3000;
   881          } else {
   882              factorBps = 40000 + (streak - 10) * 1778;
   883          }
   884          if (factorBps > 200000) factorBps = 200000;
   885          return factorBps;
   886      }
   887  
   888      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   889      // Terminal Decimator Resolution (GAMEOVER only)
   890      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   891  
   892      /// @notice Resolve terminal decimator at GAMEOVER.
   893      /// @dev Selects winning subbuckets, snapshots claim round.
   894      ///      Returns poolWei if no qualifying burns.
   895      /// @param poolWei Total ETH allocated (10% of remaining).
   896      /// @param lvl Level at GAMEOVER.
   897      /// @param rngWord VRF-derived randomness.
   898      /// @return returnAmountWei Amount to return (non-zero if no winners).
   899      function runTerminalDecimatorJackpot(
   900          uint256 poolWei,
   901          uint24 lvl,
   902          uint256 rngWord
   903      ) external returns (uint256 returnAmountWei) {
   904          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.GAME) revert OnlyGame();
   905  
   906          // Prevent double-resolution
   907          if (lastTerminalDecClaimRound.lvl == lvl) {
   908              return poolWei;
   909          }
   910  
   911          uint256 totalWinnerBurn;
   912          uint64 packedOffsets;
   913  
   914          // Select winning subbucket for each denominator (2-12)
   915          uint256 decSeed = rngWord;
   916          for (uint8 denom = 2; denom <= DECIMATOR_MAX_DENOM; ) {
   917              uint8 winningSub = _decWinningSubbucket(decSeed, denom);
   918              packedOffsets = _packDecWinningSubbucket(
   919                  packedOffsets,
   920                  denom,
   921                  winningSub
   922              );
   923  
   924              bytes32 bucketKey = keccak256(abi.encode(lvl, denom, winningSub));
   925              uint256 subTotal = terminalDecBucketBurnTotal[bucketKey];
   926              if (subTotal != 0) {
   927                  totalWinnerBurn += subTotal;
   928              }
   929              unchecked {
   930                  ++denom;
   931              }
   932          }
   933  
   934          if (totalWinnerBurn == 0) {
   935              return poolWei;
   936          }
   937  
   938          // Store packed offsets for claim validation
   939          decBucketOffsetPacked[lvl] = packedOffsets;
   940  
   941          // Snapshot claim round (single slot — no rngWord needed for terminal claims)
   942          lastTerminalDecClaimRound.lvl = lvl;
   943          lastTerminalDecClaimRound.poolWei = uint96(poolWei);
   944          lastTerminalDecClaimRound.totalBurn = uint128(totalWinnerBurn);
   945  
   946          return 0;
   947      }
   948  
   949      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   950      // Terminal Decimator Claims
   951      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   952  
   953      /// @notice Claim terminal decimator jackpot for caller.
   954      /// @dev Only callable post-GAMEOVER. Level is read from the resolved claim round.
   955      function claimTerminalDecimatorJackpot() external {
   956          uint256 amountWei = _consumeTerminalDecClaim(msg.sender);
   957  
   958          _creditClaimable(msg.sender, amountWei);
   959          emit TerminalDecimatorClaimed(
   960              msg.sender,
   961              lastTerminalDecClaimRound.lvl,
   962              amountWei
   963          );
   964      }
   965  
   966      /// @notice Check if player can claim terminal decimator jackpot.
   967      /// @param player Address to check.
   968      /// @return amountWei Claimable amount.
   969      /// @return winner True if player won.
   970      function terminalDecClaimable(
   971          address player
   972      ) external view returns (uint256 amountWei, bool winner) {
   973          uint24 lvl = lastTerminalDecClaimRound.lvl;
   974          if (lvl == 0) return (0, false);
   975  
   976          TerminalDecEntry storage e = terminalDecEntries[player];
   977          if (
   978              e.burnLevel != uint48(lvl) || e.weightedBurn == 0 || e.bucket == 0
   979          ) {
   980              return (0, false);
   981          }
   982  
   983          uint64 packedOffsets = decBucketOffsetPacked[lvl];
   984          uint8 winningSub = _unpackDecWinningSubbucket(packedOffsets, e.bucket);
   985          if (e.subBucket != winningSub) return (0, false);
   986  
   987          uint256 totalBurn = uint256(lastTerminalDecClaimRound.totalBurn);
   988          if (totalBurn == 0) return (0, false);
   989  
   990          amountWei =
   991              (uint256(lastTerminalDecClaimRound.poolWei) *
   992                  uint256(e.weightedBurn)) /
   993              totalBurn;
   994          winner = amountWei != 0;
   995      }
   996  
   997      /// @dev Validate and consume terminal dec claim.
   998      function _consumeTerminalDecClaim(
   999          address player
  1000      ) private returns (uint256 amountWei) {
  1001          uint24 lvl = lastTerminalDecClaimRound.lvl;
  1002          if (lvl == 0) revert TerminalDecNotActive();
  1003  
  1004          TerminalDecEntry storage e = terminalDecEntries[player];
  1005          if (e.burnLevel != uint48(lvl) || e.weightedBurn == 0)
  1006              revert TerminalDecNotWinner();
  1007  
  1008          // Use totalBurn == 0 as claimed flag (set to 0 after claiming)
  1009          uint88 weight = e.weightedBurn;
  1010  
  1011          uint64 packedOffsets = decBucketOffsetPacked[lvl];
  1012          uint8 winningSub = _unpackDecWinningSubbucket(packedOffsets, e.bucket);
  1013          if (e.subBucket != winningSub) revert TerminalDecNotWinner();
  1014  
  1015          uint256 totalBurn = uint256(lastTerminalDecClaimRound.totalBurn);
  1016          if (totalBurn == 0) revert TerminalDecNotWinner();
  1017  
  1018          amountWei =
  1019              (uint256(lastTerminalDecClaimRound.poolWei) * uint256(weight)) /
  1020              totalBurn;
  1021          if (amountWei == 0) revert TerminalDecNotWinner();
  1022  
  1023          // Mark claimed by zeroing weightedBurn
  1024          e.weightedBurn = 0;
  1025      }
  1026  
  1027      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1028      // Terminal Decimator Helpers
  1029      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1030  
  1031      /// @dev Time multiplier based on days remaining on death clock.
  1032      ///      > 10 days: linear 20x (day 120) to 1x (day 10)
  1033      ///      7-10 days: flat 1x
  1034      ///      <= 7 days: blocked by caller
  1035      function _terminalDecMultiplierBps(
  1036          uint256 daysRemaining
  1037      ) private pure returns (uint256) {
  1038          if (daysRemaining <= 10) return 10000;
  1039          // Linear: 1x at day 10, 20x at day 120 → slope = 190000 / 110
  1040          return 10000 + ((daysRemaining - 10) * 190000) / 110;
  1041      }
  1042  
  1043      /// @dev Compute terminal decimator bucket from activity score (lvl 100 rules).
  1044      function _terminalDecBucket(uint256 bonusBps) private pure returns (uint8) {
  1045          if (bonusBps == 0) return TERMINAL_DEC_BUCKET_BASE;
  1046          uint256 range = uint256(TERMINAL_DEC_BUCKET_BASE) -
  1047              uint256(TERMINAL_DEC_MIN_BUCKET);
  1048          uint256 reduction = (range *
  1049              bonusBps +
  1050              (TERMINAL_DEC_ACTIVITY_CAP_BPS / 2)) /
  1051              TERMINAL_DEC_ACTIVITY_CAP_BPS;
  1052          uint256 b = uint256(TERMINAL_DEC_BUCKET_BASE) - reduction;
  1053          if (b < TERMINAL_DEC_MIN_BUCKET) b = TERMINAL_DEC_MIN_BUCKET;
  1054          return uint8(b);
  1055      }
  1056  
  1057      /// @dev Calculate days remaining on death clock using day-index arithmetic. Returns 0 if expired.
  1058      function _terminalDecDaysRemaining() private view returns (uint256) {
  1059          uint24 currentDay = _simulatedDayIndex();
  1060          uint24 psd = purchaseStartDay;
  1061          uint24 deadlineDay = psd +
  1062              uint24(
  1063                  level == 0
  1064                      ? TERMINAL_DEC_IDLE_TIMEOUT_DAYS
  1065                      : TERMINAL_DEC_DEATH_CLOCK_DAYS
  1066              );
  1067          if (currentDay >= deadlineDay) return 0;
  1068          return deadlineDay - currentDay;
  1069      }
  1070  }

   162      /**
   163       * @notice Purchase a 100-level whale bundle.
   164       * @dev Available at any level. Tickets always start at x1.
   165       *      - Boosts levelCount by delta between current freeze and new freeze (max 100, no double dipping).
   166       *      - Queues 40 × quantity bonus tickets/lvl for levels passLevel-10, 2 × quantity standard tickets/lvl for the rest.
   167       *      - Lootbox: 10% of price.
   168       *      - Distributes DGNRS rewards to buyer and affiliates.
   169       *
   170       *      Price: 2.4 ETH at levels 0-3, 4 ETH at levels 4+, 10/25/50% off standard with boon.
   171       *
   172       *      Fund distribution:
   173       *      - Pre-game (level 0): 30% next pool, 70% future pool
   174       *      - Post-game (level > 0): 5% next pool, 95% future pool
   175       * @param buyer The address receiving the bundle.
   176       * @param quantity Number of bundles to purchase (1-100).
   177       * @custom:reverts E When gameOver is true.
   178       * @custom:reverts E When quantity is 0 or exceeds 100.
   179       * @custom:reverts E When msg.value does not match required price.
   180       */
   181      function purchaseWhaleBundle(
   182          address buyer,
   183          uint256 quantity
   184      ) external payable {
   185          _purchaseWhaleBundle(buyer, quantity);
   186      }
   187  
   188      function _purchaseWhaleBundle(address buyer, uint256 quantity) private {
   189          if (_livenessTriggered()) revert E();
   190          uint24 passLevel = level + 1;
   191  
   192          if (quantity == 0 || quantity > 100) revert E();
   193  
   194          // Check for valid whale boon (10/25/50% off standard price)
   195          bool hasValidBoon = false;
   196          BoonPacked storage bp = boonPacked[buyer];
   197          uint256 s0 = bp.slot0;
   198          uint24 boonDay = uint24(s0 >> BP_WHALE_DAY_SHIFT);
   199          if (boonDay != 0) {
   200              uint24 currentDay = _simulatedDayIndex();
   201              hasValidBoon = currentDay <= boonDay + 4;
   202          }
   203  
   204          uint256 prevData = mintPacked_[buyer];
   205  
   206          // Unpack current values
   207          uint24 frozenUntilLevel = uint24(
   208              (prevData >> BitPackingLib.FROZEN_UNTIL_LEVEL_SHIFT) &
   209                  BitPackingLib.MASK_24
   210          );
   211          uint24 levelCount = uint24(
   212              (prevData >> BitPackingLib.LEVEL_COUNT_SHIFT) &
   213                  BitPackingLib.MASK_24
   214          );
   215  
   216          // Bundle covers 100 levels starting from current level
   217          uint24 ticketStartLevel = passLevel;
   218  
   219          // Calculate freeze extension and stat boost (delta-based, no double dipping)
   220          uint24 targetFrozenLevel = ticketStartLevel + 99;
   221          uint24 newFrozenLevel = frozenUntilLevel > targetFrozenLevel
   222              ? frozenUntilLevel
   223              : targetFrozenLevel;
   224          uint24 deltaFreeze = newFrozenLevel > frozenUntilLevel
   225              ? (newFrozenLevel - frozenUntilLevel)
   226              : 0;
   227          uint24 levelsToAdd = 100;
   228          if (levelsToAdd > deltaFreeze) {
   229              levelsToAdd = deltaFreeze;
   230          }
   231  
   232          // Price: boon discount applies to first bundle only,
   233          //        otherwise 2.4 ETH at levels 0-3, 4 ETH after
   234          uint256 totalPrice;
   235          if (hasValidBoon) {
   236              uint8 wTier = uint8(s0 >> BP_WHALE_TIER_SHIFT);
   237              uint16 discountBps = _whaleTierToBps(wTier);
   238              if (discountBps == 0) discountBps = 1000; // Default 10% for legacy boons
   239              uint256 discountedPrice = (WHALE_BUNDLE_STANDARD_PRICE *
   240                  (10_000 - discountBps)) / 10_000;
   241              // Clear whale fields (consumed)
   242              bp.slot0 = s0 & BP_WHALE_CLEAR;
   243              totalPrice =
   244                  discountedPrice +
   245                  WHALE_BUNDLE_STANDARD_PRICE *
   246                  (quantity - 1);
   247          } else {
   248              // x99 levels: minimum 2 bundles (8 ETH) to deter fresh-account century bonus farming
   249              if (passLevel % 100 == 0 && quantity < 2) revert E();
   250              uint256 unitPrice = passLevel <= 4
   251                  ? WHALE_BUNDLE_EARLY_PRICE
   252                  : WHALE_BUNDLE_STANDARD_PRICE;
   253              totalPrice = unitPrice * quantity;
   254          }
   255  
   256          // Claimable-pay: msg.value first, claimableWinnings covers the rest.
   257          if (msg.value > totalPrice) revert E();
   258          _settleClaimableShortfall(buyer, claimableWinnings[buyer], totalPrice - msg.value);
   259          // Coin-presale-box credit accrual: 25% of the committed ETH while presale open.
   260          if (!presaleOver) {
   261              presaleBoxCredit[buyer] += totalPrice / 4;
   262          }
   263  
   264          uint24 newLevelCount = levelCount + levelsToAdd;
   265  
   266          // Update mint data
   267          uint256 data = prevData;
   268          data = BitPackingLib.setPacked(
   269              data,
   270              BitPackingLib.LEVEL_COUNT_SHIFT,
   271              BitPackingLib.MASK_24,
   272              newLevelCount
   273          );
   274          data = BitPackingLib.setPacked(
   275              data,
   276              BitPackingLib.FROZEN_UNTIL_LEVEL_SHIFT,
   277              BitPackingLib.MASK_24,
   278              newFrozenLevel
   279          );
   280          data = BitPackingLib.setPacked(
   281              data,
   282              BitPackingLib.WHALE_BUNDLE_TYPE_SHIFT,
   283              3,
   284              3
   285          ); // 3 = 100-level bundle
   286          data = BitPackingLib.setPacked(
   287              data,
   288              BitPackingLib.LAST_LEVEL_SHIFT,
   289              BitPackingLib.MASK_24,
   290              newFrozenLevel
   291          );
   292  
   293          // Update mint day
   294          uint24 day = _currentMintDay();
   295          data = _setMintDay(
   296              data,
   297              day,
   298              BitPackingLib.DAY_SHIFT,
   299              BitPackingLib.MASK_32
   300          );
   301  
   302          mintPacked_[buyer] = data;
   303  
   304          // Queue tickets: 40*quantity/lvl for bonus levels (passLevel to 10), 2*quantity/lvl for the rest
   305          uint32 bonusTickets = uint32(WHALE_BONUS_TICKETS_PER_LEVEL * quantity);
   306          uint32 standardTickets = uint32(
   307              WHALE_STANDARD_TICKETS_PER_LEVEL * quantity
   308          );
   309          for (uint24 i = 0; i < 100; ) {
   310              uint24 lvl = ticketStartLevel + i;
   311              bool isBonus = (lvl >= passLevel && lvl <= WHALE_BONUS_END_LEVEL);
   312              _queueTickets(buyer, lvl, isBonus ? bonusTickets : standardTickets, false);
   313              unchecked {
   314                  ++i;
   315              }
   316          }
   317  
   318          address affiliateAddr = affiliate.getReferrer(buyer);
   319          address upline = address(0);
   320          address upline2 = address(0);
   321          if (affiliateAddr != address(0)) {
   322              upline = affiliate.getReferrer(affiliateAddr);
   323              if (upline != address(0)) {
   324                  upline2 = affiliate.getReferrer(upline);
   325              }
   326          }
   327  
   328          for (uint256 i = 0; i < quantity; ) {
   329              _rewardWhaleBundleDgnrs(buyer, affiliateAddr, upline, upline2);
   330              unchecked {
   331                  ++i;
   332              }
   333          }
   334  
   335          // Split payment: pre-game 70/30, post-game 95/5 (future/next)
   336          uint256 nextShare;
   337  
   338          if (level == 0) {
   339              nextShare = (totalPrice * 3000) / 10_000;
   340          } else {
   341              nextShare = (totalPrice * 500) / 10_000;
   342          }
   343  
   344          if (prizePoolFrozen) {
   345              (uint128 pNext, uint128 pFuture) = _getPendingPools();
   346              _setPendingPools(
   347                  pNext + uint128(nextShare),
   348                  pFuture + uint128(totalPrice - nextShare)
   349              );
   350          } else {
   351              (uint128 next, uint128 future) = _getPrizePools();
   352              _setPrizePools(
   353                  next + uint128(nextShare),
   354                  future + uint128(totalPrice - nextShare)
   355              );
   356          }
   357  
   358          // Lootbox: 10% of price
   359          uint256 lootboxAmount = (totalPrice * WHALE_LOOTBOX_BPS) / 10_000;
   360          _recordLootboxEntry(buyer, lootboxAmount, passLevel, data);
   361      }
   362  
   363      /**
   364       * @notice Purchase a 10-level lazy pass (direct in-game activation).
   365       * @dev Available at levels 0-2, x9 (9, 19, 29... excluding x99), or x0 (10, 20, 30...
   366       *      excluding the terminal x00), or with a valid lazy pass boon.
   367       *      Can renew when 7 or fewer levels remain on current pass freeze.
   368       *      - Grants 4 tickets per level for the next 10 levels (starting at current level + 1).
   369       *      - Applies the standard 10-level stat boost via _activate10LevelPass.
   370       *      - Price: flat 0.24 ETH at levels 0-2 (excess buys bonus tickets), sum of per-level
   371       *        ticket prices across the 10-level window at levels 3+.
   372       *      - Awards a lootbox equal to 10% of pass value.
   373       *      - Boon purchases apply a discount (default 10%) to the payment amount.
   374       * @param buyer The address receiving the pass.
   375       * @custom:reverts E When level is not 0-2, x9 (excl. x99), or x0 (excl. terminal x00) and no boon, pass has 8+ levels remaining, or msg.value is incorrect.
   376       */
   377      function purchaseLazyPass(address buyer) external payable {
   378          _purchaseLazyPass(buyer);
   379      }
   380  
   381      function _purchaseLazyPass(address buyer) private {
   382          if (_livenessTriggered()) revert E();
   383          uint24 currentLevel = level;
   384          bool hasValidBoon = false;
   385          BoonPacked storage bpLazy = boonPacked[buyer];
   386          uint256 s1 = bpLazy.slot1;
   387          uint8 lazyTier = uint8(s1 >> BP_LAZY_PASS_TIER_SHIFT);
   388          uint16 boonDiscountBps = _lazyPassTierToBps(lazyTier);
   389          uint24 boonDay = uint24(s1 >> BP_LAZY_PASS_DAY_SHIFT);
   390          if (boonDay != 0) {
   391              uint24 currentDay = _simulatedDayIndex();
   392              uint24 deityDay = uint24(s1 >> BP_DEITY_LAZY_PASS_DAY_SHIFT);
   393              if (deityDay != 0 && deityDay != currentDay) {
   394                  bpLazy.slot1 = s1 & BP_LAZY_PASS_CLEAR;
   395                  boonDay = 0;
   396                  boonDiscountBps = 0;
   397              } else if (currentDay <= boonDay + 4) {
   398                  hasValidBoon = true;
   399              } else {
   400                  bpLazy.slot1 = s1 & BP_LAZY_PASS_CLEAR;
   401                  boonDay = 0;
   402                  boonDiscountBps = 0;
   403              }
   404          } else if (lazyTier != 0) {
   405              // Stale tier with no day -- clear
   406              bpLazy.slot1 = s1 & BP_LAZY_PASS_CLEAR;
   407              boonDiscountBps = 0;
   408          }
   409          // Purchasable at levels 0-2, x9 (9,19,...; not x99), or x0 (10,20,...; not the
   410          // terminal x00 whose 10-level window would overrun level 100), or with a boon.
   411          if (
   412              currentLevel > 2 &&
   413              (currentLevel % 10 != 9 || currentLevel % 100 == 99) &&
   414              (currentLevel % 10 != 0 || currentLevel % 100 == 0) &&
   415              !hasValidBoon
   416          ) revert E();
   417  
   418          // Cap 1: disallow if player has deity pass or active frozen pass
   419          uint256 prevData = mintPacked_[buyer];
   420          if (
   421              prevData >> BitPackingLib.HAS_DEITY_PASS_SHIFT & 1 != 0
   422          ) revert E();
   423          uint24 frozenUntilLevel = uint24(
   424              (prevData >> BitPackingLib.FROZEN_UNTIL_LEVEL_SHIFT) &
   425                  BitPackingLib.MASK_24
   426          );
   427          // Allow if <7 levels remain on freeze (early renewal window)
   428          if (frozenUntilLevel > currentLevel + 7) revert E();
   429  
   430          uint24 startLevel = currentLevel == 0 ? 1 : currentLevel + 1;
   431          uint256 baseCost = _lazyPassCost(startLevel);
   432  
   433          // Levels 0-2: flat 0.24 ETH worth of benefits, balance → bonus tickets
   434          // Boon at 0-2: same benefits, discounted payment
   435          // Levels 3+: baseCost, boon applies discount to baseCost
   436          // benefitValue = undiscounted value used for presale-box credit/lootbox/pool splits
   437          uint256 totalPrice;
   438          uint256 benefitValue;
   439          uint32 bonusTickets;
   440          if (currentLevel <= 2) {
   441              benefitValue = 0.24 ether;
   442              uint256 balance = benefitValue - baseCost;
   443              if (balance != 0) {
   444                  uint256 ticketPrice = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(startLevel);
   445                  bonusTickets = uint32((balance * 4) / ticketPrice);
   446              }
   447              if (hasValidBoon) {
   448                  if (boonDiscountBps == 0) {
   449                      boonDiscountBps = LAZY_PASS_BOON_DEFAULT_DISCOUNT_BPS;
   450                  }
   451                  totalPrice =
   452                      (benefitValue * (10_000 - boonDiscountBps)) /
   453                      10_000;
   454              } else {
   455                  totalPrice = benefitValue;
   456              }
   457          } else {
   458              benefitValue = baseCost;
   459              if (hasValidBoon) {
   460                  if (boonDiscountBps == 0) {
   461                      boonDiscountBps = LAZY_PASS_BOON_DEFAULT_DISCOUNT_BPS;
   462                  }
   463                  totalPrice = (baseCost * (10_000 - boonDiscountBps)) / 10_000;
   464              } else {
   465                  totalPrice = baseCost;
   466              }
   467          }
   468          if (hasValidBoon) {
   469              // Re-read slot1 in case deity path already cleared, then clear lazy pass fields
   470              s1 = bpLazy.slot1;
   471              bpLazy.slot1 = s1 & BP_LAZY_PASS_CLEAR;
   472          }
   473          // Claimable-pay: msg.value first, claimableWinnings covers the rest.
   474          if (msg.value > totalPrice) revert E();
   475          _settleClaimableShortfall(buyer, claimableWinnings[buyer], totalPrice - msg.value);
   476          // Coin-presale-box credit accrual: 25% of the benefit value while presale open.
   477          if (!presaleOver) {
   478              presaleBoxCredit[buyer] += benefitValue / 4;
   479          }
   480  
   481          _activate10LevelPass(buyer, startLevel, LAZY_PASS_TICKETS_PER_LEVEL);
   482  
   483          // Queue bonus tickets from flat-price overpayment at early levels
   484          if (bonusTickets != 0) {
   485              _queueTickets(buyer, startLevel, bonusTickets, false);
   486          }
   487  
   488          // Split actual payment into pools (future + next)
   489          uint256 futureShare = (totalPrice * LAZY_PASS_TO_FUTURE_BPS) / 10_000;
   490          uint256 nextShare;
   491          unchecked {
   492              nextShare = totalPrice - futureShare;
   493          }
   494          if (prizePoolFrozen) {
   495              (uint128 pNext, uint128 pFuture) = _getPendingPools();
   496              _setPendingPools(
   497                  pNext + uint128(nextShare),
   498                  pFuture + uint128(futureShare)
   499              );
   500          } else {
   501              (uint128 next, uint128 future) = _getPrizePools();
   502              _setPrizePools(
   503                  next + uint128(nextShare),
   504                  future + uint128(futureShare)
   505              );
   506          }
   507  
   508          // Award lootbox as 10% of pass value
   509          uint256 lootboxAmount = (benefitValue * LAZY_PASS_LOOTBOX_BPS) / 10_000;
   510          _recordLootboxEntry(
   511              buyer,
   512              lootboxAmount,
   513              currentLevel + 1,
   514              mintPacked_[buyer]
   515          );
   516      }
   517  
   518      /**
   519       * @notice Purchase a deity pass for a specific symbol.
   520       * @dev Available before gameOver. One per player, up to 32 total (one per symbol).
   521       *      Buyer chooses from available symbols (0-31). Virtual trait-targeted jackpot
   522       *      entries are computed at resolution time — no explicit ticket queuing needed.
   523       *
   524       *      Price: 24 + T(n) ETH where n = passes sold so far, T(n) = n*(n+1)/2.
   525       *      First pass costs 24 ETH, last (32nd) costs 520 ETH.
   526       *
   527       *      Fund distribution:
   528       *      - Pre-game (level 0): 30% next pool, 70% future pool
   529       *      - Post-game (level > 0): 5% next pool, 95% future pool
   530       * @param buyer The address receiving the pass.
   531       * @param symbolId Symbol to claim (0-31: Q0 Crypto 0-7, Q1 Zodiac 8-15, Q2 Cards 16-23, Q3 Dice 24-31).
   532       * @custom:reverts E When buyer already owns a deity pass.
   533       * @custom:reverts E When symbolId is out of range or already taken.
   534       * @custom:reverts E When msg.value does not match current deity pass price.
   535       */
   536      function purchaseDeityPass(address buyer, uint8 symbolId) external payable {
   537          _purchaseDeityPass(buyer, symbolId);
   538      }
   539  
   540      function _purchaseDeityPass(address buyer, uint8 symbolId) private {
   541          if (rngLockedFlag) revert RngLocked();
   542          if (_livenessTriggered()) revert E();
   543          if (symbolId >= 32) revert E();
   544          if (deityBySymbol[symbolId] != address(0)) revert E();
   545          if (
   546              mintPacked_[buyer] >> BitPackingLib.HAS_DEITY_PASS_SHIFT & 1 != 0
   547          ) revert E();
   548  
   549          uint256 k = deityPassOwners.length;
   550          uint256 basePrice = DEITY_PASS_BASE + (k * (k + 1) * 1 ether) / 2;
   551  
   552          // Apply discount boon if active (tier 1=10%, 2=20%, 3=35%)
   553          uint256 totalPrice = basePrice;
   554          BoonPacked storage bpDeity = boonPacked[buyer];
   555          uint256 s1Deity = bpDeity.slot1;
   556          uint8 boonTier = uint8(s1Deity >> BP_DEITY_PASS_TIER_SHIFT);
   557          if (boonTier != 0) {
   558              // Check expiry: 4 days for lootbox-rolled, 1 day for deity-granted
   559              bool expired;
   560              uint24 deityDay = uint24(s1Deity >> BP_DEITY_DEITY_PASS_DAY_SHIFT);
   561              if (deityDay != 0) {
   562                  expired = uint24(_simulatedDayIndex()) > deityDay;
   563              } else {
   564                  uint24 stampDay = uint24(s1Deity >> BP_DEITY_PASS_DAY_SHIFT);
   565                  expired =
   566                      stampDay > 0 &&
   567                      uint24(_simulatedDayIndex()) >
   568                      stampDay + DEITY_PASS_BOON_EXPIRY_DAYS;
   569              }
   570              if (!expired) {
   571                  uint16 discountBps = boonTier == 3
   572                      ? uint16(3500)
   573                      : (boonTier == 2 ? uint16(2000) : uint16(1000));
   574                  totalPrice = (basePrice * (10_000 - discountBps)) / 10_000;
   575              }
   576              // Consume boon regardless of expiry — clear deity pass fields
   577              bpDeity.slot1 = s1Deity & BP_DEITY_PASS_CLEAR;
   578          }
   579          // Claimable-pay: msg.value first, claimableWinnings covers the rest.
   580          if (msg.value > totalPrice) revert E();
   581          _settleClaimableShortfall(buyer, claimableWinnings[buyer], totalPrice - msg.value);
   582  
   583          uint24 passLevel = level + 1;
   584  
   585          // Issue the pass with symbol
   586          deityPassPaidTotal[buyer] += totalPrice;
   587          // Coin-presale-box credit accrual: 25% of the committed ETH while presale open.
   588          if (!presaleOver) {
   589              presaleBoxCredit[buyer] += totalPrice / 4;
   590          }
   591  
   592          mintPacked_[buyer] = BitPackingLib.setPacked(
   593              mintPacked_[buyer],
   594              BitPackingLib.HAS_DEITY_PASS_SHIFT,
   595              1,
   596              1
   597          );
   598          deityPassPurchasedCount[buyer] += 1;
   599          deityPassOwners.push(buyer);
   600          deityPassSymbol[buyer] = symbolId;
   601          deityBySymbol[symbolId] = buyer;
   602  
   603          // Mint ERC721 token (tokenId = symbolId)
   604          IDegenerusDeityPassMint(ContractAddresses.DEITY_PASS).mint(
   605              buyer,
   606              symbolId
   607          );
   608  
   609          // DGNRS rewards
   610          address affiliateAddr = affiliate.getReferrer(buyer);
   611          address upline = address(0);
   612          address upline2 = address(0);
   613          if (affiliateAddr != address(0)) {
   614              upline = affiliate.getReferrer(affiliateAddr);
   615              if (upline != address(0)) {
   616                  upline2 = affiliate.getReferrer(upline);
   617              }
   618          }
   619          _rewardDeityPassDgnrs(buyer, affiliateAddr, upline, upline2);
   620  
   621          // Queue whale-equivalent tickets: 40/lvl bonus (1-10), 2/lvl standard (11-100)
   622          uint24 ticketStartLevel = passLevel <= 4
   623              ? 1
   624              : uint24(((passLevel + 1) / 50) * 50 + 1);
   625          for (uint24 i = 0; i < 100; ) {
   626              uint24 lvl = ticketStartLevel + i;
   627              bool isBonus = (lvl >= passLevel && lvl <= WHALE_BONUS_END_LEVEL);
   628              _queueTickets(
   629                  buyer,
   630                  lvl,
   631                  isBonus
   632                      ? WHALE_BONUS_TICKETS_PER_LEVEL
   633                      : WHALE_STANDARD_TICKETS_PER_LEVEL,
   634                  false
   635              );
   636              unchecked {
   637                  ++i;
   638              }
   639          }
   640  
   641          // Fund distribution: pre-game 70/30, post-game 95/5 (future/next)
   642          uint256 nextShare;
   643          if (level == 0) {
   644              nextShare = (totalPrice * 3000) / 10_000;
   645          } else {
   646              nextShare = (totalPrice * 500) / 10_000;
   647          }
   648          if (prizePoolFrozen) {
   649              (uint128 pNext, uint128 pFuture) = _getPendingPools();
   650              _setPendingPools(
   651                  pNext + uint128(nextShare),
   652                  pFuture + uint128(totalPrice - nextShare)
   653              );
   654          } else {
   655              (uint128 next, uint128 future) = _getPrizePools();
   656              _setPrizePools(
   657                  next + uint128(nextShare),
   658                  future + uint128(totalPrice - nextShare)
   659              );
   660          }
   661  
   662          // Lootbox: 10% of price
   663          uint256 lootboxAmount = (totalPrice * DEITY_LOOTBOX_BPS) / 10_000;
   664          _recordLootboxEntry(
   665              buyer,
   666              lootboxAmount,
   667              passLevel,
   668              mintPacked_[buyer]
   669          );
   670  
   671          emit DeityPassPurchased(buyer, symbolId, totalPrice, passLevel);
   672      }
   673  
   674      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   675      // Internal Helpers
   676      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   677  
   678      /// @dev Compute the total ETH cost of a 10-level lazy pass starting at startLevel.
   679      ///      Cost equals the sum of per-level ticket prices (4 tickets per level).
   680      function _lazyPassCost(
   681          uint24 startLevel
   682      ) private pure returns (uint256 total) {
   683          for (uint24 i = 0; i < LAZY_PASS_LEVELS; ) {
   684              total += PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(startLevel + i);
   685              unchecked {
   686                  ++i;
   687              }
   688          }
   689      }
   690  
   691      /// @dev Distribute DGNRS rewards for whale bundle purchase to buyer and affiliates.
   692      /// @param buyer The bundle purchaser receiving minter reward.
   693      /// @param affiliateAddr Direct referrer (receives 0.1% of affiliate pool).
   694      /// @param upline Second-level referrer (receives 0.02% of affiliate pool).
   695      /// @param upline2 Third-level referrer (receives 0.01% of affiliate pool).
   696      function _rewardWhaleBundleDgnrs(
   697          address buyer,
   698          address affiliateAddr,
   699          address upline,
   700          address upline2
   701      ) private {
   702          uint256 whaleReserve = dgnrs.poolBalance(
   703              IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Whale
   704          );
   705          if (whaleReserve != 0) {
   706              uint256 minterShare = (whaleReserve * DGNRS_WHALE_MINTER_PPM) /
   707                  DGNRS_WHALE_REWARD_PPM_SCALE;
   708              if (minterShare != 0) {
   709                  dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   710                      IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Whale,
   711                      buyer,
   712                      minterShare
   713                  );
   714              }
   715          }
   716  
   717          uint256 affiliateReserve = dgnrs.poolBalance(
   718              IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate
   719          );
   720          if (affiliateReserve == 0) return;
   721          // Reserve the outstanding level claim allocation so whale purchases
   722          // cannot drain tokens owed to affiliate claimants.
   723          uint256 reserved = levelDgnrsAllocation[level] -
   724              levelDgnrsClaimed[level];
   725          if (reserved >= affiliateReserve) return;
   726          affiliateReserve -= reserved;
   727  
   728          if (affiliateAddr != address(0)) {
   729              uint256 affiliateShare = (affiliateReserve *
   730                  DGNRS_AFFILIATE_DIRECT_WHALE_PPM) /
   731                  DGNRS_WHALE_REWARD_PPM_SCALE;
   732              if (affiliateShare != 0) {
   733                  dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   734                      IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate,
   735                      affiliateAddr,
   736                      affiliateShare
   737                  );
   738              }
   739          }
   740  
   741          uint256 uplineShare = (affiliateReserve *
   742              DGNRS_AFFILIATE_UPLINE_WHALE_PPM) / DGNRS_WHALE_REWARD_PPM_SCALE;
   743          if (upline != address(0) && uplineShare != 0) {
   744              dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   745                  IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate,
   746                  upline,
   747                  uplineShare
   748              );
   749          }
   750          uint256 upline2Share = uplineShare / 2;
   751          if (upline2 != address(0) && upline2Share != 0) {
   752              dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   753                  IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate,
   754                  upline2,
   755                  upline2Share
   756              );
   757          }
   758      }
   759  
   760      /// @dev Distribute DGNRS rewards for deity pass purchase to buyer and affiliates.
   761      /// @param buyer The pass purchaser receiving 5% of whale pool.
   762      /// @param affiliateAddr Direct referrer (receives 0.5% of affiliate pool).
   763      /// @param upline Second-level referrer (receives 0.1% of affiliate pool).
   764      /// @param upline2 Third-level referrer (receives 0.05% of affiliate pool).
   765      /// @return buyerDgnrs The amount of DGNRS transferred to the buyer.
   766      function _rewardDeityPassDgnrs(
   767          address buyer,
   768          address affiliateAddr,
   769          address upline,
   770          address upline2
   771      ) private returns (uint96 buyerDgnrs) {
   772          uint256 whaleReserve = dgnrs.poolBalance(
   773              IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Whale
   774          );
   775          if (whaleReserve != 0) {
   776              uint256 totalReward = (whaleReserve * DEITY_WHALE_POOL_BPS) /
   777                  10_000;
   778              if (totalReward != 0) {
   779                  uint256 paid = dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   780                      IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Whale,
   781                      buyer,
   782                      totalReward
   783                  );
   784                  if (paid != 0) {
   785                      buyerDgnrs = paid > type(uint96).max
   786                          ? type(uint96).max
   787                          : uint96(paid);
   788                  }
   789              }
   790          }
   791  
   792          uint256 affiliateReserve = dgnrs.poolBalance(
   793              IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate
   794          );
   795          if (affiliateReserve == 0) return buyerDgnrs;
   796          // Reserve the outstanding level claim allocation so deity purchases
   797          // cannot drain tokens owed to affiliate claimants.
   798          uint256 reserved = levelDgnrsAllocation[level] -
   799              levelDgnrsClaimed[level];
   800          if (reserved >= affiliateReserve) return buyerDgnrs;
   801          affiliateReserve -= reserved;
   802  
   803          if (affiliateAddr != address(0)) {
   804              uint256 affiliateShare = (affiliateReserve *
   805                  DGNRS_AFFILIATE_DIRECT_DEITY_PPM) /
   806                  DGNRS_WHALE_REWARD_PPM_SCALE;
   807              if (affiliateShare != 0) {
   808                  dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   809                      IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate,
   810                      affiliateAddr,
   811                      affiliateShare
   812                  );
   813              }
   814          }
   815  
   816          uint256 uplineShare = (affiliateReserve *
   817              DGNRS_AFFILIATE_UPLINE_DEITY_PPM) / DGNRS_WHALE_REWARD_PPM_SCALE;
   818          if (upline != address(0) && uplineShare != 0) {
   819              dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   820                  IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate,
   821                  upline,
   822                  uplineShare
   823              );
   824          }
   825          uint256 upline2Share = uplineShare / 2;
   826          if (upline2 != address(0) && upline2Share != 0) {
   827              dgnrs.transferFromPool(
   828                  IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Affiliate,
   829                  upline2,
   830                  upline2Share
   831              );
   832          }
   833          return buyerDgnrs;
   834      }
   835  
   836      function _recordLootboxEntry(
   837          address buyer,
   838          uint256 lootboxAmount,
   839          uint24 purchaseLevel,
   840          uint256 cachedPacked
   841      ) private {
   842          uint48 index = uint48(_lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK));
   843  
   844          _recordLootboxMintDay(buyer, cachedPacked);
   845  
   846          uint256 packed = lootboxEth[index][buyer];
   847          uint256 existingAmount = packed & ((1 << 232) - 1);
   848  
   849          if (existingAmount == 0) {
   850              // Purchase-time EV-cap tally (first deposit). The score is snapshotted
   851              // inline (DIV-2) and the multiplier frozen from it; the cap key is
   852              // level + 1 (== the resolver's currentLevel = level + 1), distinct from the
   853              // level + 2 baseLevel sentinel packed into the word (DIV-1). A bonus box
   854              // (mult > NEUTRAL) draws add = min(deposit, CAP - used) from the shared
   855              // per-(player, level) accumulator; sub-neutral/neutral boxes draw zero cap.
   856              uint256 score = IDegenerusGame(address(this)).playerActivityScore(buyer);
   857              uint64 adj;
   858              uint256 mult = _lootboxEvMultiplierFromScore(score);
   859              if (mult > LOOTBOX_EV_NEUTRAL_BPS) {
   860                  uint256 used = lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[buyer][level + 1];
   861                  uint256 remaining = used >= LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP
   862                      ? 0
   863                      : LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP - used;
   864                  uint256 add = lootboxAmount < remaining ? lootboxAmount : remaining;
   865                  lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[buyer][level + 1] = used + add;
   866                  adj = uint64(add);
   867              }
   868              lootboxPurchasePacked[index][buyer] = _packLootboxPurchase(
   869                  uint16(score + 1),
   870                  adj,
   871                  uint24(level + 2)
   872              );
   873          }
   874          // Subsequent deposits accumulate onto the existing box — no day-coherence gate and no stored
   875          // day (the box binds to lootboxRngWordByIndex[index] and rolls from the LIVE open level, so
   876          // cross-day deposits at an un-advanced index are harmless).
   877  
   878          uint256 boostedAmount = _applyLootboxBoostOnPurchase(buyer, lootboxAmount);
   879          uint256 existingBase = lootboxEthBase[index][buyer];
   880          if (existingAmount != 0 && existingBase == 0) {
   881              existingBase = existingAmount;
   882          }
   883          lootboxEthBase[index][buyer] = existingBase + lootboxAmount;
   884  
   885          uint256 newAmount = existingAmount + boostedAmount;
   886          lootboxEth[index][buyer] = (uint256(purchaseLevel) << 232) | newAmount;
   887          _lrWrite(LR_PENDING_ETH_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_ETH_MASK, _lrRead(LR_PENDING_ETH_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_ETH_MASK) + _packEthToMilliEth(lootboxAmount));
   888  
   889          // Purchase-time EV-cap tally (subsequent deposit). The multiplier is FROZEN
   890          // from the first-deposit score snapshot read back from the packed word; the cap
   891          // key is level + 1 (== the resolver's currentLevel). A bonus box accumulates
   892          // adjustedPortion via RMW; score+1 and baseLevel+1 are preserved.
   893          if (existingAmount != 0 && lootboxAmount != 0) {
   894              (
   895                  uint16 scorePlus1,
   896                  uint64 adj,
   897                  uint24 baseLevelPlus1
   898              ) = _unpackLootboxPurchase(lootboxPurchasePacked[index][buyer]);
   899              uint256 mult = _lootboxEvMultiplierFromScore(uint256(scorePlus1 - 1));
   900              if (mult > LOOTBOX_EV_NEUTRAL_BPS) {
   901                  uint256 used = lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[buyer][level + 1];
   902                  uint256 remaining = used >= LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP
   903                      ? 0
   904                      : LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP - used;
   905                  uint256 add = lootboxAmount < remaining ? lootboxAmount : remaining;
   906                  if (add != 0) {
   907                      lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[buyer][level + 1] = used + add;
   908                      lootboxPurchasePacked[index][buyer] = _packLootboxPurchase(
   909                          scorePlus1,
   910                          adj + uint64(add),
   911                          baseLevelPlus1
   912                      );
   913                  }
   914              }
   915          }
   916  
   917          // Track distress-mode portion for proportional ticket bonus at open time
   918          if (_isDistressMode()) {
   919              lootboxDistressEth[index][buyer] += boostedAmount;
   920          }
   921  
   922          // One box-buy event across paths (same topic as the mint module's LootBoxBuy), on every
   923          // deposit. presale=false — a pass-bundled box is never a presale box.
   924          emit LootBoxBuy(buyer, index, lootboxAmount, false);
   925      }
   926  
   927      /// @dev Apply any active lootbox boost boon to the purchase amount.
   928      ///      Reads packed lootbox tier from boonPacked[player].slot0. The purchase day is read
   929      ///      in-function (only on the boost path) for the expiry check.
   930      ///      Boost is capped at LOOTBOX_BOOST_MAX_VALUE (10 ETH) and expires after 2 game days.
   931      /// @param player The player whose boost to check and consume.
   932      /// @param amount The base lootbox amount before boost.
   933      /// @return boostedAmount The lootbox amount after applying any boost.
   934      function _applyLootboxBoostOnPurchase(
   935          address player,
   936          uint256 amount
   937      ) private returns (uint256 boostedAmount) {
   938          boostedAmount = amount;
   939          BoonPacked storage bp = boonPacked[player];
   940          uint256 s0 = bp.slot0;
   941          uint8 tier = uint8(s0 >> BP_LOOTBOX_TIER_SHIFT);
   942          if (tier == 0) return boostedAmount;
   943  
   944          // The purchase day (== the buy is happening now) — read here, only on the boost path.
   945          uint24 day = _simulatedDayIndex();
   946          // Check expiry
   947          uint24 stampDay = uint24(s0 >> BP_LOOTBOX_DAY_SHIFT);
   948          if (
   949              stampDay > 0 && day > stampDay + LOOTBOX_BOOST_EXPIRY_DAYS
   950          ) {
   951              // Expired: clear lootbox fields
   952              bp.slot0 = s0 & BP_LOOTBOX_CLEAR;
   953              return boostedAmount;
   954          }
   955  
   956          // Apply boost
   957          uint16 boostBps = _lootboxTierToBps(tier);
   958          uint256 cappedAmount = amount > LOOTBOX_BOOST_MAX_VALUE
   959              ? LOOTBOX_BOOST_MAX_VALUE
   960              : amount;
   961          uint256 boost = (cappedAmount * boostBps) / 10_000;
   962          boostedAmount += boost;
   963  
   964          // Clear lootbox fields (consumed)
   965          bp.slot0 = s0 & BP_LOOTBOX_CLEAR;
   966  
   967          emit LootBoxBoostConsumed(player, day, amount, boostedAmount, boostBps);
   968      }
   969  
   970      /// @dev Record the current day in player's packed data for lootbox activity tracking.
   971      /// @param player The player address.
   972      /// @param cachedPacked The caller's cached mintPacked_ value to avoid a redundant SLOAD.
   973      function _recordLootboxMintDay(
   974          address player,
   975          uint256 cachedPacked
   976      ) private {
   977          uint24 day = _simulatedDayIndex();
   978          uint24 prevDay = uint24(
   979              (cachedPacked >> BitPackingLib.DAY_SHIFT) & BitPackingLib.MASK_32
   980          );
   981          if (prevDay == day) {
   982              return;
   983          }
   984          uint256 clearedDay = cachedPacked &
   985              ~(BitPackingLib.MASK_32 << BitPackingLib.DAY_SHIFT);
   986          mintPacked_[player] =
   987              clearedDay |
   988              (uint256(day) << BitPackingLib.DAY_SHIFT);
   989      }
   990  
   991      // =========================================================================
   992      // Whale Pass Claims
   993      // =========================================================================
   994  
   995      /// @notice Claim deferred whale pass rewards for a player.
   996      /// @dev Awards deterministic tickets based on pre-calculated half-pass count.
   997      ///      Tickets start at current level + 1 to avoid giving tickets for an already-active level.
   998      /// @param player Player address to claim for.
   999      function claimWhalePass(address player) external {
  1000          if (_livenessTriggered()) revert E();
  1001          uint256 halfPasses = whalePassClaims[player];
  1002          if (halfPasses == 0) return;
  1003  
  1004          // Clear before awarding to avoid double-claiming
  1005          whalePassClaims[player] = 0;
  1006  
  1007          // Award tickets for 100 levels, with N tickets per level (where N = half-passes)
  1008          // Tickets start at level+1 to avoid giving tickets for an already-active level
  1009          // Example: 3 half-passes = 3 tickets/level x 100 levels = 300 tickets
  1010          // Safe: halfPasses fits in uint32 (ETH supply limits prevent overflow)
  1011          uint24 startLevel = level + 1;
  1012  
  1013          _applyWhalePassStats(player, startLevel);
  1014          emit WhalePassClaimed(player, msg.sender, halfPasses, startLevel);
  1015          _queueTicketRange(player, startLevel, 100, uint32(halfPasses), false);
  1016      }
  1017  }
  1018  
  1019  /// @dev Minimal interface for minting deity pass ERC721 tokens.
  1020  interface IDegenerusDeityPassMint {
  1021      /// @param to Recipient of the minted deity pass.
  1022      /// @param tokenId Token ID to mint (matches the deity symbol ID).
  1023      function mint(address to, uint256 tokenId) external;
  1024  }

    18  /**
    19   * @title DegenerusGameJackpotModule
    20   * @author Burnie Degenerus
    21   * @notice Delegate-called module that hosts the jackpot distribution logic for `DegenerusGame`.
    22   *
    23   * @dev ARCHITECTURE NOTES:
    24   *      - This contract is ONLY meant to be invoked via `delegatecall` from the main game contract.
    25   *      - Storage layout inherits from `DegenerusGameStorage` to ensure slot alignment with the parent.
    26   *      - All external functions lack access modifiers intentionally; the parent contract controls access.
    27   *      - DO NOT deploy this contract standalone or call it directly—state would be written to the
    28   *        module's own storage rather than the game's.
    29   *
    30   *      JACKPOT FLOW OVERVIEW:
    31   *      1. Pool consolidation at level transition (prize pool splits and merges).
    32   *      2. `payDailyJackpot` — Handles purchase phase jackpots and rolling dailies at EOL.
    33   *      3. `payDailyCoinJackpot` — BURNIE jackpot distribution to near-future ticket holders.
    34   *
    35   *      FUND ACCOUNTING:
    36   *      - ETH flows through `futurePrizePool` (unified reserve), `currentPrizePool`,
    37   *        `nextPrizePool`, `claimablePool`.
    38   *      - The remainder goes to the entropy-selected solo bucket.
    39   *      - `claimableWinnings` tracks per-player ETH; `claimablePool` is the aggregate liability.
    40   *
    41   *      RANDOMNESS:
    42   *      - All entropy originates from VRF words passed by the parent contract.
    43   *      - EntropyLib.hash2 provides full-diffusion keccak derivation for sub-selections.
    44   *      - Winner selection intentionally allows duplicates (more tickets = more chances).
    45   */
    46  contract DegenerusGameJackpotModule is DegenerusGamePayoutUtils {
    47      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    48      // Errors
    49      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    50  
    51      error OnlyGame();
    52  
    53      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    54      // Events
    55      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------

    57      /// @dev Emitted when a far-future ticket holder (5-99 levels ahead) wins the daily BURNIE jackpot.
    58      ///      These winners are drawn from ticketQueue (traits not yet assigned).
    59      event FarFutureCoinJackpotWinner(
    60          address indexed winner,
    61          uint24 indexed currentLevel,

    64      );

    66      /// @dev ETH jackpot win.

    69      event JackpotEthWin(
    70          address indexed winner,
    71          uint24 indexed level,
    72          uint16 indexed traitId,
    73          uint256 amount,
    74          uint256 ticketIndex
    75      );

    77      /// @dev Ticket jackpot win. See JackpotEthWin for traitId sentinel semantics.
    78      ///      ticketCount is a whole-ticket count on all 3 paths and matches the
    79      ///      quantity queued by the adjacent _queueTickets call. roundedUp is
    80      ///      true iff the BAF _jackpotTicketRoll (traitId = BAF_TRAIT_SENTINEL)
    81      ///      Bernoulli sub-roll incremented the whole-ticket count; it is false
    82      ///      on the two trait-matched paths, which have a zero fractional part
    83      ///      by construction.
    84      event JackpotTicketWin(
    85          address indexed winner,
    86          uint24 indexed ticketLevel,

   100          uint256 ticketIndex

   131      uint8 private constant JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP = 5;

   135      /// @dev Sentinel traitId stamped on BAF jackpot payout events so indexers can
   136      ///      distinguish BAF wins from trait-bucketed daily/coin wins. Sits above
   137      ///      uint8.max (255) so it never collides with a real trait id.
   138      uint16 private constant BAF_TRAIT_SENTINEL = 420;

   144      /// @dev Day-5 trait bucket shares packed into 64 bits: [6000, 1333, 1333, 1334] = 10000 bps.
   145      ///      With rotation, the 60% share is assigned to the solo (1-winner) bucket.
   146      uint64 private constant FINAL_DAY_SHARES_PACKED =
   147          (uint64(6000)) |
   148              (uint64(1333) << 16) |
   149              (uint64(1333) << 32) |
   150              (uint64(1334) << 48);

   153      ///      Remaining 20% is assigned to the entropy-selected solo bucket.
   154      uint64 private constant DAILY_JACKPOT_SHARES_PACKED =
   155          uint64(2000) * 0x0001000100010001;

   187      /// @dev Portion of purchase-phase reward-pool jackpots converted to loot boxes (3/4).

   190      /// @dev Max winners per single trait bucket (must fit in uint8 for _randTraitTicket).

   197

   200      uint16 private constant PURCHASE_PHASE_TICKET_MAX_WINNERS = 120;
   201  
   202      /// @dev Maximum total ETH winners across daily + carryover jackpots.
   203      ///      At max scale (6.36x, 200+ ETH pool): 159 + 95 + 50 + 1 = 305.

   205

   207      uint16 private constant DAILY_COIN_MAX_WINNERS = 50;

   209      /// @dev Share of daily BURNIE budget awarded to far-future ticket holders (25%).
   210      uint16 private constant FAR_FUTURE_COIN_BPS = 2500;
   211  
   212      /// @dev Number of far-future levels to sample for BURNIE jackpot (10 winners max).
   213      uint8 private constant FAR_FUTURE_COIN_SAMPLES = 10;
   214  
   215      /// @dev Domain separator for far-future coin jackpot entropy derivation.
   216      bytes32 private constant FAR_FUTURE_COIN_TAG = keccak256("far-future-coin");
   217  
   218      /// @dev Maximum winners for lootbox jackpot distributions (gas safety).
   219      ///      Lower than the daily ETH winner ceiling because lootboxes do multiple rolls per winner.
   220      uint16 private constant LOOTBOX_MAX_WINNERS = 100;
   221  
   222      /// @dev Daily jackpot max scale (6.36x) producing bucket counts 159/95/50/1 at 200+ ETH.
   223      ///      All 305 winners (159 + 95 + 50 + 1) are paid in a single call.
   224      uint32 private constant DAILY_JACKPOT_SCALE_MAX_BPS = 63_600;
   225  
   226      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   227      // Structs
   228      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
   229  
   230      /// @dev Mutable context passed through ETH distribution loops to track cumulative state.
   231      ///      Using a struct avoids stack-too-deep and makes the flow explicit.
   232      /// @dev Packed parameters for a single jackpot execution. Keeps external call surface lean
   233      ///      and avoids passing 6+ parameters through multiple internal functions.
   234      struct JackpotParams {
   235          uint24 lvl; // Current game level (1-indexed).
   236          uint256 ethPool; // ETH available for this jackpot.
   237          uint256 entropy; // VRF-derived entropy for winner selection.
   238          uint32 winningTraitsPacked; // 4 trait IDs packed into 32 bits (8 bits each).
   239          uint64 traitShareBpsPacked; // 4 share percentages packed (16 bits each).
   240      }
   241  
   242      // =========================================================================
   243      // External Entry Points (delegatecall targets)
   244      // =========================================================================
   245  
   246      /// @notice Terminal jackpot for x00 levels: Day-5-style bucket distribution.
   247      /// @dev Called via IDegenerusGame(address(this)) from GameOverModule.
   248      ///      Uses FINAL_DAY_SHARES_PACKED (60/13/13/13) with trait-based bucket distribution.
   249      ///      Updates claimablePool internally — callers must NOT double-count.
   250      /// @param poolWei Total ETH to distribute.
   251      /// @param targetLvl Level to sample winners from (typically lvl+1).
   252      /// @param rngWord VRF entropy seed.
   253      /// @return paidWei Total ETH distributed (callers deduct from source pool).
   254      function runTerminalJackpot(
   255          uint256 poolWei,
   256          uint24 targetLvl,
   257          uint256 rngWord
   258      ) external returns (uint256 paidWei) {
   259          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.GAME) revert OnlyGame();
   260  
   261          uint32 winningTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(rngWord, false);
   262          uint256 entropy = EntropyLib.hash2(rngWord, targetLvl);
   263          uint8[4] memory traitIds = JackpotBucketLib.unpackWinningTraits(
   264              winningTraitsPacked
   265          );
   266          uint8 soloQuadrant = _pickSoloQuadrant(traitIds, entropy);
   267          uint256 effectiveEntropy = (entropy & ~uint256(3)) | uint256((3 - soloQuadrant) & 3);
   268  
   269          uint16[4] memory bucketCounts = JackpotBucketLib.bucketCountsForPoolCap(
   270              poolWei,
   271              effectiveEntropy,
   272              DAILY_ETH_MAX_WINNERS,
   273              DAILY_JACKPOT_SCALE_MAX_BPS
   274          );
   275          uint16[4] memory shareBps = JackpotBucketLib.shareBpsByBucket(
   276              FINAL_DAY_SHARES_PACKED,
   277              uint8(effectiveEntropy & 3)
   278          );
   279  
   280          paidWei = _processDailyEth(
   281              targetLvl,
   282              poolWei,
   283              effectiveEntropy,
   284              traitIds,
   285              shareBps,
   286              bucketCounts,
   287              false // not jackpot phase
   288          );
   289      }
   290  
   291      /// @notice Pays purchase phase jackpots OR rolling daily jackpots at level end.
   292      /// @dev Called by the parent game contract via delegatecall. Two distinct paths:
   293      ///
   294      ///      JACKPOT PHASE PATH (isJackpotPhase=true):
   295      ///      - Day 1-4: Distributes a random 6%-14% slice of remaining currentPrizePool.
   296      ///      - Day 5: Distributes 100% of remaining currentPrizePool.
   297      ///      - Day 1 also runs the early-bird lootbox jackpot (from futurePrizePool).
   298      ///      - On day 2-4, takes 0.5% of futurePrizePool and buys current-level tickets
   299      ///        for winners from a random source level in [lvl+1, lvl+4], deposited into nextPool.
   300      ///      - Increments jackpotCounter on completion.
   301      ///
   302      ///      PURCHASE PHASE PATH (isJackpotPhase=false):
   303      ///      - Triggered during purchase phase when burns occur.
   304      ///      - Rolls winning traits (random + hero override) and runs trait-based jackpot.
   305      ///      - Fixed winner counts [20, 12, 6, 1] = 39 ETH winners, up to 120 ticket winners.
   306      ///      - At level 1+: adds a 1% futurePrizePool ETH slice every purchase day
   307      ///        with 75% converted to lootbox tickets and remainder distributed as ETH.
   308      ///      - Level 0: no ETH distribution (BURNIE/ticket rewards only).
   309      ///
   310      /// @param isJackpotPhase True for jackpot phase dailies, false for purchase phase jackpot.
   311      /// @param lvl Current game level.
   312      /// @param randWord VRF entropy for winner selection and trait derivation.
   313      function payDailyJackpot(
   314          bool isJackpotPhase,
   315          uint24 lvl,
   316          uint256 randWord
   317      ) external {
   318          uint24 questDay = _simulatedDayIndex();
   319          uint32 winningTraitsPacked;
   320  
   321          if (isJackpotPhase) {
   322              winningTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, false);
   323  
   324              uint256 dailyEthBudget;
   325              {
   326                  uint8 counter = jackpotCounter;
   327                  uint8 counterStep = 1;
   328                  // Turbo (flag=2): all 5 logical days in 1 physical day.
   329                  // Compressed (flag=1): 5 logical days in 3 physical days.
   330                  if (compressedJackpotFlag == 2 && counter == 0) {
   331                      counterStep = JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP;
   332                  } else if (
   333                      compressedJackpotFlag == 1 &&
   334                      counter > 0 &&
   335                      counter < JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP - 1
   336                  ) {
   337                      counterStep = 2;
   338                  }
   339                  bool isFinalPhysicalDay = (counter + counterStep >=
   340                      JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP);
   341                  bool isEarlyBirdDay = (counter == 0);
   342                  uint256 poolSnapshot = _getCurrentPrizePool();
   343                  uint16 dailyBps;
   344                  if (isFinalPhysicalDay) {
   345                      dailyBps = 10_000; // Final physical day: 100% of remaining pool
   346                  } else {
   347                      dailyBps = _dailyCurrentPoolBps(counter, randWord);
   348                      // Double BPS on compressed days to combine two days' payouts.
   349                      if (counterStep == 2) {
   350                          dailyBps *= 2;
   351                      }
   352                  }
   353                  uint256 budget = (poolSnapshot * dailyBps) / 10_000;
   354  
   355                  // Run the early-bird lootbox jackpot on day 1 only.
   356                  // This day replaces the normal daily carryover flow.
   357                  if (isEarlyBirdDay) {
   358                      _runEarlyBirdLootboxJackpot(lvl + 1, randWord);
   359                  }
   360  
   361                  // Gas optimization: 20% = 1/5 (cheaper than * 2000 / 10000)
   362                  uint256 dailyLootboxBudget = budget / 5;
   363                  if (dailyLootboxBudget != 0) {
   364                      budget -= dailyLootboxBudget;
   365                  }
   366  
   367                  // Calculate daily ticket units (distributed in Phase 2 via payDailyJackpotCoinAndTickets)
   368                  uint256 dailyTicketUnits = _budgetToTicketUnits(
   369                      dailyLootboxBudget,
   370                      lvl + 1
   371                  );
   372                  if (dailyTicketUnits != 0) {
   373                      // Deduct from current pool and add to next pool to back tickets
   374                      _setCurrentPrizePool(
   375                          _getCurrentPrizePool() - dailyLootboxBudget
   376                      );
   377                      _setNextPrizePool(_getNextPrizePool() + dailyLootboxBudget);
   378                  }
   379  
   380                  uint8 sourceLevelOffset;
   381                  uint24 sourceLevel;
   382                  uint256 reserveSlice;
   383                  uint256 carryoverTicketUnits;
   384                  if (!isEarlyBirdDay) {
   385                      sourceLevelOffset = uint8(
   386                          (uint256(
   387                              keccak256(
   388                                  abi.encodePacked(
   389                                      randWord,
   390                                      DAILY_CARRYOVER_SOURCE_TAG,
   391                                      counter
   392                                  )
   393                              )
   394                          ) % DAILY_CARRYOVER_MAX_OFFSET) + 1
   395                      );
   396                      sourceLevel = lvl + uint24(sourceLevelOffset);
   397  
   398                      // 0.5% of futurePrizePool reserved for carryover tickets
   399                      uint256 futurePoolBal = _getFuturePrizePool();
   400                      reserveSlice = futurePoolBal / 200;
   401                      _setFuturePrizePool(futurePoolBal - reserveSlice);
   402                      _setNextPrizePool(_getNextPrizePool() + reserveSlice);
   403                      carryoverTicketUnits = _budgetToTicketUnits(
   404                          reserveSlice,
   405                          lvl
   406                      );
   407                  }
   408  
   409                  // Store ticket units for Phase 2 distribution
   410                  // Packing: [counterStep (8 bits)] [dailyTicketUnits (64 bits @ 8)]
   411                  // [carryoverTicketUnits (64 bits @ 72)] [carryoverSourceOffset (8 bits @ 136)]
   412                  dailyTicketBudgetsPacked = _packDailyTicketBudgets(
   413                      counterStep,
   414                      dailyTicketUnits,
   415                      carryoverTicketUnits,
   416                      sourceLevelOffset
   417                  );
   418  
   419                  dailyEthBudget = budget;
   420              }
   421  
   422              uint256 entropyDaily = EntropyLib.hash2(randWord, lvl);
   423              uint8[4] memory traitIdsDaily = JackpotBucketLib
   424                  .unpackWinningTraits(winningTraitsPacked);
   425              uint8 soloQuadrantDaily = _pickSoloQuadrant(traitIdsDaily, entropyDaily);
   426              uint256 effectiveEntropyDaily = (entropyDaily & ~uint256(3)) | uint256((3 - soloQuadrantDaily) & 3);
   427              (uint8 counterStep_, , , ) = _unpackDailyTicketBudgets(
   428                  dailyTicketBudgetsPacked
   429              );
   430              bool isFinalPhysicalDay_ = (jackpotCounter + counterStep_ >=
   431                  JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP);
   432  
   433              if (dailyEthBudget != 0) {
   434                  uint16[4] memory bucketCountsDaily = JackpotBucketLib
   435                      .bucketCountsForPoolCap(
   436                          dailyEthBudget,
   437                          effectiveEntropyDaily,
   438                          DAILY_ETH_MAX_WINNERS,
   439                          DAILY_JACKPOT_SCALE_MAX_BPS
   440                      );
   441  
   442                  // Final physical day uses weighted shares (60/13/13/13) for the big payout;
   443                  // other days use equal shares (20/20/20/20).
   444                  uint64 sharesPacked = isFinalPhysicalDay_
   445                      ? FINAL_DAY_SHARES_PACKED
   446                      : DAILY_JACKPOT_SHARES_PACKED;
   447                  uint16[4] memory shareBpsDaily = JackpotBucketLib
   448                      .shareBpsByBucket(sharesPacked, uint8(effectiveEntropyDaily & 3));
   449  
   450                  uint256 paidDailyEth = _processDailyEth(
   451                      lvl,
   452                      dailyEthBudget,
   453                      effectiveEntropyDaily,
   454                      traitIdsDaily,
   455                      shareBpsDaily,
