   456                      bucketCountsDaily,
   457                      true // jackpot phase (solo bucket gets whale pass)
   458                  );
   459                  if (isFinalPhysicalDay_) {
   460                      uint256 unpaidDailyEth = dailyEthBudget - paidDailyEth;
   461                      _setCurrentPrizePool(
   462                          _getCurrentPrizePool() - dailyEthBudget
   463                      );
   464                      if (unpaidDailyEth != 0) {
   465                          _setFuturePrizePool(
   466                              _getFuturePrizePool() + unpaidDailyEth
   467                          );
   468                      }
   469                  } else {
   470                      _setCurrentPrizePool(_getCurrentPrizePool() - paidDailyEth);
   471                  }
   472              }
   473  
   474              {
   475                  uint32 bonusTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, true);
   476                  uint256 coinEntropy = uint256(keccak256(abi.encode(randWord, lvl, COIN_JACKPOT_TAG)));
   477                  uint24 bonusTargetLevel = lvl + 1 + uint24(coinEntropy % 4);
   478                  emit DailyWinningTraits(questDay, winningTraitsPacked, bonusTraitsPacked, bonusTargetLevel);
   479              }
   480  
   481              dailyJackpotCoinTicketsPending = true;
   482              return;
   483          }
   484  
   485          // Purchase phase path - BURNIE and ETH bonuses at level 1+
   486          winningTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, false);
   487          uint8[4] memory traitIds = JackpotBucketLib.unpackWinningTraits(winningTraitsPacked);
   488          uint256 entropy = EntropyLib.hash2(randWord, lvl);
   489          uint8 soloQuadrant = _pickSoloQuadrant(traitIds, entropy);
   490          uint256 effectiveEntropy = (entropy & ~uint256(3)) | uint256((3 - soloQuadrant) & 3);
   491  
   492          {
   493              uint32 bonusTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, true);
   494              uint256 coinEntropy = uint256(keccak256(abi.encode(randWord, lvl, COIN_JACKPOT_TAG)));
   495              uint24 bonusTargetLevel = lvl + 1 + uint24(coinEntropy % 4);
   496              emit DailyWinningTraits(questDay, winningTraitsPacked, bonusTraitsPacked, bonusTargetLevel);
   497          }
   498  
   499          bool isEthDay = lvl > 0; // daily 1% drip from futurePrizePool every purchase day
   500          uint256 ethDaySlice;
   501          if (isEthDay) {
   502              uint256 poolBps = 100; // 1% daily drip from futurePool
   503              ethDaySlice = (_getFuturePrizePool() * poolBps) / 10_000;
   504          }
   505  
   506          uint256 ethPool = ethDaySlice;
   507          uint256 lootboxBudget;
   508          if (ethPool != 0) {
   509              lootboxBudget = (ethPool * PURCHASE_REWARD_JACKPOT_LOOTBOX_BPS) / 10_000;
   510              if (lootboxBudget != 0) ethPool -= lootboxBudget;
   511          }
   512          uint256 paidEth = _executeJackpot(
   513              JackpotParams({
   514                  lvl: lvl,
   515                  ethPool: ethPool,
   516                  entropy: effectiveEntropy,
   517                  winningTraitsPacked: winningTraitsPacked,
   518                  traitShareBpsPacked: DAILY_JACKPOT_SHARES_PACKED
   519              })
   520          );
   521  
   522          // Deferred deduction: deduct only what was actually consumed
   523          if (ethDaySlice != 0) {
   524              _setFuturePrizePool(
   525                  _getFuturePrizePool() - lootboxBudget - paidEth
   526              );
   527          }
   528  
   529          if (lootboxBudget != 0) {
   530              _distributeLootboxAndTickets(
   531                  lvl,
   532                  winningTraitsPacked,
   533                  lootboxBudget,
   534                  randWord,
   535                  5_000 // 50% ticket conversion — improves pool/ticket backing ratio
   536              );
   537          }
   538      }
   539  
   540      /// @notice Phase 2 of daily jackpot: distributes coin jackpot AND tickets to trait winners.
   541      /// @dev Called by advanceGame when dailyJackpotCoinTicketsPending is true.
   542      ///      Gas optimization: Separating coin+ticket distribution from ETH distribution
   543      ///      keeps each advanceGame call under the 15M gas block limit.
   544      ///
   545      ///      Traits are derived inline from randWord (main via isBonus=false, bonus via isBonus=true).
   546      ///      Uses stored values from Phase 1:
   547      ///      - rngWordCurrent: VRF entropy for deterministic winner selection
   548      ///      - dailyTicketBudgetsPacked: Packed ticket units, counter step, and carryover source offset
   549      ///
   550      /// @param randWord VRF entropy (must match rngWordCurrent from Phase 1).
   551      function payDailyJackpotCoinAndTickets(uint256 randWord) external {
   552          if (!dailyJackpotCoinTicketsPending) return;
   553  
   554          // Unpack stored values
   555          (
   556              uint8 counterStep,
   557              uint256 dailyTicketUnits,
   558              uint256 carryoverTicketUnits,
   559              uint8 carryoverSourceOffset
   560          ) = _unpackDailyTicketBudgets(dailyTicketBudgetsPacked);
   561  
   562          // Derive traits inline from randWord (DJT storage removed)
   563          uint24 lvl = level;
   564          uint32 mainTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, false);
   565          uint32 bonusTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, true);
   566          uint256 entropyDaily = EntropyLib.hash2(randWord, lvl);
   567          uint24 sourceLevel = lvl + uint24(carryoverSourceOffset);
   568          uint256 entropyNext = EntropyLib.hash2(randWord, sourceLevel);
   569  
   570          // --- Coin Jackpot ---
   571          uint256 coinBudget = _calcDailyCoinBudget(lvl);
   572          if (coinBudget != 0) {
   573              // Split: 25% far-future, 75% near-future
   574              uint256 farBudget = (coinBudget * FAR_FUTURE_COIN_BPS) / 10_000;
   575              _awardFarFutureCoinJackpot(lvl, farBudget, randWord);
   576  
   577              uint256 nearBudget = coinBudget - farBudget;
   578              if (nearBudget != 0) {
   579                  _awardDailyCoinToTraitWinners(
   580                      lvl + 1,
   581                      lvl + 4,
   582                      bonusTraitsPacked,
   583                      nearBudget,
   584                      randWord
   585                  );
   586              }
   587          }
   588  
   589          // --- Ticket Distribution ---
   590          // Distribute daily tickets to current level trait winners (main traits)
   591          if (dailyTicketUnits != 0) {
   592              _distributeTicketJackpot(
   593                  lvl,
   594                  lvl + 1,
   595                  mainTraitsPacked,
   596                  dailyTicketUnits,
   597                  entropyDaily,
   598                  LOOTBOX_MAX_WINNERS,
   599                  241
   600              );
   601          }
   602  
   603          // Distribute carryover tickets: winners from source level, tickets at current level
   604          // (or lvl+1 on final day since current level is about to end). Uses bonus traits.
   605          if (carryoverTicketUnits != 0) {
   606              bool isFinalDay = jackpotCounter + counterStep >= JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP;
   607              _distributeTicketJackpot(
   608                  sourceLevel,
   609                  isFinalDay ? lvl + 1 : lvl,
   610                  bonusTraitsPacked,
   611                  carryoverTicketUnits,
   612                  entropyNext,
   613                  LOOTBOX_MAX_WINNERS,
   614                  240
   615              );
   616          }
   617  
   618          // Complete the daily jackpot cycle
   619          unchecked {
   620              jackpotCounter += counterStep;
   621          }
   622  
   623          // Clear pending state
   624          dailyJackpotCoinTicketsPending = false;
   625          dailyTicketBudgetsPacked = 0;
   626      }
   627  
   628      /// @dev Execute the early-bird lootbox jackpot from the unified future pool.
   629      ///      100 winners (25 per bonus trait from the same 4-trait roll used by the
   630      ///      coin jackpot). All tickets queued at `lvl` (= outer level + 1).
   631      function _runEarlyBirdLootboxJackpot(uint24 lvl, uint256 rngWord) private {
   632          uint256 futurePoolLocal = _getFuturePrizePool();
   633          uint256 totalBudget = (futurePoolLocal * 300) / 10_000; // 3%
   634          if (totalBudget == 0) return;
   635          _setFuturePrizePool(futurePoolLocal - totalBudget);
   636  
   637          uint256 ticketPrice = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(lvl);
   638          uint32 ticketCount = ticketPrice != 0
   639              ? uint32((totalBudget / 100) / ticketPrice)
   640              : 0;
   641  
   642          if (ticketCount != 0) {
   643              uint8[4] memory bonusTraits = JackpotBucketLib.unpackWinningTraits(
   644                  _rollWinningTraits(rngWord, true)
   645              );
   646              address[][256] storage bucket = traitBurnTicket[lvl];
   647  
   648              for (uint8 t; t < 4; ) {
   649                  uint8 traitId = bonusTraits[t];
   650                  (
   651                      address[] memory winners,
   652                      uint256[] memory ticketIndexes
   653                  ) = _randTraitTicket(bucket, rngWord, traitId, 25, t);
   654                  uint256 len = winners.length;
   655                  for (uint256 i; i < len; ) {
   656                      address winner = winners[i];
   657                      if (winner != address(0)) {
   658                          _queueTickets(winner, lvl, ticketCount, true);
   659                          // ticketCount carries the whole ticket count awarded.
   660                          emit JackpotTicketWin(
   661                              winner,
   662                              lvl,
   663                              traitId,
   664                              ticketCount,
   665                              lvl,
   666                              ticketIndexes[i],
   667                              false
   668                          );
   669                      }
   670                      unchecked {
   671                          ++i;
   672                      }
   673                  }
   674                  unchecked {
   675                      ++t;
   676                  }
   677              }
   678          }
   679  
   680          _setNextPrizePool(_getNextPrizePool() + totalBudget);
   681      }
   682  
   683      /// @notice Distribute yield surplus (stETH appreciation) to stakeholders.
   684      /// @dev Entry point for AdvanceModule delegatecall. The selector-dispatched
   685      ///      signature carries the day's VRF word for delegatecall-shape stability;
   686      ///      the surplus split is deterministic and consumes no entropy.
   687      ///      23% each to sDGNRS, vault, and charity (GNRUS) claimable, 23% yield accumulator (~8% buffer).
   688      function distributeYieldSurplus(uint256) external {
   689          uint256 stBal = steth.balanceOf(address(this));
   690          uint256 totalBal = address(this).balance + stBal;
   691          uint256 obligations = _getCurrentPrizePool() +
   692              _getNextPrizePool() +
   693              claimablePool +
   694              _getFuturePrizePool() +
   695              yieldAccumulator;
   696  
   697          // Pending buffer is a live liability backed by ETH already in balance:
   698          // freeze-window revenue lands in balance but routes to prizePoolPendingPacked
   699          // (outside the live pools above) until _unfreezePool folds it back. Without
   700          // this, that ETH is misread as yield surplus and over-distributed.
   701          // Reads 0 when not frozen.
   702          (uint128 pNext, uint128 pFuture) = _getPendingPools();
   703          obligations += uint256(pNext) + uint256(pFuture);
   704  
   705          if (totalBal <= obligations) return;
   706  
   707          uint256 yieldPool = totalBal - obligations;
   708          uint256 quarterShare = (yieldPool * 2300) / 10_000;
   709  
   710          if (quarterShare != 0) {
   711              uint256 d0 = _addClaimableEth(ContractAddresses.VAULT, quarterShare);
   712              uint256 d1 = _addClaimableEth(ContractAddresses.SDGNRS, quarterShare);
   713              uint256 d2 = _addClaimableEth(ContractAddresses.GNRUS, quarterShare);
   714              uint256 claimableDelta = d0 + d1 + d2;
   715              if (claimableDelta != 0) claimablePool += uint128(claimableDelta);
   716              yieldAccumulator += quarterShare;
   717          }
   718      }
   719  
   720      // =========================================================================
   721      // Internal Helpers — Claimable ETH
   722      // =========================================================================
   723  
   724      /// @dev Credits ETH to a player's claimable balance. Uses unchecked arithmetic because
   725      ///      uint256 overflow is practically impossible with real ETH amounts.
   726      ///      ETH winnings always credit to claimable.
   727      /// @param beneficiary Address to credit.
   728      /// @param weiAmount Wei to add to their claimable balance.
   729      /// @return claimableDelta Amount to add to claimablePool for this credit.
   730      function _addClaimableEth(
   731          address beneficiary,
   732          uint256 weiAmount
   733      ) private returns (uint256 claimableDelta) {
   734          if (weiAmount == 0) return 0;
   735  
   736          // SAFETY: uint256 max is ~10^77 wei; overflow impossible in practice.
   737          _creditClaimable(beneficiary, weiAmount);
   738          return weiAmount;
   739      }
   740  
   741      /// @dev Converts an ETH budget to ticket units. Tickets cost ticketPrice/4.
   742      function _budgetToTicketUnits(
   743          uint256 budget,
   744          uint24 lvl
   745      ) private pure returns (uint256) {
   746          if (budget == 0) return 0;
   747          uint256 ticketPrice = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(lvl);
   748          return ticketPrice == 0 ? 0 : (budget << 2) / ticketPrice;
   749      }
   750  
   751      // =========================================================================
   752      // Internal Helpers — Ticket Rewards
   753      // =========================================================================
   754  
   755      /// @dev Distributes lootbox budget to next pool and tickets to trait winners.
   756      /// @param ticketConversionBps Fraction of budget used for ticket calculation (10000 = 100%).
   757      ///        Full budget always flows to nextPrizePool regardless of this parameter.
   758      function _distributeLootboxAndTickets(
   759          uint24 lvl,
   760          uint32 winningTraitsPacked,
   761          uint256 lootboxBudget,
   762          uint256 randWord,
   763          uint16 ticketConversionBps
   764      ) private {
   765          // Add lootbox budget to nextPrizePool
   766          _setNextPrizePool(_getNextPrizePool() + lootboxBudget);
   767  
   768          // Distribute tickets to winners (may use reduced basis for backing ratio)
   769          uint256 ticketBasis = (lootboxBudget * ticketConversionBps) / 10_000;
   770          uint256 ticketUnits = _budgetToTicketUnits(ticketBasis, lvl + 1);
   771          if (ticketUnits != 0) {
   772              _distributeTicketJackpot(
   773                  lvl,
   774                  lvl + 1,
   775                  winningTraitsPacked,
   776                  ticketUnits,
   777                  EntropyLib.hash2(randWord, lvl),
   778                  PURCHASE_PHASE_TICKET_MAX_WINNERS,
   779                  242
   780              );
   781          }
   782      }
   783  
   784      /// @dev Distributes ticket rewards to winners drawn from winning trait pools.
   785      function _distributeTicketJackpot(
   786          uint24 sourceLvl,
   787          uint24 queueLvl,
   788          uint32 winningTraitsPacked,
   789          uint256 ticketUnits,
   790          uint256 entropy,
   791          uint16 maxWinners,
   792          uint8 saltBase
   793      ) private {
   794          if (ticketUnits == 0) return;
   795  
   796          uint8[4] memory traitIds = JackpotBucketLib.unpackWinningTraits(
   797              winningTraitsPacked
   798          );
   799          uint16 cap = maxWinners;
   800          if (ticketUnits < cap) cap = uint16(ticketUnits);
   801  
   802          (uint16[4] memory counts, uint8 activeCount) = _computeBucketCounts(
   803              sourceLvl,
   804              traitIds,
   805              cap,
   806              entropy
   807          );
   808          if (activeCount == 0) return;
   809  
   810          _distributeTicketsToBuckets(
   811              sourceLvl,
   812              queueLvl,
   813              traitIds,
   814              counts,
   815              ticketUnits,
   816              entropy,
   817              cap,
   818              saltBase
   819          );
   820      }
   821  
   822      /// @dev Distributes tickets across all buckets.
   823      function _distributeTicketsToBuckets(
   824          uint24 sourceLvl,
   825          uint24 queueLvl,
   826          uint8[4] memory traitIds,
   827          uint16[4] memory counts,
   828          uint256 ticketUnits,
   829          uint256 entropy,
   830          uint16 cap,
   831          uint8 saltBase
   832      ) private {
   833          uint256 baseUnits = ticketUnits / cap;
   834          uint256 distParams = (ticketUnits % cap) | ((entropy % cap) << 128);
   835          uint256 globalIdx;
   836  
   837          for (uint8 traitIdx; traitIdx < 4; ) {
   838              if (counts[traitIdx] != 0) {
   839                  entropy = uint256(
   840                      keccak256(abi.encode(entropy, traitIdx, ticketUnits))
   841                  );
   842                  globalIdx = _distributeTicketsToBucket(
   843                      sourceLvl,
   844                      queueLvl,
   845                      traitIds[traitIdx],
   846                      counts[traitIdx],
   847                      entropy,
   848                      uint8(saltBase + traitIdx),
   849                      baseUnits,
   850                      distParams,
   851                      cap,
   852                      globalIdx
   853                  );
   854              }
   855              unchecked {
   856                  ++traitIdx;
   857              }
   858          }
   859      }
   860  
   861      /// @dev Distributes tickets to winners in a single bucket.
   862      function _distributeTicketsToBucket(
   863          uint24 sourceLvl,
   864          uint24 queueLvl,
   865          uint8 traitId,
   866          uint16 count,
   867          uint256 entropy,
   868          uint8 salt,
   869          uint256 baseUnits,
   870          uint256 distParams,
   871          uint16 cap,
   872          uint256 startIdx
   873      ) private returns (uint256 endIdx) {
   874          (
   875              address[] memory winners,
   876              uint256[] memory ticketIndexes
   877          ) = _randTraitTicket(
   878                  traitBurnTicket[sourceLvl],
   879                  entropy,
   880                  traitId,
   881                  uint8(count),
   882                  salt
   883              );
   884  
   885          uint256 extra = distParams & type(uint128).max;
   886          uint256 offset = distParams >> 128;
   887          uint256 len = winners.length;
   888          uint256 cursor = (startIdx + offset) % cap;
   889          for (uint256 i; i < len; ) {
   890              address winner = winners[i];
   891              uint256 units = baseUnits;
   892              if (extra != 0 && cursor < extra) {
   893                  units += 1;
   894              }
   895              if (winner != address(0) && units != 0) {
   896                  _queueTickets(winner, queueLvl, uint32(units), true);
   897                  // ticketCount carries the whole ticket count awarded.
   898                  emit JackpotTicketWin(
   899                      winner,
   900                      queueLvl,
   901                      traitId,
   902                      uint32(units),
   903                      sourceLvl,
   904                      ticketIndexes[i],
   905                      false
   906                  );
   907              }
   908              unchecked {
   909                  ++cursor;
   910                  if (cursor == cap) cursor = 0;
   911                  ++startIdx;
   912                  ++i;
   913              }
   914          }
   915          return startIdx;
   916      }
   917  
   918      /// @dev Computes bucket winner counts for active trait buckets (including virtual deity entries).
   919      function _computeBucketCounts(
   920          uint24 lvl,
   921          uint8[4] memory traitIds,
   922          uint16 maxWinners,
   923          uint256 entropy
   924      ) private view returns (uint16[4] memory counts, uint8 activeCount) {
   925          uint8 activeMask;
   926          for (uint8 i; i < 4; ) {
   927              uint8 trait = traitIds[i];
   928              bool hasEntries = traitBurnTicket[lvl][trait].length != 0;
   929              if (!hasEntries) {
   930                  uint8 fullSymId = (trait >> 6) * 8 + (trait & 0x07);
   931                  hasEntries =
   932                      fullSymId < 32 &&
   933                      deityBySymbol[fullSymId] != address(0);
   934              }
   935              if (hasEntries) {
   936                  activeMask |= uint8(1 << i);
   937                  unchecked {
   938                      ++activeCount;
   939                  }
   940              }
   941              unchecked {
   942                  ++i;
   943              }
   944          }
   945          if (activeCount == 0) return (counts, 0);
   946  
   947          uint16 baseCount = maxWinners / activeCount;
   948          uint16 remainder = maxWinners - baseCount * activeCount;
   949  
   950          for (uint8 i; i < 4; ) {
   951              if ((activeMask & uint8(1 << i)) != 0) {
   952                  counts[i] = baseCount;
   953              }
   954              unchecked {
   955                  ++i;
   956              }
   957          }
   958  
   959          if (remainder != 0) {
   960              uint8 idx = uint8(entropy & 3);
   961              while (remainder != 0) {
   962                  if ((activeMask & uint8(1 << idx)) != 0) {
   963                      counts[idx] += 1;
   964                      unchecked {
   965                          --remainder;
   966                      }
   967                  }
   968                  idx = uint8((idx + 1) & 3);
   969              }
   970          }
   971      }
   972  
   973      // =========================================================================
   974      // Internal Helpers — Jackpot Execution
   975      // =========================================================================
   976  
   977      /// @dev Picks the solo bucket quadrant for ETH-distribution rotation.
   978      ///      When any winning trait has color==7 (gold tier), returns a uniformly-random
   979      ///      gold quadrant via bits 4+ of `entropy` (disjoint from the bucket-rotation
   980      ///      low 2 bits at `entropy & 3`). Otherwise returns the existing rotation index
   981      ///      `uint8((3 - (entropy & 3)) & 3)` matching `JackpotBucketLib.soloBucketIndex`.
   982      /// @param traits The 4 winning trait IDs (each [QQ][CCC][SSS] packed: quadrant 2 bits,
   983      ///        color 3 bits, symbol 3 bits).
   984      /// @param entropy VRF-derived entropy. Bits 0-1 drive bucket rotation; bits 4+ drive
   985      ///        gold tie-break (bits 2-3 unused by either path).
   986      /// @return Quadrant index 0-3 to receive the solo bucket assignment.
   987      function _pickSoloQuadrant(uint8[4] memory traits, uint256 entropy) internal pure returns (uint8) {
   988          // Pack gold quadrant indices into a uint256 (4 slots × 8 bits each).
   989          // Each slot holds a quadrant index 0-3. Pure-stack representation —
   990          // no memory allocation per call.
   991          uint256 goldQuads;
   992          uint8 goldCount;
   993          for (uint8 i; i < 4; ++i) {
   994              if (((traits[i] >> 3) & 7) == 7) {
   995                  goldQuads |= uint256(i) << (goldCount * 8);
   996                  unchecked { ++goldCount; }
   997              }
   998          }
   999          if (goldCount == 0) {
  1000              return uint8((3 - (entropy & 3)) & 3);
  1001          }
  1002          uint8 idx = uint8((entropy >> 4) % goldCount);
  1003          return uint8((goldQuads >> (idx * 8)) & 0xFF);
  1004      }
  1005  
  1006      /// @dev Core jackpot execution: distributes ETH to winners.
  1007      ///      This is the unified entry point for daily and purchase phase jackpots.
  1008      ///      COIN jackpots are handled separately by _executeCoinJackpot.
  1009      ///      Pool debits are handled by the caller.
  1010      ///
  1011      /// @param jp Packed jackpot parameters.
  1012      /// @return paidEth Total ETH paid out (for pool accounting).
  1013      function _executeJackpot(
  1014          JackpotParams memory jp
  1015      ) private returns (uint256 paidEth) {
  1016          uint8[4] memory traitIds = JackpotBucketLib.unpackWinningTraits(
  1017              jp.winningTraitsPacked
  1018          );
  1019          uint16[4] memory shareBps = JackpotBucketLib.shareBpsByBucket(
  1020              jp.traitShareBpsPacked,
  1021              uint8(jp.entropy & 3)
  1022          );
  1023  
  1024          if (jp.ethPool != 0) {
  1025              paidEth = _runJackpotEthFlow(jp, traitIds, shareBps);
  1026          }
  1027      }
  1028  
  1029      /// @dev ETH flow for purchase phase jackpots (via _executeJackpot).
  1030      ///      Fixed bucket counts [20, 12, 6, 1] = 39 winners, rotated by entropy.
  1031      function _runJackpotEthFlow(
  1032          JackpotParams memory jp,
  1033          uint8[4] memory traitIds,
  1034          uint16[4] memory shareBps
  1035      ) private returns (uint256 totalPaidEth) {
  1036          uint8 offset = uint8(jp.entropy & 3);
  1037          uint16[4] memory base;
  1038          base[0] = 20;
  1039          base[1] = 12;
  1040          base[2] = 6;
  1041          base[3] = 1;
  1042          uint16[4] memory bucketCounts;
  1043          for (uint8 i; i < 4; ) {
  1044              bucketCounts[i] = base[(i + offset) & 3];
  1045              unchecked { ++i; }
  1046          }
  1047          return
  1048              _processDailyEth(
  1049                  jp.lvl,
  1050                  jp.ethPool,
  1051                  jp.entropy,
  1052                  traitIds,
  1053                  shareBps,
  1054                  bucketCounts,
  1055                  false // not jackpot phase
  1056              );
  1057      }
  1058  
  1059      // =========================================================================
  1060      // Daily Jackpot ETH — Distribution
  1061      // =========================================================================
  1062  
  1063      /// @dev Unified ETH distribution across trait buckets. All buckets are paid
  1064      ///      in a single call (the full DAILY_ETH_MAX_WINNERS ceiling).
  1065      ///
  1066      ///      JACKPOT PHASE vs PURCHASE/TERMINAL:
  1067      ///      - Jackpot phase (isJackpotPhase=true): Solo bucket gets whale pass + DGNRS on final day.
  1068      ///      - Purchase/terminal (isJackpotPhase=false): All buckets paid uniformly.
  1069      ///
  1070      /// @param lvl The level whose winners are being paid.
  1071      /// @param ethPool Total ETH to distribute.
  1072      /// @param entropy VRF-derived random word for winner selection.
  1073      /// @param traitIds The 4 winning trait IDs.
  1074      /// @param shareBps Basis-point share for each of the 4 buckets.
  1075      /// @param bucketCounts Number of holders in each trait bucket.
  1076      /// @param isJackpotPhase True during jackpot phase (solo bucket gets whale pass).
  1077      /// @return paidEth Total ETH actually paid out in this call.
  1078      function _processDailyEth(
  1079          uint24 lvl,
  1080          uint256 ethPool,
  1081          uint256 entropy,
  1082          uint8[4] memory traitIds,
  1083          uint16[4] memory shareBps,
  1084          uint16[4] memory bucketCounts,
  1085          bool isJackpotPhase
  1086      ) private returns (uint256 paidEth) {
  1087          if (ethPool == 0) {
  1088              return 0;
  1089          }
  1090  
  1091          uint256 unit = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(lvl + 1) >> 2;
  1092          uint8 remainderIdx = JackpotBucketLib.soloBucketIndex(entropy);
  1093          uint256[4] memory shares = JackpotBucketLib.bucketShares(
  1094              ethPool, shareBps, bucketCounts, remainderIdx, unit
  1095          );
  1096  
  1097          uint8[4] memory order = JackpotBucketLib.bucketOrderLargestFirst(
  1098              bucketCounts
  1099          );
  1100  
  1101          uint256 entropyState = entropy;
  1102          uint256 liabilityDelta;
  1103  
  1104          for (uint8 j; j < 4; ++j) {
  1105              uint8 traitIdx = order[j];
  1106  
  1107              uint16 count = bucketCounts[traitIdx];
  1108              uint256 share = shares[traitIdx];
  1109              if (count == 0 || share == 0) continue;
  1110  
  1111              entropyState = uint256(
  1112                  keccak256(abi.encode(entropyState, traitIdx, share))
  1113              );
  1114  
  1115              uint256 paidDelta;
  1116              uint256 claimDelta;
  1117              (paidDelta, claimDelta, entropyState) = _processBucket(
  1118                  lvl,
  1119                  traitIds[traitIdx],
  1120                  traitIdx,
  1121                  count,
  1122                  share,
  1123                  entropyState,
  1124                  isJackpotPhase && traitIdx == remainderIdx
  1125              );
  1126              paidEth += paidDelta;
  1127              liabilityDelta += claimDelta;
  1128          }
  1129  
  1130          if (liabilityDelta != 0) {
  1131              claimablePool += uint128(liabilityDelta);
  1132          }
  1133      }
  1134  
  1135      /// @dev Resolves and pays one trait bucket. Selects up to MAX_BUCKET_WINNERS
  1136      ///      ticket holders for the bucket and credits each winner. The solo path
  1137      ///      (isSolo, jackpot phase only) routes the single winner through the
  1138      ///      whale-pass + final-day DGNRS handler; every other bucket pays 100% ETH.
  1139      /// @return paidDelta ETH value paid out for this bucket.
  1140      /// @return claimDelta Claimable-liability added for this bucket.
  1141      /// @return newEntropy Updated entropy after winner selection.
  1142      function _processBucket(
  1143          uint24 lvl,
  1144          uint8 traitId,
  1145          uint8 traitIdx,
  1146          uint16 count,
  1147          uint256 share,
  1148          uint256 entropy,
  1149          bool isSolo
  1150      ) private returns (uint256 paidDelta, uint256 claimDelta, uint256 newEntropy) {
  1151          newEntropy = entropy;
  1152  
  1153          uint16 totalCount = count;
  1154          if (totalCount > MAX_BUCKET_WINNERS) totalCount = MAX_BUCKET_WINNERS;
  1155  
  1156          (
  1157              address[] memory winners,
  1158              uint256[] memory ticketIndexes
  1159          ) = _randTraitTicket(
  1160                  traitBurnTicket[lvl],
  1161                  newEntropy,
  1162                  traitId,
  1163                  uint8(totalCount),
  1164                  uint8(200 + traitIdx)
  1165              );
  1166          if (winners.length == 0) return (0, 0, newEntropy);
  1167  
  1168          uint256 perWinner = share / totalCount;
  1169          if (perWinner == 0) return (0, 0, newEntropy);
  1170  
  1171          if (isSolo) {
  1172              // Solo bucket (jackpot phase): whale pass + DGNRS on final day
  1173              address w = winners[0];
  1174              if (w != address(0)) {
  1175                  (claimDelta, paidDelta, newEntropy) = _handleSoloBucketWinner(
  1176                      w, lvl, traitId, ticketIndexes[0],
  1177                      perWinner, newEntropy
  1178                  );
  1179              }
  1180          } else {
  1181              // Normal bucket: 100% ETH
  1182              (paidDelta, claimDelta) = _payNormalBucket(
  1183                  winners, ticketIndexes, perWinner, lvl, traitId
  1184              );
  1185          }
  1186      }
  1187  
  1188      // =========================================================================
  1189      // Internal Helpers — Winner Resolution
  1190      // =========================================================================
  1191  
  1192      /// @dev Resolves winners for a single trait bucket and distributes ETH.
  1193      ///
  1194      ///      FLOW:
  1195      ///      1. Early exit if no share or no winners.
  1196      ///      2. Select random ticket holders from the trait's burn ticket pool.
  1197      ///      3. Credit ETH payouts to claimableWinnings (with optional loot box conversion).
  1198      ///
  1199      /// @param lvl Current level for ticket pool lookup.
  1200      /// @param traitId Which trait's ticket pool to draw from.
  1201      /// @param traitIdx Bucket index (0-3) for entropy derivation.
  1202      /// @param traitShare Total ETH allocated to this bucket.
  1203      /// @param entropy Current entropy state.
  1204      /// @param winnerCount Number of winners to select.
  1205      /// @return entropyState Updated entropy after selection.
  1206      /// @return ethDelta ETH credited to claimable balances.
  1207      /// @return liabilityDelta Total claimable liability added.
  1208      /// @return ticketSpent Whale pass ETH routed to futurePrizePool.
  1209      function _resolveTraitWinners(
  1210          uint24 lvl,
  1211          uint8 traitId,
  1212          uint8 traitIdx,
  1213          uint256 traitShare,
  1214          uint256 entropy,
  1215          uint16 winnerCount
  1216      )
  1217          private
  1218          returns (
  1219              uint256 entropyState,
  1220              uint256 ethDelta,
  1221              uint256 liabilityDelta,
  1222              uint256 ticketSpent
  1223          )
  1224      {
  1225          entropyState = entropy;
  1226  
  1227          // Early exits for edge cases.
  1228          if (traitShare == 0) return (entropyState, 0, 0, 0);
  1229  
  1230          uint16 totalCount = winnerCount;
  1231          if (totalCount == 0) return (entropyState, 0, 0, 0);
  1232  
  1233          // Cap to MAX_BUCKET_WINNERS to fit in uint8 and bound gas.
  1234          if (totalCount > MAX_BUCKET_WINNERS) totalCount = MAX_BUCKET_WINNERS;
  1235  
  1236          // Derive sub-entropy and select winners from the trait's ticket pool.
  1237          entropyState = uint256(
  1238              keccak256(abi.encode(entropyState, traitIdx, traitShare))
  1239          );
  1240          (
  1241              address[] memory winners,
  1242              uint256[] memory ticketIndexes
  1243          ) = _randTraitTicket(
  1244                  traitBurnTicket[lvl],
  1245                  entropyState,
  1246                  traitId,
  1247                  uint8(totalCount),
  1248                  uint8(200 + traitIdx) // Salt to differentiate trait buckets
  1249              );
  1250          if (winners.length == 0) return (entropyState, 0, 0, 0);
  1251  
  1252          uint256 perWinner = traitShare / totalCount;
  1253          if (perWinner == 0) return (entropyState, 0, 0, 0);
  1254  
  1255          uint256 len = winners.length;
  1256  
  1257          uint256 totalPayout;
  1258          uint256 totalLiability;
  1259          for (uint256 i; i < len; ) {
  1260              address w = winners[i];
  1261              if (w != address(0)) {
  1262                  uint256 claimableDelta = _addClaimableEth(w, perWinner);
  1263                  emit JackpotEthWin(
  1264                      w,
  1265                      lvl,
  1266                      traitId,
  1267                      perWinner,
  1268                      ticketIndexes[i]
  1269                  );
  1270                  totalPayout += perWinner;
  1271                  totalLiability += claimableDelta;
  1272              }
  1273              unchecked {
  1274                  ++i;
  1275              }
  1276          }
  1277          if (totalPayout == 0) return (entropyState, 0, 0, 0);
  1278  
  1279          liabilityDelta = totalLiability;
  1280          ethDelta = totalPayout;
  1281  
  1282          return (entropyState, ethDelta, liabilityDelta, 0);
  1283      }
  1284  
  1285      // =========================================================================
  1286      // Internal Helpers — Quest & Credit
  1287      // =========================================================================
  1288  
  1289      /// @dev Thin wrapper called from _processDailyEth to avoid stack-too-deep.
  1290      ///      Calls _processSoloBucketWinner, emits specialized events, and returns
  1291      ///      only the three values the outer loop needs.
  1292      function _handleSoloBucketWinner(
  1293          address w,
  1294          uint24 lvl,
  1295          uint8 traitId,
  1296          uint256 ticketIndex,
  1297          uint256 perWinner,
  1298          uint256 entropy
  1299      )
  1300          private
  1301          returns (uint256 claimDelta, uint256 paidDelta, uint256 newEntropy)
  1302      {
  1303          (
  1304              uint256 claimableDelta,
  1305              uint256 paid,
  1306              uint256 wpSpent,
  1307              uint256 newEnt
  1308          ) = _processSoloBucketWinner(w, perWinner, entropy);
  1309          newEntropy = newEnt;
  1310          claimDelta = claimableDelta;
  1311          if (paid != 0) {
  1312              emit JackpotEthWin(
  1313                  w,
  1314                  lvl,
  1315                  traitId,
  1316                  paid,
  1317                  ticketIndex
  1318              );
  1319              paidDelta += paid;
  1320          }
  1321          if (wpSpent != 0) {
  1322              emit JackpotWhalePassWin(w, lvl, wpSpent / HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE);
  1323              paidDelta += wpSpent;
  1324          }
  1325      }
  1326  
  1327      /// @dev Pays normal (non-solo) bucket winners. Extracted to avoid stack-too-deep in _processDailyEth.
  1328      function _payNormalBucket(
  1329          address[] memory winners,
  1330          uint256[] memory ticketIndexes,
  1331          uint256 perWinner,
  1332          uint24 lvl,
  1333          uint8 traitId
  1334      ) private returns (uint256 totalPaid, uint256 totalLiability) {
  1335          uint256 len = winners.length;
  1336          for (uint256 i; i < len; ) {
  1337              address w = winners[i];
  1338              if (w != address(0)) {
  1339                  uint256 claimableDelta = _addClaimableEth(w, perWinner);
  1340                  emit JackpotEthWin(w, lvl, traitId, perWinner, ticketIndexes[i]);
  1341                  totalPaid += perWinner;
  1342                  totalLiability += claimableDelta;
  1343              }
  1344              unchecked {
  1345                  ++i;
  1346              }
  1347          }
  1348      }
  1349  
  1350      /// @dev Processes solo bucket winner: 75% ETH, 25% as whale passes (only if
  1351      ///      the 25% covers at least one half-pass; otherwise 100% ETH).
  1352      /// @return claimableDelta Amount to add to claimablePool.
  1353      /// @return ethPaid Total ETH value credited.
  1354      /// @return whalePassSpent Amount moved to futurePrizePool from whale pass conversion.
  1355      /// @return newEntropy Updated entropy.
  1356      function _processSoloBucketWinner(
  1357          address winner,
  1358          uint256 perWinner,
  1359          uint256 entropy
  1360      )
  1361          private
  1362          returns (
  1363              uint256 claimableDelta,
  1364              uint256 ethPaid,
  1365              uint256 whalePassSpent,
  1366              uint256 newEntropy
  1367          )
  1368      {
  1369          // 75/25 split: whale pass only if 25% covers at least one half-pass
  1370          uint256 quarterAmount = perWinner >> 2; // perWinner / 4
  1371          uint256 whalePassCount = quarterAmount / HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE;
  1372          newEntropy = entropy;
  1373  
  1374          if (whalePassCount != 0) {
  1375              uint256 whalePassCost = whalePassCount * HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE;
  1376              uint256 ethAmount = perWinner - whalePassCost;
  1377  
  1378              claimableDelta = _addClaimableEth(winner, ethAmount);
  1379              ethPaid = ethAmount;
  1380  
  1381              whalePassClaims[winner] += whalePassCount;
  1382              _setFuturePrizePool(_getFuturePrizePool() + whalePassCost);
  1383              whalePassSpent = whalePassCost;
  1384          } else {
  1385              // 25% too small for a whale pass — pay full amount as ETH
  1386              claimableDelta = _addClaimableEth(winner, perWinner);
  1387              ethPaid = perWinner;
  1388          }
  1389      }
  1390  
  1391      /// @dev Replaces the winning quadrant's trait with a hero-symbol override sampled by
  1392      ///      `_rollHeroSymbol` from the prior day's settled wager pool. Applied to all jackpot
  1393      ///      paths (purchase phase + jackpot phase). Reads `dailyHeroWagers[dailyIdx]`:
  1394      ///      `dailyIdx` is written only at `_unlockRng` (AdvanceModule), so during jackpot
  1395      ///      processing it is frozen at the previous day's index — every consumer in a single
  1396      ///      jackpot resolution therefore reads the same wager pool. Bets placed on day D
  1397      ///      write to `dailyHeroWagers[D]`; day D+1's jackpot reads slot[D] via
  1398      ///      `dailyIdx == D` (set by day D's `_unlockRng`).
  1399      ///
  1400      ///      `heroEntropy` is the raw VRF entropy word for the day; the same value flows into
  1401      ///      every `_applyHeroOverride` invocation within a jackpot resolution, so on days
  1402      ///      that produce both regular and bonus trait rolls both rolls land on the same hero
  1403      ///      `(quadrant, symbol)` pair (only the per-quadrant colors differ, sampled from
  1404      ///      `randomWord`). Symbol entropy and color entropy live in orthogonal domains:
  1405      ///      colors read bit-slices of `randomWord`; the symbol roll consumes
  1406      ///      `keccak256(abi.encode(heroEntropy, day))`.
  1407      function _applyHeroOverride(
  1408          uint8[4] memory w,
  1409          uint256 randomWord,
  1410          uint256 heroEntropy
  1411      ) private view {
  1412          (
  1413              bool hasHeroWinner,
  1414              uint8 heroQuadrant,
  1415              uint8 heroSymbol
  1416          ) = _rollHeroSymbol(dailyIdx, heroEntropy);
  1417          if (!hasHeroWinner) return;
  1418  
  1419          uint8 heroColor;
  1420          if (heroQuadrant == 0) {
  1421              heroColor = uint8(randomWord & 7);
  1422          } else if (heroQuadrant == 1) {
  1423              heroColor = uint8((randomWord >> 3) & 7);
  1424          } else if (heroQuadrant == 2) {
  1425              heroColor = uint8((randomWord >> 6) & 7);
  1426          } else {
  1427              heroColor = uint8((randomWord >> 9) & 7);
  1428          }
  1429  
  1430          w[heroQuadrant] = uint8(
  1431              (uint256(heroQuadrant) << 6) |
  1432                  (uint256(heroColor) << 3) |
  1433                  uint256(heroSymbol)
  1434          );
  1435      }
  1436  
  1437      /// @dev Samples the day's hero `(quadrant, symbol)` via a weighted random roll across
  1438      ///      the 32 packed slots of `dailyHeroWagers[day]`. Pass 1 SLOADs the 4 packed
  1439      ///      quadrants once, decodes 32 uint32 amounts, accumulates the total, and tracks
  1440      ///      the largest-amount slot (first-seen on ties to match the scan order).
  1441      ///      Pass 2 walks the cached weights with a cumulative cursor against
  1442      ///      `pick = uint64(uint256(keccak256(abi.encode(entropy, day))) % effectiveTotal)`
  1443      ///      and applies a `leaderBonus = maxAmount / 2` add at the largest-amount slot —
  1444      ///      effective ×1.5 weight on the leader, no min-wager floor on any other slot.
  1445      ///      Returns `(false, 0, 0)` when no slot has any wagers.
  1446      function _rollHeroSymbol(
  1447          uint24 day,
  1448          uint256 entropy
  1449      )
  1450          private
  1451          view
  1452          returns (bool hasWinner, uint8 winQuadrant, uint8 winSymbol)
  1453      {
  1454          uint32[32] memory weights;
  1455          uint64 total;
  1456          uint32 maxAmount;
  1457          uint8 leaderIdx;
  1458  
  1459          for (uint8 q; q < 4; ) {
  1460              uint256 packed = dailyHeroWagers[day][q];
  1461              for (uint8 s; s < 8; ) {
  1462                  uint32 amount = uint32(
  1463                      (packed >> (uint256(s) * 32)) & 0xFFFFFFFF
  1464                  );
  1465                  uint8 idx;
  1466                  unchecked {
  1467                      idx = (q << 3) | s;
  1468                  }
  1469                  weights[idx] = amount;
  1470                  total += uint64(amount);
  1471                  if (amount > maxAmount) {
  1472                      maxAmount = amount;
  1473                      leaderIdx = idx;
  1474                  }
  1475                  unchecked {
  1476                      ++s;
  1477                  }
  1478              }
  1479              unchecked {
  1480                  ++q;
  1481              }
  1482          }
  1483  
  1484          if (total == 0) {
  1485              return (false, 0, 0);
  1486          }
  1487  
  1488          uint64 leaderBonus = uint64(maxAmount) / 2;
  1489          uint64 effectiveTotal = total + leaderBonus;
  1490          uint64 pick = uint64(
  1491              uint256(keccak256(abi.encode(entropy, day))) % effectiveTotal
  1492          );
  1493  
  1494          uint64 cumulative;
  1495          for (uint8 idx; idx < 32; ) {
  1496              cumulative += uint64(weights[idx]);
  1497              if (idx == leaderIdx) {
  1498                  cumulative += leaderBonus;
  1499              }
  1500              if (cumulative > pick) {
  1501                  return (true, uint8(idx >> 3), uint8(idx & 7));
  1502              }
  1503              unchecked {
  1504                  ++idx;
  1505              }
  1506          }
  1507      }
  1508  
  1509      // =========================================================================
  1510      // Internal Helpers — Winner Selection
  1511      // =========================================================================
  1512  
  1513      /// @dev Selects random winners from a trait's ticket pool, returning both addresses and indices.
  1514      function _randTraitTicket(
  1515          address[][256] storage traitBurnTicket_,
  1516          uint256 randomWord,
  1517          uint8 trait,
  1518          uint8 numWinners,
  1519          uint8 salt
  1520      )
  1521          private
  1522          view
  1523          returns (address[] memory winners, uint256[] memory ticketIndexes)
  1524      {
  1525          address[] storage holders = traitBurnTicket_[trait];
  1526          uint256 len = holders.length;
  1527  
  1528          // Virtual deity entries (if a deity exists for this symbol):
  1529          //   Gold tier (color == 7): flat 1 virtual entry.
  1530          //   Common tier (color in [0..6]): floor(2% of bucket), minimum 2.
  1531          // traitId layout: (quadrant << 6) | (color << 3) | symIdx
  1532          // fullSymId = quadrant * 8 + symIdx
  1533          uint8 fullSymId = (trait >> 6) * 8 + (trait & 0x07);
  1534          address deity;
  1535          uint256 virtualCount;
  1536          if (fullSymId < 32) {
  1537              deity = deityBySymbol[fullSymId];
  1538              if (deity != address(0)) {
  1539                  if (((trait >> 3) & 7) == 7) {
  1540                      virtualCount = 1;
  1541                  } else {
  1542                      virtualCount = len / 50;
  1543                      if (virtualCount < 2) virtualCount = 2;
  1544                  }
  1545              }
  1546          }
  1547  
  1548          uint256 effectiveLen = len + virtualCount;
  1549          if (effectiveLen == 0 || numWinners == 0) {
  1550              return (new address[](0), new uint256[](0));
  1551          }
  1552  
  1553          winners = new address[](numWinners);
  1554          ticketIndexes = new uint256[](numWinners);
  1555          for (uint256 i; i < numWinners; ) {
  1556              uint256 idx = uint256(
  1557                  keccak256(abi.encode(randomWord, trait, salt, i))
  1558              ) % effectiveLen;
  1559              if (idx < len) {
  1560                  winners[i] = holders[idx];
  1561                  ticketIndexes[i] = idx;
  1562              } else {
  1563                  winners[i] = deity;
  1564                  ticketIndexes[i] = type(uint256).max;
  1565              }
  1566              unchecked {
  1567                  ++i;
  1568              }
  1569          }
  1570      }
  1571  
  1572      /// @notice Pays daily BURNIE jackpot to random ticket holders.
  1573      /// @dev Runs every day in its own transaction. Awards 0.5% of prize pool target in BURNIE.
  1574      ///      75% goes to near-future trait-matched winners in [minLevel, maxLevel].
  1575      ///      25% goes to far-future ticketQueue holders ([lvl+5, lvl+99]).
  1576      /// @param lvl Current level.
  1577      /// @param randWord VRF entropy for winner selection.
  1578      /// @param minLevel Minimum target level for near-future coin distribution (inclusive).
  1579      /// @param maxLevel Maximum target level for near-future coin distribution (inclusive).
  1580      function payDailyCoinJackpot(uint24 lvl, uint256 randWord, uint24 minLevel, uint24 maxLevel) external {
  1581          uint256 coinBudget = _calcDailyCoinBudget(lvl);
  1582          if (coinBudget == 0) return;
  1583  
  1584          // Split: 25% far-future, 75% near-future
  1585          uint256 farBudget = (coinBudget * FAR_FUTURE_COIN_BPS) / 10_000;
  1586          uint256 nearBudget = coinBudget - farBudget;
  1587  
  1588          // --- Far-future portion (ticketQueue-based, no traits) ---
  1589          _awardFarFutureCoinJackpot(lvl, farBudget, randWord);
  1590  
  1591          // --- Near-future portion (trait-matched) ---
  1592          if (nearBudget == 0) return;
  1593  
  1594          uint32 bonusTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, true);
  1595  
  1596          _awardDailyCoinToTraitWinners(
  1597              minLevel,
  1598              maxLevel,
  1599              bonusTraitsPacked,
  1600              nearBudget,
  1601              randWord
  1602          );
  1603      }
  1604  
  1605      /// @dev Emit DailyWinningTraits without running any distribution.
  1606      ///      Used at purchaseLevel==1 where payDailyJackpot is skipped and two coin
  1607      ///      jackpots replace the ETH jackpot. First coin call (the "main") uses
  1608      ///      bonus-derived traits from randWord. Second coin call uses traits from
  1609      ///      a salted randWord (keccak256(randWord, BONUS_TRAITS_TAG)).
  1610      /// @param bonusTargetLevel Target level for the first (main-equivalent) coin distribution.
  1611      function emitDailyWinningTraits(uint24, uint256 randWord, uint24 bonusTargetLevel) external {
  1612          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.GAME) revert OnlyGame();
  1613          uint24 questDay = _simulatedDayIndex();
  1614          uint32 mainTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(randWord, true);
  1615          uint256 saltedRng = uint256(keccak256(abi.encodePacked(randWord, BONUS_TRAITS_TAG)));
  1616          uint32 bonusTraitsPacked = _rollWinningTraits(saltedRng, true);
  1617          emit DailyWinningTraits(questDay, mainTraitsPacked, bonusTraitsPacked, bonusTargetLevel);
  1618      }
  1619  
  1620      /// @dev Awards BURNIE to per-pull random ticket holders across [minLevel, maxLevel].
  1621      ///      Each pull samples its own random level via keccak256(randomWord, COIN_LEVEL_TAG, i)
  1622      ///      and rotates trait deterministically via i % 4. Each pull awards the floored
  1623      ///      whole-BURNIE `baseAmount` (1 BURNIE = 1 ether); empty (lvl', trait_i) buckets
  1624      ///      silently skip. Sub-1-BURNIE residues — the `coinBudget % cap` remainder and any
  1625      ///      sub-1-ether base — evaporate.
  1626      ///      Per-trait deity addresses are cached at loop entry; the holder-index keccak is
  1627      ///      keccak256(randomWord, trait_i, lvlPrime, i) so two pulls at the same (trait, i)
  1628      ///      but different sampled levels do not collapse to the same holder index.
  1629      function _awardDailyCoinToTraitWinners(
  1630          uint24 minLevel,
  1631          uint24 maxLevel,
  1632          uint32 winningTraitsPacked,
  1633          uint256 coinBudget,
  1634          uint256 randomWord
  1635      ) private {
  1636          if (coinBudget == 0) return;
  1637          uint16 cap = DAILY_COIN_MAX_WINNERS;
  1638          if (cap > coinBudget) cap = uint16(coinBudget);
  1639  
  1640          uint8[4] memory traitIds = JackpotBucketLib.unpackWinningTraits(
  1641              winningTraitsPacked
  1642          );
  1643  
  1644          // Per-trait deity cache: deityBySymbol is level-independent, so one read per trait
  1645          // serves all 50 pulls of that trait.
  1646          address[4] memory deityCache;
  1647          for (uint8 t; t < 4; ) {
  1648              uint8 trait = traitIds[t];
  1649              uint8 fullSymId = (trait >> 6) * 8 + (trait & 0x07);
  1650              if (fullSymId < 32) {
  1651                  deityCache[t] = deityBySymbol[fullSymId];
  1652              }
  1653              unchecked { ++t; }
  1654          }
  1655  
  1656          uint256 baseAmount = ((coinBudget / cap) / 1 ether) * 1 ether;
  1657          uint24 range = maxLevel - minLevel + 1;
  1658  
  1659          for (uint256 i; i < cap; ) {
  1660              uint8 traitIdx = uint8(i % 4);
  1661              uint8 trait_i = traitIds[traitIdx];
  1662  
  1663              uint24 lvlPrime = minLevel + uint24(uint256(keccak256(
  1664                  abi.encode(randomWord, COIN_LEVEL_TAG, i)
  1665              )) % range);
  1666  
  1667              address[] storage holders = traitBurnTicket[lvlPrime][trait_i];
  1668              uint256 len = holders.length;
  1669              address deity = deityCache[traitIdx];
  1670              uint256 virtualCount;
  1671              // Virtual deity entries (if a deity exists for this symbol):
  1672              //   Gold tier (color == 7): flat 1 virtual entry.
  1673              //   Common tier (color in [0..6]): floor(2% of bucket), minimum 2.
  1674              if (deity != address(0)) {
  1675                  if (((trait_i >> 3) & 7) == 7) {
  1676                      virtualCount = 1;
  1677                  } else {
  1678                      virtualCount = len / 50;
  1679                      if (virtualCount < 2) virtualCount = 2;
  1680                  }
  1681              }
  1682              uint256 effectiveLen = len + virtualCount;
  1683              if (effectiveLen == 0) {
  1684                  unchecked {
  1685                      ++i;
  1686                  }
  1687                  continue;
  1688              }
  1689  
  1690              uint256 idx = uint256(keccak256(
  1691                  abi.encode(randomWord, trait_i, lvlPrime, i)
  1692              )) % effectiveLen;
  1693              address winner;
  1694              uint256 ticketIdx;
  1695              if (idx < len) {
  1696                  winner = holders[idx];
  1697                  ticketIdx = idx;
  1698              } else {
  1699                  winner = deity;
  1700                  ticketIdx = type(uint256).max;
  1701              }
  1702  
  1703              uint256 amount = baseAmount;
  1704  
  1705              if (winner != address(0) && amount != 0) {
  1706                  emit JackpotBurnieWin(
  1707                      winner,
  1708                      lvlPrime,
  1709                      trait_i,
  1710                      amount,
  1711                      ticketIdx
  1712                  );
  1713                  coinflip.creditFlip(winner, amount);
  1714              }
  1715  
  1716              unchecked {
  1717                  ++i;
  1718              }
  1719          }
  1720      }
  1721  
  1722      /// @dev Awards 25% of the BURNIE coin budget to random ticket holders on far-future levels.
  1723      ///      Samples up to 10 random levels in [lvl+5, lvl+99], picks 1 winner per level from
  1724      ///      that level's ticketQueue (traits not yet assigned), and splits the budget evenly.
  1725      function _awardFarFutureCoinJackpot(
  1726          uint24 lvl,
  1727          uint256 farBudget,
  1728          uint256 rngWord
  1729      ) private {
  1730          if (farBudget == 0) return;
  1731  
  1732          uint256 entropy = uint256(
  1733              keccak256(abi.encode(rngWord, lvl, FAR_FUTURE_COIN_TAG))
  1734          );
  1735  
  1736          // First pass: find up to FAR_FUTURE_COIN_SAMPLES winners from ticketQueue
  1737          address[10] memory winners;
  1738          uint24[10] memory winnerLevels;
  1739          uint8 found;
  1740  
  1741          for (uint8 s; s < FAR_FUTURE_COIN_SAMPLES; ) {
  1742              entropy = EntropyLib.hash2(entropy, s);
  1743  
  1744              // Pick a random level in [lvl+5, lvl+99]
  1745              uint24 candidate = lvl + 5 + uint24(entropy % 95);
  1746  
  1747              address[] storage queue = ticketQueue[_tqFarFutureKey(candidate)];
  1748              uint256 len = queue.length;
  1749  
  1750              if (len != 0) {
  1751                  address winner = queue[(entropy >> 32) % len];
  1752                  if (winner != address(0)) {
  1753                      winners[found] = winner;
  1754                      winnerLevels[found] = candidate;
  1755                      unchecked {
  1756                          ++found;
  1757                      }
  1758                  }
  1759              }
  1760  
  1761              unchecked {
  1762                  ++s;
  1763              }
  1764          }
  1765  
  1766          if (found == 0) return;
  1767  
  1768          // Distribute evenly among found winners, floored to whole-BURNIE
  1769          // (1 BURNIE = 1 ether); sub-1-BURNIE residue evaporates.
  1770          uint256 perWinner = ((farBudget / found) / 1 ether) * 1 ether;
  1771          if (perWinner == 0) return;
  1772  
  1773          address[] memory batchPlayers = new address[](found);
  1774          uint256[] memory batchAmounts = new uint256[](found);
  1775  
  1776          for (uint8 i; i < found; ) {
  1777              emit FarFutureCoinJackpotWinner(
  1778                  winners[i],
  1779                  lvl,
  1780                  winnerLevels[i],
  1781                  perWinner
  1782              );
  1783  
  1784              batchPlayers[i] = winners[i];
  1785              batchAmounts[i] = perWinner;
  1786  
  1787              unchecked {
  1788                  ++i;
  1789              }
  1790          }
  1791  
  1792          coinflip.creditFlipBatch(batchPlayers, batchAmounts);
  1793      }
  1794  
  1795      /// @dev Roll winning traits with hero symbol override.
  1796      ///      All paths use fully random traits (6 bits per quadrant).
  1797      ///      Hero override replaces the winning quadrant's trait if a top hero symbol exists.
  1798      /// @param randWord VRF entropy.
  1799      /// @param isBonus When true, applies keccak256 domain separation for independent bonus traits.
  1800      function _rollWinningTraits(
  1801          uint256 randWord,
  1802          bool isBonus
  1803      ) private view returns (uint32 packed) {
  1804          uint256 r = isBonus
  1805              ? uint256(keccak256(abi.encodePacked(randWord, BONUS_TRAITS_TAG)))
  1806              : randWord;
  1807          uint8[4] memory traits = JackpotBucketLib.getRandomTraits(r);
  1808          _applyHeroOverride(traits, r, randWord);
  1809          packed = JackpotBucketLib.packWinningTraits(traits);
  1810      }
  1811  
  1812      /// @dev Calculate 0.5% of prize pool target in BURNIE.
  1813      function _calcDailyCoinBudget(uint24 lvl) private view returns (uint256) {
  1814          uint256 priceWei = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(level);
  1815          if (priceWei == 0) return 0;
  1816          return (levelPrizePool[lvl - 1] * PRICE_COIN_UNIT) / (priceWei * 200);
  1817      }
  1818  
  1819      /// @dev Current-pool daily jackpot share:
  1820      ///      - Days 1-4: random 6%-14% (avg 10%)
  1821      ///      - Day 5: 100% of remaining currentPrizePool
  1822      function _dailyCurrentPoolBps(
  1823          uint8 counter,
  1824          uint256 randWord
  1825      ) private pure returns (uint16 bps) {
  1826          if (counter >= JACKPOT_LEVEL_CAP - 1) return 10_000;
  1827  
  1828          uint16 range = DAILY_CURRENT_BPS_MAX - DAILY_CURRENT_BPS_MIN + 1;
  1829          uint256 seed = uint256(
  1830              keccak256(
  1831                  abi.encodePacked(randWord, DAILY_CURRENT_BPS_TAG, counter)
  1832              )
  1833          );
  1834          return uint16(DAILY_CURRENT_BPS_MIN + (seed % range));
  1835      }
  1836  
  1837      function _packDailyTicketBudgets(
  1838          uint8 counterStep,
  1839          uint256 dailyTicketUnits,
  1840          uint256 carryoverTicketUnits,
  1841          uint8 carryoverSourceOffset
  1842      ) private pure returns (uint256) {
  1843          return
  1844              uint256(counterStep) |
  1845              (dailyTicketUnits << 8) |
  1846              (carryoverTicketUnits << 72) |
  1847              (uint256(carryoverSourceOffset) << 136);
  1848      }
  1849  
  1850      function _unpackDailyTicketBudgets(
  1851          uint256 packed
  1852      )
  1853          private
  1854          pure
  1855          returns (
  1856              uint8 counterStep,
  1857              uint256 dailyTicketUnits,
  1858              uint256 carryoverTicketUnits,
  1859              uint8 carryoverSourceOffset
  1860          )
  1861      {
  1862          counterStep = uint8(packed);
  1863          dailyTicketUnits = uint64(packed >> 8);
  1864          carryoverTicketUnits = uint64(packed >> 72);
  1865          carryoverSourceOffset = uint8(packed >> 136);
  1866      }
  1867  
  1868      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1869      // Reward Jackpots (BAF + Decimator Dispatch)
  1870      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
  1871  
  1872      /**
  1873       * @notice Execute BAF (Big-Ass Flip) jackpot distribution.
  1874       * @dev Large winners (>=5% of pool) receive 50% ETH / 50% lootbox.
  1875       *      Small winners (<5% of pool) alternate: even-index gets 100% ETH,
  1876       *      odd-index gets 100% lootbox (gas-efficient batching).
  1877       *
  1878       * @param poolWei Total ETH for BAF distribution.
  1879       * @param lvl Level triggering the BAF.
  1880       * @param rngWord VRF entropy for winner selection.
  1881       * @return claimableDelta ETH credited to claimable balances.
  1882       *         Refund, lootbox, and whale pass ETH stay in futurePool implicitly.
  1883       *
  1884       * ## Payout Split
  1885       *
  1886       * | Winner Size        | Portion | Reward Type                              |
  1887       * |--------------------|---------|------------------------------------------|
  1888       * | Large (>=5% pool)  | 50%     | Claimable ETH (immediate)                |
  1889       * | Large (>=5% pool)  | 50%     | Lootbox future tickets (claimWhalePass)  |
  1890       * | Small even-index   | 100%    | Claimable ETH (immediate)                |
  1891       * | Small odd-index    | 100%    | Lootbox future tickets                   |
  1892       *
  1893       * ## Lootbox Flow (Tiered by Amount)
  1894       *
  1895       * **All payouts:**
  1896       * - Large lootbox payouts defer via `claimWhalePass` for gas safety
  1897       *
  1898       * All lootbox ETH stays in futurePrizePool (source pool).
  1899       *
  1900       */
  1901      function runBafJackpot(
  1902          uint256 poolWei,
  1903          uint24 lvl,
  1904          uint256 rngWord
  1905      ) external returns (uint256 claimableDelta) {
  1906          if (msg.sender != address(this)) revert E();
  1907          // Get winners and payout info from jackpots contract
  1908          (address[] memory winnersArr, uint256[] memory amountsArr, ) = jackpots
  1909              .runBafJackpot(poolWei, lvl, rngWord);
  1910  
  1911          // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
  1912          // Process each winner with gas-optimized payout structure
  1913          // Large winners (>=5% of pool): 50% ETH, 50% lootbox (balanced)
  1914          // Small winners (<5% of pool): alternate 100% ETH or 100% lootbox (gas-efficient)
  1915          // ---------------------------------------------------------------------
  1916  
  1917          uint256 largeWinnerThreshold = poolWei / 20; // 5% of total BAF pool
  1918  
  1919          uint256 winnersLen = winnersArr.length;
  1920          for (uint256 i; i < winnersLen; ) {
  1921              address winner = winnersArr[i];
  1922              uint256 amount = amountsArr[i];
  1923  
  1924              // Large winners: keep 50/50 split for balanced payout
  1925              if (amount >= largeWinnerThreshold) {
  1926                  uint256 ethPortion = amount / 2;
  1927                  uint256 lootboxPortion = amount - ethPortion;
  1928  
  1929                  // Credit ETH half to claimable balance
  1930                  {
  1931                      uint256 cd = _addClaimableEth(winner, ethPortion);
  1932                      claimableDelta += cd;
  1933                      emit JackpotEthWin(winner, lvl, BAF_TRAIT_SENTINEL, ethPortion, 0);
  1934                  }
  1935  
  1936                  // Lootbox half: small amounts awarded immediately, large deferred
  1937                  if (lootboxPortion <= LOOTBOX_CLAIM_THRESHOLD) {
  1938                      // Small lootbox: award immediately (2 rolls, probabilistic targeting).
  1939                      // JackpotTicketWin is emitted per-roll inside _jackpotTicketRoll
  1940                      // with the real targetLevel and scaled ticketCount.
  1941                      rngWord = _awardJackpotTickets(
  1942                          winner,
  1943                          lootboxPortion,
  1944                          lvl,
  1945                          rngWord
  1946                      );
  1947                  } else {
  1948                      // Large lootbox: defer to claim (whale pass equivalent)
  1949                      _queueWhalePassClaimCore(winner, lootboxPortion);
  1950                      emit JackpotWhalePassWin(
  1951                          winner,
  1952                          lvl,
  1953                          lootboxPortion / HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE
  1954                      );
  1955                  }
  1956              }
  1957              // Small winners: alternate between 100% ETH and 100% lootbox for gas efficiency
  1958              else if (i % 2 == 0) {
  1959                  // Even index: 100% ETH (immediate liquidity)
  1960                  uint256 cd = _addClaimableEth(winner, amount);
  1961                  claimableDelta += cd;
  1962                  emit JackpotEthWin(winner, lvl, BAF_TRAIT_SENTINEL, amount, 0);
  1963              } else {
  1964                  // Odd index: 100% lootbox (upside exposure).
  1965                  // JackpotTicketWin is emitted per-roll inside _jackpotTicketRoll;
  1966                  // whale-pass fallback (amount > LOOTBOX_CLAIM_THRESHOLD) emits
  1967                  // JackpotWhalePassWin inside _awardJackpotTickets.
  1968                  rngWord = _awardJackpotTickets(winner, amount, lvl, rngWord);
  1969              }
  1970  
  1971              unchecked {
  1972                  ++i;
  1973              }
  1974          }
  1975  
  1976          // Refund + lootbox + whale pass ETH stays in futurePool implicitly:
  1977          // caller only deducts claimableDelta from memFuture. No storage write needed.
  1978      }
  1979  
  1980      /**
  1981       * @notice Unified jackpot ticket award function for all jackpots.
  1982       * @dev Awards tickets using two-tier system:
  1983       *      Small (0.5-5 ETH): Split in half, 2 probabilistic rolls
  1984       *      Large (> 5 ETH): Whale pass equivalent (100-ticket chunks)
  1985       *      Uses actual game ticket pricing for target levels.
  1986       *
  1987       * @param winner Address to receive rewards.
  1988       * @param amount ETH amount for ticket conversion.
  1989       * @param minTargetLevel Minimum target level for tickets.
  1990       * @param entropy RNG state.
  1991       * @return Updated entropy state.
  1992       */
  1993      function _awardJackpotTickets(
  1994          address winner,
  1995          uint256 amount,
  1996          uint24 minTargetLevel,
  1997          uint256 entropy
  1998      ) private returns (uint256) {
  1999          // Large amounts (> 5 ETH): defer to whale pass claim system
  2000          if (amount > LOOTBOX_CLAIM_THRESHOLD) {
  2001              _queueWhalePassClaimCore(winner, amount);
  2002              emit JackpotWhalePassWin(
  2003                  winner,
  2004                  minTargetLevel,
  2005                  amount / HALF_WHALE_PASS_PRICE
  2006              );
  2007              return entropy;
  2008          }
  2009  
  2010          // Very small amounts (<= 0.5 ETH): single roll
  2011          if (amount <= SMALL_LOOTBOX_THRESHOLD) {
  2012              return _jackpotTicketRoll(winner, amount, minTargetLevel, entropy);
  2013          }
  2014  
  2015          // Medium amounts (0.5-5 ETH): split in half, 2 rolls
  2016          uint256 halfAmount = amount / 2;
  2017  
  2018          // First roll
  2019          entropy = _jackpotTicketRoll(
  2020              winner,
  2021              halfAmount,
  2022              minTargetLevel,
  2023              entropy
  2024          );
  2025  
  2026          // Second roll (with remainder if amount was odd)
  2027          uint256 secondAmount = amount - halfAmount;
  2028          entropy = _jackpotTicketRoll(
  2029              winner,
  2030              secondAmount,
  2031              minTargetLevel,
  2032              entropy
  2033          );
  2034  
  2035          return entropy;
  2036      }
  2037  
  2038      /**
  2039       * @notice Resolve a single jackpot ticket roll into ticket awards.
  2040       * @dev Selects target level based on probability, then Bernoulli-collapses
  2041       *      the scaled ticket count to a whole-ticket count before queueing.
  2042       *      Uses actual game pricing for the selected target level.
  2043       *      Entropy bit allocation in the per-roll keccak word `entropy`
  2044       *      (evolved via EntropyLib.hash2 on entry, so every bit — including
  2045       *      the low bits read below — is full-diffusion keccak output):
  2046       *        bits[0..12]     path/level selection — `entropy % 100` range roll,
  2047       *                        `(entropy / 100) % 4` near offset,
  2048       *                        `(entropy / 100) % 46` far offset
  2049       *        bits[200..215]  jackpotTicketRoundUp % 100 — Bernoulli whole-ticket
  2050       *                        collapse sub-roll (relative bias < 0.10%)
  2051       *      The two consumption windows are separated by 180+ bits of the same
  2052       *      256-bit keccak word, so the round-up sub-roll is statistically
  2053       *      independent of the path/level selection.
  2054       * @param winner Address to receive tickets.
  2055       * @param amount ETH amount for this roll.
  2056       * @param minTargetLevel Minimum target level (usually current level during SETUP phase).
  2057       * @param entropy RNG state.
  2058       * @return Updated entropy state.
  2059       */
  2060      function _jackpotTicketRoll(
  2061          address winner,
  2062          uint256 amount,
  2063          uint24 minTargetLevel,
  2064          uint256 entropy
  2065      ) private returns (uint256) {
  2066          entropy = EntropyLib.hash2(entropy, entropy);
  2067  
  2068          // Roll for outcome (0-99 for percentage-based probabilities)
  2069          uint256 entropyDiv100 = entropy / 100;
  2070          uint256 roll = entropy - (entropyDiv100 * 100);
  2071          uint24 targetLevel;
  2072  
  2073          if (roll < 30) {
  2074              // 30% chance: minimum level ticket
  2075              targetLevel = minTargetLevel;
  2076          } else if (roll < 95) {
  2077              // 65% chance: +1 to +4 levels ahead
  2078              uint256 offset = 1 + (entropyDiv100 % 4); // 1-4 inclusive
  2079              targetLevel = minTargetLevel + uint24(offset);
  2080          } else {
  2081              // 5% chance: +5 to +50 levels ahead (rare)
  2082              uint256 offset = 5 + (entropyDiv100 % 46); // 5-50 inclusive
  2083              targetLevel = minTargetLevel + uint24(offset);
  2084          }
  2085  
  2086          // Calculate tickets for target level
  2087          uint256 targetPrice = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(targetLevel);
  2088  
  2089          uint256 quantityScaled = (amount * TICKET_SCALE) / targetPrice;
  2090  
  2091          // Bernoulli-collapse the scaled count to a whole-ticket count: the
  2092          // fractional part rounds up with probability frac/TICKET_SCALE using
  2093          // bits[200..215] of the per-roll entropy word.
  2094          uint32 scaledTickets = uint32(quantityScaled);
  2095          uint32 whole = scaledTickets / uint32(TICKET_SCALE);
  2096          uint32 frac = scaledTickets % uint32(TICKET_SCALE);
  2097          bool roundedUp = false;
  2098          if (frac != 0 && (uint16(entropy >> 200) % uint16(TICKET_SCALE)) < uint16(frac)) {
  2099              unchecked {
  2100                  whole += 1;
  2101              }
  2102              roundedUp = true;
  2103          }
  2104          _queueTickets(winner, targetLevel, whole, true);
  2105  
  2106          // ticketCount is the whole ticket count queued above; roundedUp is true
  2107          // iff the bits[200..215] Bernoulli sub-roll incremented that count.
  2108          emit JackpotTicketWin(
  2109              winner,
  2110              targetLevel,
  2111              BAF_TRAIT_SENTINEL,
  2112              whole,
  2113              minTargetLevel,
  2114              0,
  2115              roundedUp
  2116          );
  2117  
  2118          return entropy;
  2119      }
  2120  }
