    12  /// @title IGameRouter
    13  /// @notice Minimal in-context self-call surface the router uses to reach the
    14  ///         Game-proper advance entrypoint. The router runs in the Game's storage
    15  ///         context (delegatecall), so `address(this)` IS the Game;
    16  ///         the self-call re-enters the Game's own `advanceGame` dispatch (which
    17  ///         delegatecalls the AdvanceModule, running the required-path process STAGE
    18  ///         in-context — 349-05). Signatures match `DegenerusGame.sol` verbatim
    19  ///         (`advanceGame` :275 / `advanceDue` :1690). `mintPrice` / `level` are read
    20  ///         in-context (inherited helpers), so they are NOT routed through here.
    21  interface IGameRouter {
    22      function advanceGame() external returns (uint8 mult);
    23      function advanceDue() external view returns (bool);
    24      function enqueueBoxForAutoOpen(uint48 index, address player) external;
    25  }
    26  
    27  /**
    28   * @title GameAfkingModule
    29   * @author Burnie Degenerus
    30   * @notice Delegate-called module owning the AfKing subscription logic. Its bytecode
    31   *         is its OWN EIP-170 budget — 0 B to the DegenerusGame image — so the
    32   *         running-total is unaffected by this module.
    33   *
    34   * @dev DELEGATECALL CONTEXT: the module inherits `DegenerusGameStorage` (via
    35   *      `DegenerusGameMintStreakUtils`), so the subscriber set
    36   *      (`_subOf`/`_subscribers`/`_subscriberIndex`), the cursors
    37   *      (`_subCursor`/`_subOpenCursor`), the `subsFullyProcessed` STAGE
    38   *      drain-completion flag, the `afkingFunding` ledger, `claimablePool`, `operatorApprovals`,
    39   *      and the activity-score helpers are all in-context plain SLOADs/SSTOREs.
    40   *      The operator-approval / pass-horizon / afking-snapshot / afking-funding
    41   *      reads are all in-context here (the established module pattern — cf.
    42   *      `DegenerusGameBingoModule` reading `operatorApprovals` directly). The Game
    43   *      reaches these via its delegatecall dispatch stubs; a direct call to this
    44   *      module address would have the wrong `msg.sender` for any Game-context
    45   *      invariant.
    46   *
    47   * @dev PART A: `subscribe` — the SINGLE consent-gated subscription
    48   *      entrypoint (create / replace / cancel) carrying the CONSENT-01 OPEN-E gates
    49   *      verbatim + the FREEZE-01 rngLock guard + the 500 active-sub cap guard — and
    50   *      the REQUIRED-PATH PROCESS
    51   *      STAGE (the chunked pre-RNG stamp pass the AdvanceModule STAGE drives across
    52   *      the set, 349-05).
    53   * @dev PART B (this plan, 349-04, same file): the post-RNG OPEN-PASS (the
    54   *      afking-stamp open leg, driven by `_subOpenCursor`, materializing each box
    55   *      from its frozen stamp via a delegatecall to the LootboxModule's
    56   *      `resolveAfkingBox` — the FROZEN-INPUT twin of `resolveLootboxDirect`) and
    57   *      the ROUTER (`mintBurnie`/`autoOpen`, the one-category early-return
    58   *      dispatch). The open consumes the stamp the PART-A process STAGE produces.
    59   * @dev PLACE-02 bounty: the buy/process bounty FOLDS INTO the advance bounty
    60   *      (`mintBurnie`'s advance leg pays `2×·mult`, scaling the AdvanceModule's
    61   *      day-epoch stall `mult` 2×/4×/6× — the process STAGE rides it); the OPEN
    62   *      stays a NORMAL post-RNG `OPEN_BATCH`-style router category with the
    63   *      `OPEN_KNEE` work-scaled pro-rate (farm-by-splitting resistant). Payment is
    64   *      the deferred `creditFlip` BURNIE flip-credit (never a transfer / mintForGame).
    65   *
    66   * @custom:invariant No reentrancy guard — strict CEI everywhere; the module is
    67   *                   never a payee. The two-tier funding-skip exemption keys on
    68   *                   the un-spoofable pinned `ContractAddresses.VAULT` / `SDGNRS`
    69   *                   identity (on `player`, never `src`) — no settable exemption.
    70   * @custom:invariant NO error-swallowing valve anywhere (D-348-04 / REVERT-02
    71   *                   no-valve): the funded process buy is revert-free by
    72   *                   construction (obligation 1 — REVERT-01); a class-B solvency
    73   *                   underflow FAILS LOUD (the `claimablePool -=` propagates, it is
    74   *                   never swallowed). There is no try-block / handler pair.
    75   */
    76  contract GameAfkingModule is DegenerusGameMintStreakUtils {
    77      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
    78                                Custom errors
    79      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
    80      // error RngLocked() — inherited from DegenerusGameStorage. Reverts a
    81      // subscribe (create / replace / cancel) attempted during the RNG freeze
    82      // window: the subscriber set must be frozen across [request -> unlock].
    83      /// @dev subscribe with reinvestPct > 100 (a percentage).
    84      error InvalidReinvestPct();
    85      /// @dev Third-party subscribe(player, ...) where the caller is neither the
    86      ///      player nor a game operator the player approved; OR a non-zero,
    87      ///      non-self fundingSource that has not operator-approved the subscriber.
    88      error NotApproved();
    89      /// @dev subscribe(_, 0) cancel where the caller has no active subscription
    90      ///      (nothing to tombstone).
    91      error NotSubscribed();
    92      /// @dev subscribe would grow the active subscriber set past the uint16 cursor
    93      ///      cap (65,535). NEW-subscriber path only — re-subscribe never trips it.
    94      error SubscriberCapReached();
    95      /// @dev mintBurnie() found all router categories empty — the clean no-work signal
    96      ///      (ROUTER-06; the unbounded-scan-free early-return on no pending work).
    97      error NoWork();
    98      /// @dev subscribe (upsert) where the subscriber's live pass horizon does not reach
    99      ///      the current level — an active sub must hold a pass that covers `level` so it
   100      ///      cannot occupy a subscriber slot without a valid pass.
   101      error NoPass();
   102      /// @dev subscribe (upsert) starting a NEW afking run that is not grounded on a real
   103      ///      purchase — neither already bought today nor a funded in-tx cover-buy. An
   104      ///      unfunded start now reverts instead of beginning an inert, free-riding run.
   105      error MustPurchaseToBeginAfking();

   110      /// @dev Single canonical subscription-state stream — POST-WRITE full state.
   111      ///      Cancel (subscribe(_, 0)) emits with dailyQuantity == 0.
   112      ///      `fundingSource` is the stored funding wallet (address(0) = self);
   113      ///      indexed so a source can filter the log for every account it funds.
   114      event SubscriptionUpdated(
   115          address indexed player,
   116          uint8 dailyQuantity,
   117          bool drainGameCreditFirst,
   118          bool useTickets,
   119          uint8 reinvestPct,
   120          address indexed fundingSource
   121      );
   122      /// @dev Per-player pre-check skip inside the process pass. `reason`:

   124      ///        3 = InsufficientPool  (afkingFunding[src] < ethValue) — funding skip
   125      ///      lastAutoBoughtDay is UNCHANGED on a skip.
   126      event PlayerSkipped(address indexed player, uint8 reason);
   127      /// @dev Pass-validity refresh — emitted at the AFSUB-03 crossing branch when
   128      ///      the re-read horizon still covers the current level. Writes the new

   130      event SubscriptionExtendedFree(address indexed player, uint24 day);
   131      /// @dev Subscription removed from the iterable set. `reason`:

   133      ///        2 = CancelReclaim (in-pass reclaim of an externally-cancelled tombstone)
   134      event SubscriptionExpired(address indexed player, uint8 reason);

   152      /// @dev Afking-local ticket scaling multiplier. TICKET_SCALE = 400 makes the
   153      ///      cost formula unit-consistent: a ticket `amount = effectiveQty * 400`
   154      ///      entry-units, which the Game's mint recompute divides by `4 * 100`
   155      ///      (the inherited Storage `TICKET_SCALE = 100`), so `cost` stays
   156      ///      `mintPrice * effectiveQty` in both ticket and lootbox mode.
   157      ///      ⚠ 348-INVARIANT-CARRY §3-i (LOAD-BEARING dual constant): this 400 is
   158      ///      NUMERICALLY EQUAL to the Game's `4 * TICKET_SCALE` (= 4 × 100) but is a
   159      ///      DISTINCT named constant — it must NOT be collapsed with the inherited
   160      ///      `TICKET_SCALE` (100). They play different roles (entry-unit multiplier
   161      ///      vs the Game divisor base) that happen to compose to the same 400.
   162      uint256 internal constant AFKING_TICKET_SCALE = 400;
   163  
   164      /// @dev drainGameCreditFirst bit within Sub.flags — when set the buy spends
   165      ///      protocol-side claimable credit before tapping afkingFunding ETH.

   177      uint8 internal constant FLAG_EXTERNAL_FUNDING = 1;
   178  
   179      /// @dev Active-subscriber cap = 500. Bounds the iterable set the protocol pays
   180      ///      to iterate every cycle — the advance chain walks `_subscribers` in the
   181      ///      process/open passes, so an unbounded set would bog the daily heartbeat.
   182      ///      1000 keeps the per-cycle work cheap (every pass is weight-/OPEN_BATCH-chunked,
   183      ///      so the cap bounds total subs, not per-tx gas) and sits well within the uint16
   184      ///      `_subCursor`/`_subOpenCursor` range (no cursor aliasing). `subscribe`
   185      ///      reverts a NEW-subscriber insert at the cap; a re-subscribe of an existing
   186      ///      member does not grow the set, so it is exempt. Demand past 1000 is not the
   187      ///      protocol's burden to service — those users arrange their own keepering.
   188      uint256 internal constant SUBSCRIBER_CAP = 1000;
   189  
   190      /// @dev Per-sub gas-weight of a LOOTBOX buy — the unit the ticket/evict weights are ratioed
   191      ///      against. Measured ≈34k marginal; pinned at 2 (not 1) so ticket (≈73k → 4) and evict
   192      ///      (≈18k → 1) land on integer ratios and every op costs ~18k per weight-unit, making the
   193      ///      chunk gas composition-flat (`per-call overhead + budget × ~18k`, any mix).
   194      uint256 internal constant SUB_STAGE_LOOTBOX_WEIGHT = 2;
   195  
   196      /// @dev Per-sub gas-weight of an in-stage sub-ending finalize (cancel-reclaim / pass-evict
   197      ///      / funding-kill) relative to the lootbox-buy unit (weight 2). The finalize does a
   198      ///      cross-contract quest read + streak write the call-free buy does not; measured ≈18k vs
   199      ///      the ≈34k lootbox marginal → weight 1. The chunk ends on accumulated weight, bounding
   200      ///      every mix under the advance-chain ceiling.
   201      uint256 internal constant SUB_STAGE_EVICT_WEIGHT = 1;
   202  
   203      /// @dev Per-sub gas-weight of a TICKET buy relative to the lootbox-buy unit (weight 2). A
   204      ///      ticket queues a cold ticketQueue push + an owed-mapping SSTORE the lootbox stamp does
   205      ///      not — measured ≈73k vs the ≈34k lootbox marginal → weight 4. Weighting the two buy
   206      ///      modes by true marginal cost makes the chunk gas composition-flat (~18k per weight-unit
   207      ///      either way), so the budget binds on real gas, not sub count.
   208      uint256 internal constant SUB_STAGE_TICKET_WEIGHT = 4;
   209

   211      ///      (a private constant not visible cross-contract). Each delivered afking buy accrues
   212      ///      `QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD` (whole BURNIE) into the sub's claimable `pendingBurnie`, pulled
   213      ///      via `claimAfkingBurnie`. Only values the BURNIE mint, off the solvency path.
   214      uint256 internal constant QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD = 100 ether;
   215  
   216      /// @dev Prize-pool routing splits for the batched afking buy, mirroring the canonical

   219      ///      lootbox spend routes 90% future / 10% next; a ticket spend the inverse.
   220      uint256 internal constant AFKING_LOOTBOX_FUTURE_BPS = 9000;
   221      uint256 internal constant AFKING_TICKET_FUTURE_BPS = 1000;
   222  
   223      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
   224                            Router bounty constants (PLACE-02)
   225      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   226      /// @dev ETH-equivalent advance/open-bounty target per unit of work (in ETH wei).
   227      ///      A frozen constant (a module cannot hold a deploy-time immutable in the
   228      ///      Game's storage context). ⚠ The bounty target tune is the GAS phase's charge;
   229      ///      this carries the current value unchanged.
   230      uint256 internal constant BOUNTY_ETH_TARGET = 885_000_000;
   231  
   232      /// @dev Advance reward ratio (2× · mult). The process STAGE rides the advance
   233      ///      bounty (PLACE-02 §6): mintBurnie's advance leg pays `unit · 2 · mult`, scaling
   234      ///      the AdvanceModule's day-epoch stall `mult` (1/2/4/6, AdvanceModule:226-242).
   235      uint256 internal constant ADVANCE_RATIO_NUM = 2;
   236  
   237      /// @dev Open reward pro-rate knee (1× at/above, pro-rated below): a mid-day open of
   238      ///      k < 5 boxes earns `unit · k / 5`, so a single-box open earns 0.2× — below a
   239      ///      one-box tx's gas. This is the in-codebase farm-by-splitting answer (pay for
   240      ///      work done, not once-per-call — the "middle-chunk-unpaid" liveness gap).
   241      uint256 internal constant OPEN_KNEE = 5;
   242  
   243      /// @dev Open-leg default box-count budget (the post-RNG `_subOpenCursor` drain). The per-box
   244      ///      open is uniform O(1) (the afking box rolls boons like a human box). Measured ≈74k/box
   245      ///      (worst box): 80 boxes ≈ 9.15M, under the 10M comfort target and far under the 16.7M
   246      ///      hard ceiling.
   247      uint256 internal constant OPEN_BATCH = 80;
   248  
   249      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
   250                            Subscription entrypoint (CONSENT-01 carried verbatim)
   251      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   252      /// @notice The SINGLE subscription entrypoint — create, replace, or cancel a
   253      ///         daily subscription for `player`. dailyQuantity >= 1 upserts
   254      ///         (create-or-replace in place); dailyQuantity == 0 cancels (writes the
   255      ///         SUB-07 tombstone sentinel, relocating no one). Every mutation flows
   256      ///         through this one consent-gated path.
   257      /// @dev FREEZE-01 rngLock guard: subscribe reverts during the RNG freeze window
   258      ///      (`rngLockedFlag`), for ALL of create / replace / cancel — the subscriber
   259      ///      set must be frozen across [request -> unlock] so the stamped set the open
   260      ///      consumes cannot shift mid-cycle. Callers wait for the unlock.
   261      /// @dev SUB-02 authorization is checked ONCE here, third-party path only:
   262      ///      `player == address(0)` or `player == msg.sender` is self-consent (no
   263      ///      check); otherwise the caller must be a game operator the player
   264      ///      approved (in-context `operatorApprovals[subscriber][msg.sender]` —
   265      ///      the same predicate `isOperatorApproved` returns). Authorization is
   266      ///      NEVER re-checked at process-time.
   267      /// @dev AFSUB-02 pass-gating: subscribe encodes the subscriber's current pass
   268      ///      horizon (in-context `_passHorizonOf(subscriber)`) into
   269      ///      `Sub.validThroughLevel` with a SINGLE read. No BURNIE charge — the
   270      ///      v50.0 pass-gated model. The per-iter process validity check is the
   271      ///      cheap stored-field compare `level <= sub.validThroughLevel`; at the
   272      ///      crossing the pass is re-read EXACTLY ONCE and refresh-or-evicted.
   273      /// @dev msg.value > 0 credits the Game's afkingFunding ledger in-context
   274      ///      (claimablePool moved in tandem — the SOLVENCY-01 invariant), keyed on the
   275      ///      resolved funding bucket (the funder for an operator-funded sub, else the
   276      ///      subscriber).
   277      /// @dev OPEN-E 4-protection (re-attested):
   278      ///        (1) consent-gate-at-subscribe — auth + fundingSource gate checked HERE only;
   279      ///        (2) default-self — `fundingSource == 0` resolves to `subscriber`, no gate;
   280      ///        (3) no-escalation — the source is fixed at subscribe, not changeable per-draw to escalate;
   281      ///        (4) trust-the-sub — a later approval revoke does NOT stop an active sub (re-pointing the source = re-subscribe, which re-checks).
   282      /// @param player Subscriber to act for (0 or msg.sender = self).
   283      /// @param drainGameCreditFirst When true, the buy spends claimable credit first.
   284      /// @param useTickets Mint mode — true = tickets, false = lootboxes.
   285      /// @param dailyQuantity Daily buy units, 1..255 (upsert); 0 cancels (SUB-07 tombstone).
   286      /// @param reinvestPct Claimable reinvest percentage, 0..100.
   287      /// @param fundingSource Wallet whose `afkingFunding` funds this sub; address(0) = self.
   288      ///        A non-zero, non-self source is honored ONLY when it has
   289      ///        operator-approved the subscriber (checked at subscribe ONLY).
   290      function subscribe(
   291          address player,
   292          bool drainGameCreditFirst,
   293          bool useTickets,
   294          uint8 dailyQuantity,
   295          uint8 reinvestPct,
   296          address fundingSource
   297      ) external payable {
   298          // FREEZE-01 — block ALL subscribe (create / replace / cancel) during the
   299          // RNG freeze window: the subscriber set the stamp pass + open consume must
   300          // stay frozen across [request -> unlock]. Callers wait for the unlock.
   301          if (rngLockedFlag) revert RngLocked();
   302          if (reinvestPct > 100) revert InvalidReinvestPct();
   303  
   304          // SUB-02 — self-consent (player == 0 or msg.sender) or operator-approval.
   305          address subscriber = player == address(0) ? msg.sender : player;
   306          if (subscriber != msg.sender) {
   307              if (!operatorApprovals[subscriber][msg.sender]) {
   308                  revert NotApproved();
   309              }
   310          }
   311  
   312          // OPENE-04 — a non-zero, non-self fundingSource must have operator-approved
   313          // the subscriber on the game. address(0) (self) short-circuits the read;
   314          // checked HERE only — the renewal and per-draw paths never re-check.
   315          if (
   316              fundingSource != address(0) &&
   317              fundingSource != subscriber &&
   318              !operatorApprovals[fundingSource][subscriber]
   319          ) {
   320              revert NotApproved();
   321          }
   322  
   323          // msg.value > 0 credits the Game's afkingFunding ledger in-context (A2 —
   324          // the Game holds the ETH; claimablePool moved in tandem so the invariant
   325          // claimablePool == Σ claimableWinnings + Σ afkingFunding holds). It credits the
   326          // SAME bucket the draws debit: the resolved funding source — the non-self
   327          // `fundingSource` for an operator-funded sub (already OPENE-04-approved just
   328          // above, so the funder consented to fund this subscriber), else the subscriber
   329          // itself. So a deposit attached to subscribe always funds the bucket that
   330          // actually pays for this sub's auto-buys — never misdirected to an unused player
   331          // bucket on an operator-funded sub.
   332          if (msg.value > 0) {
   333              address fundDest = (fundingSource != address(0) &&
   334                  fundingSource != subscriber)
   335                  ? fundingSource
   336                  : subscriber;
   337              afkingFunding[fundDest] += msg.value;
   338              claimablePool += uint128(msg.value);
   339          }
   340  
   341          // CANCEL branch — dailyQuantity == 0 writes the `dailyQuantity = 0` tombstone in
   342          // place and relocates no one (the in-pass reclaim swap-pops the tombstone when the
   343          // process stage reaches it). Revert if the caller has no active sub. Any msg.value
   344          // above was still credited to funding, so a cancel-with-ETH never strands the
   345          // deposit (it stays game-side withdrawable).
   346          if (dailyQuantity == 0) {
   347              if (_subscriberIndex[subscriber] == 0) revert NotSubscribed();
   348              Sub storage c = _subOf[subscriber];
   349              // Auto-claim BEFORE clearing: the next advance-driven reclaim deletes the
   350              // slot (wiping both accumulators), so leaving them for a later pull would
   351              // lose them in that race. Pay the sub its own pendingBurnie (CEI: zero
   352              // first), then settle the upline affiliate tree, THEN finalize + tombstone.
   353              uint256 owed = uint256(c.pendingBurnie); // whole BURNIE
   354              if (owed != 0) {
   355                  c.pendingBurnie = 0;
   356                  if (!presaleOver) {
   357                      uint256 credit = (owed * 0.0025 ether) / 100;
   358                      if ((c.flags & FLAG_USE_TICKETS) != 0) credit /= 2;
   359                      presaleBoxCredit[subscriber] += credit;
   360                  }
   361                  coinflip.creditFlip(subscriber, owed * 1 ether);
   362              }
   363              // Drain affiliateBase to the 75/20/5 upline tree (50/50 VAULT/DGNRS if no
   364              // referrer). The affiliate consumes the base via the AFFILIATE-only
   365              // drainAffiliateBase callback, so this must run while the slot still holds it.
   366              address[] memory drainOne = new address[](1);
   367              drainOne[0] = subscriber;
   368              IDegenerusAffiliate(ContractAddresses.AFFILIATE).claim(drainOne);
   369  
   370              // Hand the afking-computed streak back to the manual quest system, then tombstone.
   371              _finalizeAfking(subscriber, c, _simulatedDayIndex());
   372              c.dailyQuantity = 0;
   373              emit SubscriptionUpdated(
   374                  subscriber,
   375                  0,
   376                  (c.flags & FLAG_DRAIN_FIRST) != 0,
   377                  (c.flags & FLAG_USE_TICKETS) != 0,
   378                  c.reinvestPct,
   379                  _fundingSourceOf[subscriber]
   380              );
   381              return;
   382          }
   383  
   384          // UPSERT branch (dailyQuantity >= 1) — create-or-replace in place. `_addToSet`
   385          // is idempotent (adds only when `_subscriberIndex == 0`), so a re-subscribe of
   386          // an active member replaces its fields without set churn.
   387          Sub storage s = _subOf[subscriber];
   388  
   389          // Captured BEFORE the dailyQuantity overwrite: a non-zero stored dailyQuantity means the
   390          // sub is mid-afking-run (afkingActive set) — a re-subscribe CONTINUES that run; 0 means
   391          // new / cancelled / evicted (afkingActive cleared by a prior finalize) — a fresh run.
   392          bool wasActive = s.dailyQuantity != 0;
   393  
   394          s.dailyQuantity = dailyQuantity;
   395          if (drainGameCreditFirst) s.flags |= FLAG_DRAIN_FIRST;
   396          else s.flags &= ~FLAG_DRAIN_FIRST;
   397          if (useTickets) s.flags |= FLAG_USE_TICKETS;
   398          else s.flags &= ~FLAG_USE_TICKETS;
   399          s.reinvestPct = reinvestPct;
   400          // The two protocol self-subscribers (VAULT / sDGNRS) self-subscribe at
   401          // construction with no pass and no funds; they are exempt from the pass-required
   402          // and purchase-grounded gates below, keyed on the un-spoofable resolved subscriber
   403          // identity. Every other sub must clear both gates.
   404          bool exemptSub = subscriber == ContractAddresses.VAULT ||
   405              subscriber == ContractAddresses.SDGNRS;
   406          // Single read; encodes the subscriber's pass horizon (deity sentinel =
   407          // type(uint24).max) into the field the per-iter check and crossing branch compare
   408          // against.
   409          s.validThroughLevel = _passHorizonOf(subscriber);
   410          // Pass-required: the just-stored horizon must reach the current level (the deity
   411          // sentinel type(uint24).max always covers). Reuses the value written above — no
   412          // second pass read. A zero horizon means NO pass and is rejected at every level —
   413          // including level 0, where `< level` (0 < 0) would otherwise be vacuously false and
   414          // let a passless EOA afk through level 0 (a real pass has horizon >= passLevel+99,
   415          // never 0). A pass valid now can still be outgrown later; the per-iter crossing
   416          // eviction handles that.
   417          if (!exemptSub && (s.validThroughLevel == 0 || s.validThroughLevel < level))
   418              revert NoPass();
   419          // Sparse funder map: store only a non-self source; clear on self so re-pointing an
   420          // operator-funded sub back to self does not strand a stale funder. Re-pointing the
   421          // source IS a re-subscribe, which re-runs the operator-approval gate.
   422          if (fundingSource != address(0)) {
   423              _fundingSourceOf[subscriber] = fundingSource;
   424              s.flags |= FLAG_EXTERNAL_FUNDING;
   425          } else {
   426              delete _fundingSourceOf[subscriber];
   427              s.flags &= ~FLAG_EXTERNAL_FUNDING;
   428          }
   429  
   430          // Afking-run start (new sub) OR a streak-refreshing cover-buy (active sub re-subscribe).
   431          {
   432              uint24 today = _simulatedDayIndex();
   433              if (wasActive) {
   434                  // ACTIVE sub re-subscribe — subscribe doubles as a manual "keep my streak alive +
   435                  // buy something" action. Do a funded cover-buy for TODAY (advancing the funded
   436                  // high-water afkCoveredThroughDay), which CONTINUES the run's streak via
   437                  // _deliverAfkingBuy's own gap-resume/accrue: a still-current run keeps its streak
   438                  // and gains today; a gapped run re-bases to 0 (a full missed day is gone, same as
   439                  // the stage). No re-snapshot / no forfeit — the afking streak is never reset by a
   440                  // re-subscribe. Skipped (streak just persists + decays on read) when already
   441                  // bought today OR a pending unopened box exists (re-stamping would orphan it — the
   442                  // no-orphan rule) OR the cover-buy is unfunded.
   443                  if (
   444                      s.lastAutoBoughtDay != uint24(today) &&
   445                      s.lastOpenedDay >= s.lastAutoBoughtDay
   446                  ) {
   447                      uint256 mp = _mintPriceInContext();
   448                      (
   449                          ,
   450                          uint256 ethValue,
   451                          uint256 buyAmount,
   452                          bool isTicket,
   453                          uint256 playerFunding,
   454                          uint256 claimableUse
   455                      ) = _resolveBuy(s, subscriber, mp);
   456                      address src = (s.flags & FLAG_EXTERNAL_FUNDING) != 0
   457                          ? _fundingSourceOf[subscriber]
   458                          : subscriber;
   459                      if (
   460                          (src == subscriber ? playerFunding : afkingFunding[src]) >=
   461                          ethValue
   462                      ) {
   463                          _deliverAfkingBuy(
   464                              subscriber,
   465                              s,
   466                              today,
   467                              mp,
   468                              level,
   469                              src,
   470                              ethValue,
   471                              claimableUse,
   472                              buyAmount,
   473                              isTicket,
   474                              true
   475                          );
   476                      }
   477                  }
   478              } else {
   479                  // NEW run. Snapshot the player's (gap-synced) manual quest streak and flip the
   480                  // afking flag (slot-0 completions become streak-neutral / reward-deferred — the
   481                  // Game-side compute-on-read owns the streak until finalize hands it back). The run
   482                  // is grounded on a FUNDED day-0 (a funded min-buy OR an already-complete manual
   483                  // slot-0 today) — the debit-gate that makes the streak unfarmable. An unfunded
   484                  // start reverts (MustPurchaseToBeginAfking); only VAULT / SDGNRS, which
   485                  // self-subscribe with no funds at construction, forfeit the snapshot (base 0)
   486                  // instead.
   487                  uint256 snap = quests.beginAfking(subscriber, today); // syncs + sets afkingActive
   488                  // Frame the run on today (the compute-on-read base; afkCovered == today keeps the
   489                  // delivery's gap-reset from wiping the snapshot and guarantees
   490                  // afkCovered >= afkingStartDay so the streak span never underflows).
   491                  s.afkCoveredThroughDay = uint24(today);
   492                  s.afkingStartDay = uint24(today);
   493  
   494                  (, , , bool[2] memory done) = questView.playerQuestStates(subscriber);
   495                  if (done[0]) {
   496                      _setStreakBase(s, snap); // funded (manual) day-0 — keep the snapshot
   497                      s.lastAutoBoughtDay = uint24(today);
   498                      s.lastOpenedDay = uint24(today); // no pending box
   499                  } else if (s.lastAutoBoughtDay == uint24(today)) {
   500                      // Already bought today in a prior subscribe cycle this day — the cancel
   501                      // tombstone retained the stamp across the unsub/re-subscribe. The run is
   502                      // already purchase-grounded, so keep the snapshot and skip a second
   503                      // cover-buy: the per-day flat slot-0 reward is not re-accrued, and
   504                      // lastOpenedDay is left untouched so a pending box is not orphaned. This
   505                      // mirrors the active-sub re-subscribe guard above.
   506                      _setStreakBase(s, snap);
   507                  } else {
   508                      uint256 mp = _mintPriceInContext();
   509                      (
   510                          ,
   511                          uint256 ethValue,
   512                          uint256 buyAmount,
   513                          bool isTicket,
   514                          uint256 playerFunding,
   515                          uint256 claimableUse
   516                      ) = _resolveBuy(s, subscriber, mp);
   517                      address src = (s.flags & FLAG_EXTERNAL_FUNDING) != 0
   518                          ? _fundingSourceOf[subscriber]
   519                          : subscriber;
   520                      if (
   521                          (src == subscriber ? playerFunding : afkingFunding[src]) >=
   522                          ethValue
   523                      ) {
   524                          _setStreakBase(s, snap); // funded day-0 — keep the snapshot
   525                          _deliverAfkingBuy(
   526                              subscriber,
   527                              s,
   528                              today,
   529                              mp,
   530                              level,
   531                              src,
   532                              ethValue,
   533                              claimableUse,
   534                              buyAmount,
   535                              isTicket,
   536                              true
   537                          );
   538                      } else if (exemptSub) {
   539                          // VAULT / sDGNRS bootstrap: unfunded at construction — forfeit the
   540                          // snapshot and start the run from base 0 without reverting.
   541                          _setStreakBase(s, 0);
   542                      } else {
   543                          // A NEW run must be grounded on a real purchase: already bought
   544                          // today (the done[0] branch above) or a funded in-tx cover-buy (the
   545                          // branch above). An unfunded start would free-ride the advance gate.
   546                          revert MustPurchaseToBeginAfking();
   547                      }
   548                  }
   549              }
   550          }
   551  
   552          _addToSet(subscriber);
   553          emit SubscriptionUpdated(
   554              subscriber,
   555              dailyQuantity,
   556              drainGameCreditFirst,
   557              useTickets,
   558              reinvestPct,
   559              fundingSource
   560          );
   561      }
   562  
   563      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
   564                            In-context views (CONSENT-01)
   565      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   566      /// @dev In-context pass-horizon read (the AFSUB pass-gating producer, D-11).
   567      ///      Mirrors the Game's `lazyPassHorizon` (:1582) so the
   568      ///      subscribe-time write + the process-pass crossing re-read share the exact
   569      ///      horizon semantics: deity holders return the type(uint24).max sentinel;
   570      ///      everyone else returns their frozenUntilLevel. Single definition (one
   571      ///      canonical horizon read), called at subscribe + the crossing branch.
   572      function _passHorizonOf(address player) internal view returns (uint24) {
   573          uint256 packed = mintPacked_[player];
   574          if (packed >> BitPackingLib.HAS_DEITY_PASS_SHIFT & 1 != 0) {
   575              return type(uint24).max;
   576          }
   577          return
   578              uint24(
   579                  (packed >> BitPackingLib.FROZEN_UNTIL_LEVEL_SHIFT) &
   580                      BitPackingLib.MASK_24
   581              );
   582      }
   583  
   584      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
   585                            Iterable set (hand-inlined OZ EnumerableSet)
   586      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   587      /// @dev Iterable set insert. Idempotent on already-in-set. 1-indexed
   588      ///      `_subscriberIndex` (0 = not in set). Reverts a NEW insert at
   589      ///      SUBSCRIBER_CAP (500 active subs) — the protocol caps the set it pays to
   590      ///      iterate each cycle. A re-subscribe of an existing member is
   591      ///      already-in-set (no growth) so it never trips the cap.
   592      function _addToSet(address player) internal {
   593          if (_subscriberIndex[player] == 0) {
   594              // Cap the NEW-subscriber path only: bound the active set the advance
   595              // chain walks (SUBSCRIBER_CAP = 500) so the per-cycle work stays cheap.
   596              if (_subscribers.length >= SUBSCRIBER_CAP) {
   597                  revert SubscriberCapReached();
   598              }
   599              _subscribers.push(player);
   600              _subscriberIndex[player] = _subscribers.length;
   601          }
   602      }
   603  
   604      /// @dev Iterable set remove via swap-and-pop. Idempotent on not-in-set.
   605      ///      1-indexed: move the last element into the vacated slot (and update its
   606      ///      index), pop the tail, clear the removed player's index. The process
   607      ///      pass's "no cursor-advance after swap-pop" pattern (CONSENT-02 —
   608      ///      H-CANCEL-SWAP-MISS) enforces iteration safety; this helper is itself
   609      ///      iteration-safe (membership ⟺ packed-index != 0 preserved).
   610      function _removeFromSet(address player) internal {
   611          uint256 idxPlus1 = _subscriberIndex[player];
   612          if (idxPlus1 == 0) return; // not in set — silent no-op
   613          uint256 idx = idxPlus1 - 1;
   614          uint256 last = _subscribers.length - 1;
   615          if (idx != last) {
   616              address mover = _subscribers[last];
   617              _subscribers[idx] = mover;
   618              _subscriberIndex[mover] = idxPlus1; // mover takes the vacated 1-indexed slot
   619          }
   620          _subscribers.pop();
   621          delete _subscriberIndex[player];
   622      }
   623  
   624      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
   625                    The _resolveBuy slice builder (REVERT-01)
   626      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   627      /// @dev Per-player funding resolution for the process pass — SUB-04 effective
   628      ///      quantity → cost → purchase mode + funding split, carrying the slice-builder
   629      ///      validation invariants that make a funded buy revert-free BY CONSTRUCTION (REVERT-01,
   630      ///      the SOLE no-brick guarantor under the D-348-04 no-valve model). The five
   631      ///      obligation-1 invariants (348-INVARIANT-CARRY §1, /contract-auditor PASS §5):
   632      ///        (1) effectiveQty = max(dailyQuantity, reinvestQty) ≥ 1 (dailyQuantity ≥ 1
   633      ///            is the subscribe-time floor) → never the Game's totalCost==0 / dust /
   634      ///            TICKET_MIN reverts;
   635      ///        (2) cost = mintPrice * effectiveQty → the exact cost the Game recomputes;
   636      ///        (3) cost ≥ mintPrice ≥ 0.01 ETH (the priceForLevel floor) → a lootbox amount
   637      ///            always meets any min-spend floor; no skip/decline needed;
   638      ///        (4) 1-wei claimable sentinel → leaves claimable > cost / basis > shortfall →
   639      ///            never Game:976 (Claimable claimable<=amount) nor Storage:843 (settle);
   640      ///        (5) ev = cost - claimableUse with claimableUse ∈ [0, cost], enum-typed
   641      ///            payKind ∈ {Claimable, DirectEth, Combined} → never Game:985/1003/1006
   642      ///            nor an out-of-range MintPaymentKind enum-cast Panic 0x21.
   643      ///      ⚠ Dual TICKET_SCALE (§3-i, LOAD-BEARING): the ticket entry-unit `amount`
   644      ///      uses `AFKING_TICKET_SCALE = 400`; the Game's `/ (4 * 100)` recompute uses the
   645      ///      inherited Storage `TICKET_SCALE = 100` — the two constants are NOT collapsed,
   646      ///      so `cost` stays `mintPrice * effectiveQty`.
   647      ///      ⚠ NO error-swallowing valve (REVERT-02 no-valve): a funded slice is revert-free
   648      ///      by construction, with no pre-emptive decline and no reactive error-trap; the
   649      ///      per-cycle eviction cap is DROPPED.
   650      ///      In-context: `claimable` is the swept-gated raw `claimableWinnings[player]`
   651      ///      (== afkingSnapshot's claimable / claimableWinningsOf, incl. the 1-wei sentinel)
   652      ///      and `playerFunding` is the raw `afkingFunding[player]` (== afkingFundingOf,
   653      ///      D-MR-01), read as in-context SLOADs. View — no state writes.
   654      /// @return payKind Payment mode (DirectEth / Claimable / Combined) for the slice.
   655      /// @return ethValue Fresh-ETH portion debited from the funder's afkingFunding (0 = pure claimable).
   656      /// @return amount Ticket entry-units (isTicket) or lootbox spend in wei (!isTicket).
   657      /// @return isTicket True = buy `amount` ticket entry-units; false = buy an `amount`-wei lootbox.
   658      /// @return playerFunding The player's afkingFunding (the common-path funding-skip source; D-MR-01).
   659      /// @return claimableUse Claimable portion of `cost` (reinvest / drainFirst); cost == ethValue + claimableUse.
   660      function _resolveBuy(
   661          Sub storage sub,
   662          address player,
   663          uint256 mp
   664      )
   665          internal
   666          view
   667          returns (
   668              MintPaymentKind payKind,
   669              uint256 ethValue,
   670              uint256 amount,
   671              bool isTicket,
   672              uint256 playerFunding,
   673              uint256 claimableUse
   674          )
   675      {
   676          bool drainFirst = (sub.flags & FLAG_DRAIN_FIRST) != 0;
   677          // ONE in-context read pair: the player's
   678          // claimable (reinvest / drainFirst funding split) AND afkingFunding (the
   679          // common-path funding-skip source — D-MR-01; the src != player OPEN-E slice
   680          // reads afkingFunding[src] separately at the call site). Swept-gated to mirror
   681          // afkingSnapshot / claimableWinningsOf exactly.
   682          uint256 claimable = _goRead(GO_SWEPT_SHIFT, GO_SWEPT_MASK) != 0
   683              ? 0
   684              : claimableWinnings[player];
   685          playerFunding = afkingFunding[player];
   686  
   687          // Total quantity = max(dailyQuantity, reinvestPct% of claimable / price).
   688          uint256 effectiveQty = sub.dailyQuantity;
   689          if (sub.reinvestPct > 0) {
   690              uint256 reinvestQty = (claimable * sub.reinvestPct) / 100 / mp;
   691              if (reinvestQty > effectiveQty) effectiveQty = reinvestQty;
   692          }
   693          uint256 cost = mp * effectiveQty;
   694  
   695          // Mode routing. Ticket mode buys `effectiveQty` whole tickets (entry-units =
   696          // effectiveQty * AFKING_TICKET_SCALE [= 400]); lootbox mode buys a `cost`-wei box.
   697          isTicket = (sub.flags & FLAG_USE_TICKETS) != 0;
   698          amount = isTicket ? effectiveQty * AFKING_TICKET_SCALE : cost;
   699  
   700          // Funding split (USER model): reinvestPct always spends that % of claimable;
   701          // drainFirst is a superset (claimable-first up to cost). The afkingFunding pool
   702          // funds the remainder. Never spend the entire claimable balance — leave >= 1 wei
   703          // (the GAME's Claimable branch needs claimable strictly > cost, and the claimable
   704          // shortfall settle needs basis > shortfall).
   705          uint256 reinvestSpend = sub.reinvestPct > 0
   706              ? (claimable * sub.reinvestPct) / 100
   707              : 0;
   708          if (reinvestSpend > cost) reinvestSpend = cost;
   709          claimableUse = drainFirst
   710              ? (claimable < cost ? claimable : cost)
   711              : reinvestSpend;
   712          if (claimable > 0 && claimableUse >= claimable) claimableUse = claimable - 1;
   713          ethValue = cost - claimableUse;
   714          payKind = ethValue == 0
   715              ? MintPaymentKind.Claimable
   716              : (claimableUse == 0 ? MintPaymentKind.DirectEth : MintPaymentKind.Combined);
   717      }
   718  
   719      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
   720                Shared per-sub funded delivery + compute-on-read streak
   721      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
   722      /// @dev The shared per-sub funded delivery — used by both the process STAGE (after its
   723      ///      pre-buy gates, `coverBuy == false`) and the subscribe-time grounding cover-buy
   724      ///      (`coverBuy == true`). The slice is already confirmed funded by the caller
   725      ///      (`afkingFunding[src] >= ethValue`), so this is revert-free by construction (no
   726      ///      try/catch). Debits the fresh-ETH leg + the reinvest claimable leg (claimablePool in
   727      ///      tandem, fail-loud on underflow — a debit can never exceed afkingFunding[src] ≤ the
   728      ///      claimablePool reservation, so a revert here means solvency is already violated and
   729      ///      must propagate), materializes the buy per mode, accrues the day's affiliate base + the
   730      ///      slot-0 pendingBurnie reward, advances the compute-on-read streak markers (gap-resuming
   731      ///      a fresh run from zero if the last funded day is older than yesterday), and sets the
   732      ///      success marker. The frozen activity score reads the COMPUTE-ON-READ streak off the Sub
   733      ///      slot — no DegenerusQuests STATICCALL on the hot path. boons OFF ⇒ amount == spend.
   734      ///
   735      ///      Lootbox materialization differs by mode: the daily STAGE writes a gas-light warm
   736      ///      Sub-stamp box (the EV-cap RMW deferred to OPEN), whereas the cover-buy writes a full
   737      ///      INDEXED box resolved off `lootboxRngWordByIndex` — a future word never knowable at
   738      ///      subscribe — so a player-timed subscribe cannot select a pre-revealed seed (a
   739      ///      `rngWordByDay`-keyed Sub-stamp box would break the RNG-freeze invariant here, since
   740      ///      subscribe runs after the day's word is public). Pool routing also differs: the STAGE
   741      ///      accrues the cost into the caller's batched per-chunk credit; the cover-buy (a single
   742      ///      buy) routes inline here.
   743      /// @param player The subscriber being delivered to (the credit recipient).
   744      /// @param sub The subscriber's record (storage ref — stamped/accrued here).
   745      /// @param processDay The delivered day (the stamp's frozen seed day + the streak marker).
   746      /// @param mp The in-context mint price.
   747      /// @param currentLevel The hoisted level (the buy's target-level base).
   748      /// @param src The funding bucket the fresh-ETH leg debits.
   749      /// @param ethValue The fresh-ETH portion (0 = pure claimable).
   750      /// @param claimableUse The reinvest/drainFirst claimable portion of the cost.
   751      /// @param amount Ticket entry-units (ticket mode) or lootbox spend in wei (lootbox mode).
   752      /// @param isTicket Mode — true = queue tickets, false = a lootbox box.
   753      /// @param coverBuy True = subscribe-time grounding buy (indexed box + inline pool routing);
   754      ///        false = daily STAGE buy (Sub-stamp box + caller-batched pool routing).
   755      function _deliverAfkingBuy(
   756          address player,
   757          Sub storage sub,
   758          uint24 processDay,
   759          uint256 mp,
   760          uint24 currentLevel,
   761          address src,
   762          uint256 ethValue,
   763          uint256 claimableUse,
   764          uint256 amount,
   765          bool isTicket,
   766          bool coverBuy
   767      ) private {
   768          if (ethValue != 0) {
   769              afkingFunding[src] -= ethValue;
   770              claimablePool -= uint128(ethValue);
   771          }
   772          // Reinvest/drainFirst claimable portion of the cost. The _resolveBuy 1-wei sentinel
   773          // guarantees claimableUse <= claimable - 1, so this never underflows. claimableWinnings
   774          // rides in claimablePool, so the pool moves in tandem (the SOLVENCY-01 invariant).
   775          if (claimableUse != 0) {
   776              claimableWinnings[player] -= claimableUse;
   777              claimablePool -= uint128(claimableUse);
   778          }
   779  
   780          if (isTicket) {
   781              // Ticket minimal-write primitive: queue resolution-equivalent ticket entries and
   782              // accrue the ticket buyer-bonus into the warm Sub slot. The affiliate flat-7% and the
   783              // slot-0 reward are added by the mode-agnostic accrue below (not re-accrued here).
   784              uint24 targetLevel = jackpotPhaseFlag
   785                  ? currentLevel
   786                  : currentLevel + 1;
   787  
   788              // Century (x00-level) quantity bonus at parity with the manual mint, reusing the
   789              // per-player centuryBonusUsed storage and the per-buy activity score
   790              // off the COMPUTE-ON-READ streak (no STATICCALL). The purchase-boost quantity
   791              // multiplier is omitted, matching the boons-off lootbox leg.
   792              uint32 adjustedQty = uint32(amount);
   793              if (targetLevel % 100 == 0) {
   794                  uint256 cachedScore = _playerActivityScore(
   795                      player,
   796                      _afkingStreak(sub, processDay),
   797                      targetLevel
   798                  );
   799                  if (cachedScore != 0) {
   800                      uint256 priceWei = PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(targetLevel);
   801                      uint256 _score = cachedScore > 30_500 ? 30_500 : cachedScore;
   802                      uint256 bonusQty = (uint256(adjustedQty) * _score) / 30_500;
   803                      if (bonusQty != 0 && priceWei != 0) {
   804                          uint256 maxBonus = (20 ether) / (priceWei >> 2);
   805                          uint256 used = _centuryUsedFor(player, targetLevel);
   806                          uint256 remaining = maxBonus > used ? maxBonus - used : 0;
   807                          if (bonusQty > remaining) bonusQty = remaining;
   808                          if (bonusQty != 0) {
   809                              _setCenturyUsedFor(player, targetLevel, used + bonusQty);
   810                              adjustedQty += uint32(bonusQty);
   811                          }
   812                      }
   813                  }
   814              }
   815  
   816              _queueTicketsScaled(player, targetLevel, adjustedQty, false);
   817  
   818              // 10%/20% ticket buyer-bonus → claimable pendingBurnie (pulled via
   819              // claimAfkingBurnie). Uses the pre-bonus `amount`; whole BURNIE with the 100M clamp.
   820              uint256 coinCost = (amount * (PRICE_COIN_UNIT / 4)) / TICKET_SCALE;
   821              uint256 bonusBase = coinCost / 10; // flat 10%
   822              if (amount >= 10 * 4 * TICKET_SCALE) {
   823                  bonusBase += (amount * PRICE_COIN_UNIT) / (40 * TICKET_SCALE); // +10% → 20% on ≥10 tickets
   824              }
   825              uint256 bonusWhole = bonusBase / 1 ether;
   826              if (bonusWhole != 0) {
   827                  uint256 newOwed = uint256(sub.pendingBurnie) + bonusWhole;
   828                  if (newOwed > 100_000_000) newOwed = 100_000_000;
   829                  sub.pendingBurnie = uint32(newOwed);
   830              }
   831  
   832              // No pending box: keep lastOpenedDay == lastAutoBoughtDay so the no-orphan guard and
   833              // _afkingBoxReady never treat a ticket sub as box-pending.
   834              sub.lastOpenedDay = uint24(processDay);
   835          } else {
   836              // Lootbox box. The per-buy manual side-effects (handlePurchase, affiliate ×2, the
   837              // per-buy creditFlip) are deferred to the in-slot accrue (affiliate pulled via
   838              // drainAffiliateBase; the slot-0 reward into pendingBurnie). The frozen scorePlus1
   839              // (the EV input at open, off the compute-on-read streak — no STATICCALL) is computed
   840              // once for either box shape.
   841              uint256 activityScore = _playerActivityScore(
   842                  player,
   843                  _afkingStreak(sub, processDay),
   844                  currentLevel + 1
   845              );
   846              uint16 scorePlus1 = activityScore + 1 > type(uint16).max
   847                  ? type(uint16).max
   848                  : uint16(activityScore + 1);
   849              if (coverBuy) {
   850                  // Subscribe-time grounding box: a full INDEXED box on the live lootbox index,
   851                  // resolved off lootboxRngWordByIndex (a future word). Rides the auto-open queue,
   852                  // so the markers go box-clean (lastOpenedDay == lastAutoBoughtDay) and the
   853                  // no-orphan guard never trips on a freshly-subscribed sub.
   854                  _recordAfkingCoverBox(
   855                      player,
   856                      currentLevel,
   857                      amount,
   858                      scorePlus1,
   859                      activityScore
   860                  );
   861                  sub.lastOpenedDay = uint24(processDay);
   862              } else {
   863                  // Daily STAGE Sub-stamp box: the warm Sub slot IS the box record (no cold
   864                  // ledger); the EV-cap RMW is deferred to OPEN, fed this frozen scorePlus1, and
   865                  // the level + EV-cap key read LIVE at open. milli-ETH stamp (the EV/seed input
   866                  // only — the ETH debit used the full wei ethValue).
   867                  sub.scorePlus1 = scorePlus1;
   868                  sub.amount = uint24(_packEthToMilliEth(amount));
   869              }
   870          }
   871  
   872          // Mode-agnostic accrue — one warm in-slot write, zero cross-contract calls:
   873          //   • affiliate base: flat 7% of the full ETH spend (== amount), whole BURNIE, 100M clamp;
   874          //   • slot-0 quest reward: QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD (whole BURNIE) into the claimable pendingBurnie;
   875          //   • compute-on-read streak markers: gap-resume a fresh run from zero if the last funded
   876          //     day is older than yesterday (matching the decay-on-read), then advance the
   877          //     funded-day high-water mark afkCoveredThroughDay.
   878          {
   879              uint256 base = (_ethToBurnie(amount, mp) * 7) / 100;
   880              if (base != 0) {
   881                  uint256 newBase = uint256(sub.affiliateBase) + base;
   882                  if (newBase > 100_000_000) newBase = 100_000_000;
   883                  sub.affiliateBase = uint32(newBase);
   884              }
   885              {
   886                  uint256 newOwed = uint256(sub.pendingBurnie) +
   887                      (QUEST_SLOT0_REWARD / 1 ether);
   888                  if (newOwed > 100_000_000) newOwed = 100_000_000;
   889                  sub.pendingBurnie = uint32(newOwed);
   890              }
   891              if (sub.afkCoveredThroughDay + 1 < processDay) {
   892                  sub.afkingStartDay = uint24(processDay);
   893                  _setStreakBase(sub, 0);
   894              }
   895              sub.afkCoveredThroughDay = uint24(processDay);
   896          }
   897  
   898          sub.lastAutoBoughtDay = uint24(processDay);
   899  
   900          // The cover-buy is a single buy (not part of a STAGE chunk), so it credits the prize
   901          // pools inline here — a box spend funds the box pool, a ticket spend the ticket pool. The
   902          // STAGE path instead defers this to the caller's batched per-chunk `_routeAfkingPoolEth`.
   903          if (coverBuy) {
   904              uint256 cost = ethValue + claimableUse;
   905              if (isTicket) _routeAfkingPoolEth(0, cost);
   906              else _routeAfkingPoolEth(cost, 0);
   907          }
   908      }
   909  
   910      /// @dev Write a subscribe-time grounding lootbox as a full INDEXED box on the live lootbox
   911      ///      index — the cover-buy's freeze-safe box record, mirroring the manual
   912      ///      `_recordLootboxEntry` minus the boons-off legs (no boost, no distress tally, no
   913      ///      mint-day record). The box binds to `lootboxRngWordByIndex[index]` — a future word
   914      ///      written at the next advance, never knowable at subscribe — and rolls from the LIVE
   915      ///      open level, so the stored day and purchase-level are pure seed labels (the day-1
   916      ///      genesis box resolves on its index word at the first advance, unlike `rngWordByDay[1]`,
   917      ///      which is never written, so a genesis lootbox sub is never bricked). First deposit
   918      ///      enqueues the index for the permissionless auto-open cursor and runs the purchase-time
   919      ///      EV-cap tally (a bonus box draws `add = min(spend, CAP - used)` from the shared
   920      ///      per-(player, level) accumulator, freezing the adjustedPortion into the packed word); a
   921      ///      subsequent deposit at the same un-advanced index accumulates onto it with the
   922      ///      multiplier frozen from the first-deposit score. The EV-cap key is `currentLevel + 1`
   923      ///      (== the resolver's open level = level + 1).
   924      /// @param player The box recipient.
   925      /// @param currentLevel The live game level (== the STAGE's hoisted currentLevel).
   926      /// @param amount The lootbox spend in wei (boons off ⇒ no boost; amount == spend).
   927      /// @param scorePlus1 The frozen activity-score+1 EV input (first deposit only).
   928      /// @param activityScore The raw activity score backing scorePlus1 (first-deposit EV mult).
   929      function _recordAfkingCoverBox(
   930          address player,
   931          uint24 currentLevel,
   932          uint256 amount,
   933          uint16 scorePlus1,
   934          uint256 activityScore
   935      ) private {
   936          uint48 index = uint48(_lrRead(LR_INDEX_SHIFT, LR_INDEX_MASK));
   937          uint24 capKey = currentLevel + 1; // resolver open level == the per-(player, level) cap key
   938          uint256 existingAmount = lootboxEth[index][player] & ((1 << 232) - 1);
   939  
   940          if (existingAmount == 0) {
   941              uint64 adj;
   942              if (
   943                  _lootboxEvMultiplierFromScore(activityScore) >
   944                  LOOTBOX_EV_NEUTRAL_BPS
   945              ) {
   946                  uint256 used = lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[player][capKey];
   947                  uint256 remaining = used >= LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP
   948                      ? 0
   949                      : LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP - used;
   950                  uint256 add = amount < remaining ? amount : remaining;
   951                  lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[player][capKey] = used + add;
   952                  adj = uint64(add);
   953              }
   954              lootboxPurchasePacked[index][player] = _packLootboxPurchase(
   955                  scorePlus1,
   956                  adj,
   957                  capKey // baseLevel+1: vestigial post-grace-removal (openLootBox drops it)
   958              );
   959              // First deposit for this (index, player): enqueue for the permissionless auto-open
   960              // cursor (the consumer gates each index on lootboxRngWordByIndex != 0, so this is
   961              // producer-only). The box is discovered via that cursor walk, not an event.
   962              IGameRouter(address(this)).enqueueBoxForAutoOpen(index, player);
   963          } else if (amount != 0) {
   964              // Subsequent deposit at the same un-advanced index (only reachable in the
   965              // pre-first-advance genesis window): accumulate the EV-cap with the multiplier
   966              // FROZEN from the first-deposit score read back from the packed word.
   967              (uint16 sp1, uint64 adj0, uint24 blp1) = _unpackLootboxPurchase(
   968                  lootboxPurchasePacked[index][player]
   969              );
   970              if (
   971                  _lootboxEvMultiplierFromScore(uint256(sp1 - 1)) >
   972                  LOOTBOX_EV_NEUTRAL_BPS
   973              ) {
   974                  uint256 used = lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[player][capKey];
   975                  uint256 remaining = used >= LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP
   976                      ? 0
   977                      : LOOTBOX_EV_BENEFIT_CAP - used;
   978                  uint256 add = amount < remaining ? amount : remaining;
   979                  if (add != 0) {
   980                      lootboxEvBenefitUsedByLevel[player][capKey] = used + add;
   981                      lootboxPurchasePacked[index][player] = _packLootboxPurchase(
   982                          sp1,
   983                          adj0 + uint64(add),
   984                          blp1
   985                      );
   986                  }
   987              }
   988          }
   989  
   990          uint256 existingBase = lootboxEthBase[index][player];
   991          if (existingAmount != 0 && existingBase == 0) {
   992              existingBase = existingAmount;
   993          }
   994          lootboxEthBase[index][player] = existingBase + amount;
   995          // purchaseLevel (high 24 bits) is vestigial post-grace-removal — openLootBox rolls from
   996          // the LIVE level. boons OFF ⇒ no boost, so the stored amount is the raw spend.
   997          lootboxEth[index][player] =
   998              (uint256(capKey) << 232) |
   999              (existingAmount + amount);
  1000          _lrWrite(
  1001              LR_PENDING_ETH_SHIFT,
  1002              LR_PENDING_ETH_MASK,
  1003              _lrRead(LR_PENDING_ETH_SHIFT, LR_PENDING_ETH_MASK) +
  1004                  _packEthToMilliEth(amount)
  1005          );
  1006  
  1007          // One box-buy event across paths (same topic as the mint + whale LootBoxBuy).
  1008          emit LootBoxBuy(
  1009              player,
  1010              index,
  1011              amount,
  1012              _psRead(PS_ACTIVE_SHIFT, PS_ACTIVE_MASK) != 0
  1013          );
  1014      }
  1015  
  1016      /// @dev Compute-on-read effective afking quest streak from the Sub slot — no DegenerusQuests
  1017      ///      STATICCALL. The run's snapshot (`streakAtAfkingStart`) plus the funded delivered days
  1018      ///      since the run's base day, while the last funded day is no older than yesterday;
  1019      ///      otherwise 0 (decay-on-read: miss one full day and the streak is gone). Capped to 100
  1020      ///      downstream by the activity score.
  1021      function _afkingStreak(Sub storage sub, uint24 currentDay)
  1022          private
  1023          view
  1024          returns (uint32)
  1025      {
  1026          uint24 covered = sub.afkCoveredThroughDay;
  1027          if (currentDay == 0 || covered + 1 < currentDay) return 0;
  1028          return uint32(_streakBaseOf(sub)) + uint32(covered - sub.afkingStartDay);
  1029      }
  1030  
  1031      /// @dev Hand the afking-computed streak back to the manual quest system on a sub-ending path,
  1032      ///      BEFORE the Sub slot is deleted. Computes the run's earned streak (snapshot + funded
  1033      ///      delivered days) and the afking funded high-water day, then defers the decay decision
  1034      ///      and the anchor to `quests.finalizeAfking`, which also folds in any manual completion
  1035      ///      day (so a sub who let afking funding lapse but kept minting manually is not wrongly
  1036      ///      zeroed) and is idempotent (a no-op if the player is not currently afking — safe for the
  1037      ///      cancel-then-reclaim double call). Clears the Sub's afking framing. The cross-contract
  1038      ///      read+write is the heavier (EVICT_WEIGHT) STAGE branch.
  1039      /// @param player The subscriber whose run is ending.
  1040      /// @param sub The subscriber's record (storage ref — afking framing cleared here).
  1041      /// @param currentDay The current day (the decay reference passed to DegenerusQuests).
  1042      function _finalizeAfking(
  1043          address player,
  1044          Sub storage sub,
  1045          uint24 currentDay
  1046      ) private {
  1047          uint24 covered = sub.afkCoveredThroughDay;
  1048          uint256 earned = uint256(_streakBaseOf(sub)) +
  1049              (covered - sub.afkingStartDay);
  1050          quests.finalizeAfking(
  1051              player,
  1052              earned > type(uint24).max ? type(uint24).max : uint24(earned),
  1053              covered,
  1054              currentDay
  1055          );
  1056          sub.afkingStartDay = 0;
  1057          _setStreakBase(sub, 0);
  1058      }
  1059  
  1060      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
  1061                The REQUIRED-PATH process STAGE (BOX-02 stamp + BOX-03 debit + CONSENT-02)
  1062      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
  1063      /// @notice The chunked pre-RNG stamp/buy pass the AdvanceModule STAGE drives across
  1064      ///         the subscriber set, immediately before `rngGate` on the new-day path
  1065      ///         (D-348-01 required-path; 349.1-04 owns the AdvanceModule insertion). A
  1066      ///         NO-ORPHAN guard (§3) runs FIRST per sub: a sub with a pending unopened box
  1067      ///         (`lastOpenedDay < lastAutoBoughtDay`) is left ENTIRELY untouched this cycle
  1068      ///         (no reclaim / evict / funding-kill / re-stamp), so its paid-for box is never
  1069      ///         orphaned. For each funded, well-formed sub it then builds the `_resolveBuy`
  1070      ///         slice (REVERT-01) and, per mode (P2): a LOOTBOX sub STAMPS the two
  1071      ///         genuinely-per-sub box inputs (`scorePlus1`, `amount`) warm-dirty into the
  1072      ///         single-slot Sub record (BOX-02) — the box is materialized LATER by the open
  1073      ///         leg at the LIVE level (349.1-03); a TICKET sub QUEUES whole tickets NOW via
  1074      ///         the MintModule `purchaseWith` path (no box). Both modes debit
  1075      ///         `afkingFunding[src]` then set the `lastAutoBoughtDay` success-marker AFTER
  1076      ///         the debit (BOX-03; it also doubles as the lootbox seed `day`), and carry the
  1077      ///         CONSENT-02 set-mutation semantics (no cursor advance after swap-pop).
  1078      /// @dev FREEZE-02b: the STAGE runs strictly pre-RNG (before `rngGate`), so the day-D
  1079      ///      word `rngWordByDay[processDay]` is uncommitted at stamp — the freeze property
  1080      ///      (349.1-DESIGN §2). The lootbox open sources its word from
  1081      ///      `rngWordByDay[lastAutoBoughtDay]` and rolls the level LIVE at open; there is no
  1082      ///      stored per-day epoch. The boundary-pinned `processDay` is computed once by the
  1083      ///      STAGE and passed in (it is the stamped `lastAutoBoughtDay`, the frozen seed
  1084      ///      `day`, FREEZE-03; never open-time `_simulatedDayIndex()`).
  1085      /// @dev BOX-02 stamp-only (lootbox mode): this pass writes NO cold box-ledger entry —
  1086      ///      the warm Sub stamp is the box record (no cold ledger). boons OFF ⇒ `amount` = spend.
  1087      /// @dev DOUBLE-DRAW GUARD (EVCAP-01 producer): the lootbox path STAMPS only — the
  1088      ///      single EV-cap RMW happens at OPEN, fed the FROZEN `evMultiplierBps`
  1089      ///      derived from the stamped `scorePlus1`. The ticket path defers all EV to the
  1090      ///      MintModule buy (it computes the ticket's own activity score on the buy path).
  1091      /// @dev NO error-swallowing valve (REVERT-02 no-valve, D-348-04): a funded slice is
  1092      ///      revert-free by construction (REVERT-01); there is no pre-emptive lootbox skip;
  1093      ///      rule-(1) unfunded eviction is a separate pre-buy decision
  1094      ///      (a NORMAL sub is auto-paused via swap-pop; VAULT/SDGNRS are EXEMPT by pinned
  1095      ///      identity); the SOLVENCY-01 `claimablePool -=` site FAILS LOUD (class B, must
  1096      ///      propagate). The per-cycle eviction cap is DROPPED.
  1097      /// @param processDay The boundary-pinned process day (computed once by the STAGE).
  1098      /// @param weightBudget Per-call gas-weight budget (caller-bounded — the anti-gas-DoS
  1099      ///        property). Each iteration consumes weight — a cheap local buy/skip 1, a
  1100      ///        cross-contract sub-ending finalize `SUB_STAGE_EVICT_WEIGHT` — and the chunk ends
  1101      ///        when the accumulated weight reaches the budget, bounding even an all-evicts chunk.
  1102      /// @return processed Number of set entries advanced/handled this chunk.
  1103      function processSubscriberStage(
  1104          uint24 processDay,
  1105          uint256 weightBudget
  1106      ) external returns (uint256 processed) {
  1107          uint256 mp = _mintPriceInContext();
  1108          // AFSUB-02 — hoist the level read ONCE so the per-iter validity check is a pure
  1109          // stored-field compare (no SLOAD on the non-crossing path). GASOPT-05 preserved.
  1110          uint24 currentLevel = level;
  1111  
  1112          uint256 cursor = _subCursor;
  1113          uint256 weight; // accumulated gas-weight; the chunk ends at weightBudget
  1114          // Batched prize-pool routing: each funded buy debits its full cost from the funding
  1115          // source and accrues that spend here by mode; the pools are credited ONCE at chunk end
  1116          // (boxes 90% future / 10% next, tickets 90% next / 10% future) so the per-sub cost is
  1117          // an add, not a pool SSTORE.
  1118          uint256 boxEthAccrued;
  1119          uint256 ticketEthAccrued;
  1120  
  1121          while (weight < weightBudget && cursor < _subscribers.length) {
  1122              address player = _subscribers[cursor];
  1123              Sub storage sub = _subOf[player];
  1124  
  1125              // (-1) NO-ORPHAN guard (§3 — the load-bearing correctness rule). A box is
  1126              // STAMPED at process (day D) but OPENED later; it exists ONLY as
  1127              // (Sub stamp + lastAutoBoughtDay) with no cold ledger, so ANY mutation of the
  1128              // Sub OR removal from `_subscribers` between stamp and open ORPHANS the
  1129              // paid-for box (the player was debited at stamp, gets nothing). A sub with a
  1130              // pending unopened box (`lastOpenedDay < lastAutoBoughtDay`) is therefore left
  1131              // ENTIRELY untouched this cycle — no reclaim, no evict, no funding-kill, no
  1132              // re-stamp; it stays in-set (reachable), `_autoOpen` opens it, and a LATER
  1133              // cycle processes it (now boxless, lastOpenedDay == lastAutoBoughtDay).
  1134              // Positioned BEFORE the cancel-reclaim so it dominates ALL FOUR orphan paths
  1135              // (re-stamp / cancel-reclaim / pass-evict / funding-kill). SKIP, not
  1136              // force-open (LOCKED §3): keeps the heavy open out of the gas-critical advance
  1137              // chain; the BURNIE open-bounty keeps opens prompt so it ~never skips a buy. No
  1138              // double-charge — the debit is downstream of this guard. Composes with the
  1139              // same-day idempotency skip at (1) (lastAutoBoughtDay >= processDay), which
  1140              // still handles the chunked-same-day case.
  1141              if (sub.lastOpenedDay < sub.lastAutoBoughtDay) {
  1142                  unchecked {
  1143                      ++cursor;
  1144                      ++processed;
  1145                      ++weight;
  1146                  }
  1147                  continue;
  1148              }
  1149  
  1150              // (0) Cancel-tombstone reclaim (CONSENT-02 — SUB-07 / H-CANCEL-SWAP-MISS).
  1151              // An externally-cancelled sub (subscribe(_, 0)) is an in-set
  1152              // `dailyQuantity == 0` tombstone: it relocated no one on cancel, so it cannot
  1153              // have pushed a pending entry behind the cursor. Finalize the afking streak (a
  1154              // no-op if the cancel already did — idempotent), then delete the `_subOf` record,
  1155              // swap-pop it out, and continue WITHOUT advancing the cursor — the swap-pop
  1156              // occupant (a mover from ahead, still pending) is processed at this slot this pass.
  1157              // Ordered ahead of the AlreadyAutoBoughtToday skip so a tombstone is ALWAYS
  1158              // reclaimed, independent of its lastAutoBoughtDay. The finalize is the cross-contract
  1159              // work that makes this the heavier (EVICT_WEIGHT) branch.
  1160              if (sub.dailyQuantity == 0) {
  1161                  _finalizeAfking(player, sub, processDay);
  1162                  // The streak base was already handed back to the manual streak by the finalize
  1163                  // above, so the sub is fully cleared on reclaim.
  1164                  delete _subOf[player];
  1165                  _removeFromSet(player);
  1166                  emit SubscriptionExpired(player, 2);
  1167                  unchecked {
  1168                      ++processed;
  1169                      weight += SUB_STAGE_EVICT_WEIGHT;
  1170                  }
  1171                  continue;
  1172              }
  1173  
  1174              // (1) AlreadyAutoBoughtToday — cheapest SLOAD-only skip (the BOX-03 marker is
  1175              // the idempotency backstop: a sub stamped this cycle is not re-stamped).
  1176              if (sub.lastAutoBoughtDay >= processDay) {
  1177                  emit PlayerSkipped(player, 2);
  1178                  unchecked {
  1179                      ++cursor;
  1180                      ++processed;
  1181                      ++weight;
  1182                  }
  1183                  continue;
  1184              }
  1185  
  1186              // (2) AFSUB-02/03 pass-validity gate. Non-crossing path is a pure stored-field
  1187              // compare (currentLevel <= validThroughLevel) — no extra read. At the crossing
  1188              // the pass re-reads the horizon EXACTLY ONCE and refreshes (still covered) or
  1189              // evicts via the tombstone-then-reclaim shape (CONSENT-02 — membership ⟺ packed
  1190              // != 0 preserved; a direct mid-pass removal would re-open H-CANCEL-SWAP-MISS).
  1191              if (currentLevel > sub.validThroughLevel) {
  1192                  uint24 h = _passHorizonOf(player);
  1193                  if (currentLevel <= h) {
  1194                      // REFRESH — still covered (newly minted pass, upgrade, etc.).
  1195                      sub.validThroughLevel = h;
  1196                      emit SubscriptionExtendedFree(player, processDay);
  1197                  } else {
  1198                      // EVICT — finalize the afking streak (hand it back), then delete the slot
  1199                      // and swap-pop out of the set (no cursor advance after the swap-pop). The
  1200                      // finalize is the EVICT_WEIGHT cross-call. A got-kicked sub forfeits both
  1201                      // accumulators: deleting _subOf wipes pendingBurnie / affiliateBase so
  1202                      // nothing survives claimable out-of-set.
  1203                      _finalizeAfking(player, sub, processDay);
  1204                      delete _subOf[player];
  1205                      _removeFromSet(player);
  1206                      emit SubscriptionExpired(player, 1);
  1207                      unchecked {
  1208                          ++processed;
  1209                          weight += SUB_STAGE_EVICT_WEIGHT;
  1210                      }
  1211                      continue;
  1212                  }
  1213              }
  1214  
  1215              // Funding resolution (cost + payment mode + ethValue slice). The slice builder
  1216              // computes everything revert-free by construction.
  1217              (
  1218                  ,
  1219                  uint256 ethValue,
  1220                  uint256 amount,
  1221                  bool isTicket,
  1222                  uint256 playerFunding,
  1223                  uint256 claimableUse
  1224              ) = _resolveBuy(sub, player, mp);
  1225  
  1226              // Resolve the once-per-iteration funding source. The common self-funded path
  1227              // is detected from the already-loaded `sub.flags` (FLAG_EXTERNAL_FUNDING clear
  1228              // ⇒ src = player) and skips the `_fundingSourceOf` SLOAD entirely; only the rare
  1229              // operator-funded sub (flag set) reads the sparse map. Both the funding skip-gate
  1230              // read and the debit key on this same `src`. The VAULT/SDGNRS exemption below
  1231              // stays keyed on the un-spoofable `player`, never `src`.
  1232              address src = (sub.flags & FLAG_EXTERNAL_FUNDING) != 0
  1233                  ? _fundingSourceOf[player]
  1234                  : player;
  1235  
  1236              // Funding skip → two-tier skip-kill. Read afkingFunding[src]: the common path
  1237              // (src == player) reuses `playerFunding` from _resolveBuy (no extra SLOAD); the
  1238              // rare operator-funded slice (src != player) reads afkingFunding[src]. A normal
  1239              // underfunded sub is cancelled via swap-pop (auto-pause WITHOUT advancing the
  1240              // cursor — the mover into this slot is processed this pass). VAULT and sDGNRS are
  1241              // exempt by the un-spoofable pinned ContractAddresses identity (kept on `player`,
  1242              // never `src`) — a funding skip is transient for them (no-op-and-retry, stays in
  1243              // the set). The exemption is the pinned-address branch only; there is no flag.
  1244              if (
  1245                  (src == player ? playerFunding : afkingFunding[src]) < ethValue
  1246              ) {
  1247                  if (
  1248                      player == ContractAddresses.VAULT ||
  1249                      player == ContractAddresses.SDGNRS
  1250                  ) {
  1251                      emit PlayerSkipped(player, 3);
  1252                      unchecked {
  1253                          ++cursor;
  1254                          ++processed;
