  1255                          ++weight;
  1256                      }
  1257                      continue;
  1258                  }
  1259                  // Funding-kill of a NORMAL underfunded sub — finalize the afking streak (hand it
  1260                  // back; its decay-on-read zeroes only if a full prior day was missed with NO
  1261                  // valid mint, afking OR manual), then delete the slot + swap-pop. A got-kicked
  1262                  // sub forfeits both accumulators: deleting _subOf wipes pendingBurnie /
  1263                  // affiliateBase so nothing survives claimable out-of-set.
  1264                  _finalizeAfking(player, sub, processDay);
  1265                  delete _subOf[player];
  1266                  _removeFromSet(player);
  1267                  emit SubscriptionExpired(player, 1);
  1268                  unchecked {
  1269                      ++processed;
  1270                      weight += SUB_STAGE_EVICT_WEIGHT;
  1271                  }
  1272                  continue;
  1273              }
  1274  
  1275              // BUY + DEBIT + ACCRUE + MARKER. The funded, well-formed slice is delivered
  1276              // revert-free by construction (no try/catch) by the shared `_deliverAfkingBuy`:
  1277              // debit `afkingFunding[src]` (claimablePool in tandem, fail-loud on underflow),
  1278              // stamp the lootbox box / queue the tickets, accrue the day's affiliate + the
  1279              // pendingBurnie reward, advance the compute-on-read streak markers (gap-resuming a
  1280              // fresh run if a day was missed), and set the success marker. A lootbox buy is weight
  1281              // SUB_STAGE_LOOTBOX_WEIGHT; a ticket buy SUB_STAGE_TICKET_WEIGHT (the cold ticketQueue
  1282              // push makes it ~2x a lootbox), so the budget binds on the true per-buy cost.
  1283              _deliverAfkingBuy(
  1284                  player,
  1285                  sub,
  1286                  processDay,
  1287                  mp,
  1288                  currentLevel,
  1289                  src,
  1290                  ethValue,
  1291                  claimableUse,
  1292                  amount,
  1293                  isTicket,
  1294                  false
  1295              );
  1296  
  1297              // Accrue the full buy cost (afking ethValue + reinvest claimableUse) for the
  1298              // batched pool credit below — a box buy funds the box pool, a ticket buy the ticket
  1299              // pool. The afking entry-unit `amount` is the box's wei spend only in lootbox mode,
  1300              // so the routing keys on `cost`, never `amount`.
  1301              uint256 cost = ethValue + claimableUse;
  1302              if (isTicket) ticketEthAccrued += cost;
  1303              else boxEthAccrued += cost;
  1304  
  1305              unchecked {
  1306                  ++cursor;
  1307                  ++processed;
  1308                  weight += isTicket ? SUB_STAGE_TICKET_WEIGHT : SUB_STAGE_LOOTBOX_WEIGHT;
  1309              }
  1310          }
  1311  
  1312          // Persist the advanced cursor (uint16) for the next chunk / call.
  1313          _subCursor = uint16(cursor);
  1314          // Credit the prize pools once for this chunk's batched box + ticket spend.
  1315          _routeAfkingPoolEth(boxEthAccrued, ticketEthAccrued);
  1316          return processed;
  1317      }
  1318  
  1319      /// @dev Route a chunk's batched afking spend to the prize pools, mirroring the normal-buy
  1320      ///      splits: lootbox ETH 90% future / 10% next (100% next in distress, matching
  1321      ///      `_purchaseForWith`), ticket ETH 90% next / 10% future (matching `recordMint`). One
  1322      ///      pooled read+write per chunk; routes to the pending pools while the prize pool is
  1323      ///      frozen. The per-buy debit already moved the ETH out of the funding source, so this
  1324      ///      only credits the pools (the SOLVENCY-01 counterpart of that debit).
  1325      function _routeAfkingPoolEth(uint256 boxEth, uint256 ticketEth) private {
  1326          if (boxEth == 0 && ticketEth == 0) return;
  1327          uint256 nextShare;
  1328          uint256 futureShare;
  1329          if (boxEth != 0) {
  1330              if (_isDistressMode()) {
  1331                  nextShare += boxEth;
  1332              } else {
  1333                  uint256 boxFuture = (boxEth * AFKING_LOOTBOX_FUTURE_BPS) / 10_000;
  1334                  futureShare += boxFuture;
  1335                  nextShare += boxEth - boxFuture;
  1336              }
  1337          }
  1338          if (ticketEth != 0) {
  1339              uint256 tFuture = (ticketEth * AFKING_TICKET_FUTURE_BPS) / 10_000;
  1340              futureShare += tFuture;
  1341              nextShare += ticketEth - tFuture;
  1342          }
  1343          if (prizePoolFrozen) {
  1344              (uint128 pNext, uint128 pFuture) = _getPendingPools();
  1345              _setPendingPools(
  1346                  pNext + uint128(nextShare),
  1347                  pFuture + uint128(futureShare)
  1348              );
  1349          } else {
  1350              (uint128 next, uint128 future) = _getPrizePools();
  1351              _setPrizePools(
  1352                  next + uint128(nextShare),
  1353                  future + uint128(futureShare)
  1354              );
  1355          }
  1356      }
  1357  
  1358      /*==================================================================
  1359          PART B (349-04) — the post-RNG OPEN-PASS + the ROUTER + PLACE-02
  1360      ==================================================================*/
  1361  
  1362      /// @dev Reverts with the delegatecall failure reason bytes. Canonical module tail
  1363      ///      (cf. DegenerusGameDegeneretteModule:123 / DecimatorModule:90) for the
  1364      ///      nested delegatecall into the LootboxModule's `resolveAfkingBox`.
  1365      function _revertDelegate(bytes memory reason) private pure {
  1366          if (reason.length == 0) revert E();
  1367          assembly ("memory-safe") {
  1368              revert(add(32, reason), mload(reason))
  1369          }
  1370      }
  1371  
  1372      /// @dev Materialize ONE subscriber's stamped afking box (the freeze-critical open).
  1373      ///      The box's word comes from `rngWordByDay[sub.lastAutoBoughtDay]` (the frozen
  1374      ///      stamp day); the level and the EV-cap key read live inside `resolveAfkingBox`;
  1375      ///      the per-sub inputs (amount, scorePlus1) come from the Sub record. Day-keyed
  1376      ///      no-double-open: the leg runs only while `lastOpenedDay < lastAutoBoughtDay`
  1377      ///      (pre-gated by `_afkingBoxReady`), and advances the marker
  1378      ///      (`lastOpenedDay = lastAutoBoughtDay`) BEFORE the resolve (effects-before-
  1379      ///      interaction; a re-entrant open re-checks the now-equal marker and no-ops). The
  1380      ///      box is materialized by delegatecalling the LootboxModule's `resolveAfkingBox`
  1381      ///      (the live-level twin of `resolveLootboxDirect`) with: the stamped spend (boons
  1382      ///      OFF ⇒ amount == spend), the frozen process `day` = `lastAutoBoughtDay`, the
  1383      ///      frozen day's word `rngWordByDay[day]`, and the frozen
  1384      ///      `activityScore = scorePlus1 - 1`. The draw math and the single EV-cap RMW live in
  1385      ///      `resolveAfkingBox`; this leg is the thin cursor/marker/dispatch shell.
  1386      ///      `resolveAfkingBox` is the one freeze-correct seam (the public
  1387      ///      `resolveLootboxDirect` derives its seed from the live day and would NOT freeze the
  1388      ///      seed `day`). No stored baseLevel/index — the live roll needs no floor.
  1389      /// @param player The subscriber whose box is materialized.
  1390      /// @param sub The subscriber's stamped record (storage ref — the marker advances here).
  1391      function _openAfkingBox(address player, Sub storage sub, uint256 word) private {
  1392          // lastAutoBoughtDay is the frozen stamp day used as the seed/word key.
  1393          uint24 day = sub.lastAutoBoughtDay;
  1394          // Advance the day-keyed no-double-open marker BEFORE the resolve (effects-first; a
  1395          // re-entrant open re-checks `lastOpenedDay < lastAutoBoughtDay` → false → no-op).
  1396          sub.lastOpenedDay = sub.lastAutoBoughtDay;
  1397  
  1398          // boons OFF ⇒ the stamped spend IS the box amount (unpacked milli-ETH → wei). The
  1399          // word (the frozen stamp day's `rngWordByDay[day]`, passed in from the readiness check
  1400          // so it isn't re-read) keeps the open from being re-seeded; the level and EV-cap read
  1401          // live in the callee. No index, no baseLevel.
  1402          (bool ok, bytes memory data) = ContractAddresses
  1403              .GAME_LOOTBOX_MODULE
  1404              .delegatecall(
  1405                  abi.encodeWithSelector(
  1406                      IDegenerusGameLootboxModule.resolveAfkingBox.selector,
  1407                      player,
  1408                      _unpackMilliEthToWei(uint64(sub.amount)), // milli-ETH → wei
  1409                      day,
  1410                      word,
  1411                      uint16(sub.scorePlus1) - 1
  1412                  )
  1413              );
  1414          if (!ok) _revertDelegate(data);
  1415      }
  1416  
  1417      /// @notice The post-RNG afking-box OPEN leg — an `OPEN_BATCH`-style router category
  1418      ///         driven by `_subOpenCursor` (not folded into advance).
  1419      /// @dev The open leg no-ops during the freeze (a mid-day RNG lock or the terminal-jackpot
  1420      ///      liveness control), so the loop body cannot revert under the entry-gate (each open
  1421      ///      is pre-gated on a landed word) — no per-item try/catch. Walks `_subscribers` from
  1422      ///      `_subOpenCursor`, opening up to `maxCount` materializable boxes; the per-sub
  1423      ///      day-keyed `lastOpenedDay` marker makes the walk idempotent, so the cursor
  1424      ///      wrap-resets to 0 at the set end (a re-walk skips already-opened subs by the marker
  1425      ///      — no extra per-index storage). Concurrent callers self-partition via the advancing
  1426      ///      cursor.
  1427      /// @param maxCount Max boxes to open this call (0 = OPEN_BATCH). Caller-bounded; every
  1428      ///        afking box is uniform O(1), like a human box.
  1429      /// @return opened The number of afking boxes materialized this call.
  1430      function _autoOpen(uint256 maxCount) internal returns (uint256 opened) {
  1431          if (maxCount == 0) maxCount = OPEN_BATCH;
  1432          // Entry-gate (RD-3/RD-5): the open path no-ops in the freeze / terminal control.
  1433          if (rngLockedFlag || _livenessTriggered()) return 0;
  1434  
  1435          uint256 len = _subscribers.length;
  1436          if (len == 0) return 0;
  1437          uint256 cursor = _subOpenCursor;
  1438          // Wrap a spent cursor back to the set start (the marker makes the re-walk a no-op
  1439          // on already-opened subs; a fresh-stamp sub past its marker opens).
  1440          if (cursor >= len) cursor = 0;
  1441  
  1442          // Day-cache: the boxes in one pass are almost always all stamped on the current day,
  1443          // so the frozen stamp-day word is read from `rngWordByDay` once per DISTINCT day, not
  1444          // once per box. Mixed days CAN occur (the open leg falls behind OPEN_BATCH or a keeper
  1445          // skips a day → the no-orphan rule keeps an old-day box), so each box still resolves
  1446          // ITS OWN stamp day — the cache only short-circuits the repeated same-day SLOAD, never
  1447          // crosses a box to another day's word (the seed-freeze invariant).
  1448          uint24 cachedDay;
  1449          uint256 cachedWord; // != 0 ⇒ cache holds rngWordByDay[cachedDay]
  1450  
  1451          while (cursor < len && opened < maxCount) {
  1452              address player = _subscribers[cursor];
  1453              Sub storage sub = _subOf[player];
  1454              unchecked {
  1455                  ++cursor;
  1456              }
  1457              // Skip subs with no pending box (already-opened: lastOpenedDay >= lastAutoBoughtDay).
  1458              uint24 stampDay = sub.lastAutoBoughtDay;
  1459              if (sub.lastOpenedDay >= stampDay) continue;
  1460              // Resolve this box's frozen stamp-day word — cache hit on the common same-day path.
  1461              uint256 word;
  1462              if (stampDay == cachedDay && cachedWord != 0) {
  1463                  word = cachedWord;
  1464              } else {
  1465                  word = rngWordByDay[stampDay];
  1466                  cachedDay = stampDay;
  1467                  cachedWord = word;
  1468              }
  1469              // word == 0 ⇒ the stamp day's word hasn't landed yet — skip until it does.
  1470              if (word == 0) continue;
  1471              // Guaranteed-non-reverting under the entry-gate + the readiness pre-gate.
  1472              _openAfkingBox(player, sub, word);
  1473              unchecked {
  1474                  ++opened;
  1475              }
  1476          }
  1477  
  1478          _subOpenCursor = uint16(cursor);
  1479      }
  1480  
  1481      /// @notice Unified permissionless afking router: do ONE category of pending work this
  1482      ///         call (priority advance → afking-box open) and pay ONE bounty (PLACE-02).
  1483      /// @dev ROUTER one-category STRUCTURAL early-return: the rngLock-aware O(1) predicates
  1484      ///      pick the first category with work; the advance and open bounties can never
  1485      ///      stack in one tx. NO `nonReentrant` guard (ROUTER-07 — the module is
  1486      ///      afking-never-a-payee: every external call is to a pinned `ContractAddresses.*`
  1487      ///      [GAME self-call / LootboxModule delegatecall / COINFLIP], player value flows
  1488      ///      through the game's claimable pull ledger, and the bounty is minted flip-credit
  1489      ///      — never an ETH push the router receives). The legs return raw counts/mult and
  1490      ///      NEVER self-credit; only `mintBurnie` credits, ONCE, CEI-last after the
  1491      ///      one-category early-return.
  1492      /// @dev PLACE-02 bounty: the buy/process bounty FOLDS INTO the advance bounty — the
  1493      ///      process STAGE runs inside `advanceGame` (the required path, 349-05), so the
  1494      ///      advance leg's `unit · 2 · mult` IS the process bounty, scaled by the
  1495      ///      AdvanceModule's day-epoch stall `mult` (1/2/4/6, :226-242). The OPEN leg pays
  1496      ///      the `OPEN_KNEE` work-scaled pro-rate (pay for work done, farm-by-splitting
  1497      ///      resistant). `mult == 0` (the gameover advance path) pays no bounty.
  1498      function mintBurnie() external {
  1499          uint256 mp = _mintPriceInContext();
  1500          uint256 unit = (BOUNTY_ETH_TARGET * PRICE_COIN_UNIT) / mp;
  1501          uint256 bountyEarned;
  1502  
  1503          // (1) advance — highest priority, liveness-critical (TRUE regardless of rngLock).
  1504          // The self-call re-enters the Game's advanceGame, which runs the required-path
  1505          // process STAGE in-context (349-05); the process bounty rides this 2x·mult.
  1506          if (IGameRouter(address(this)).advanceDue()) {
  1507              // Read pay-eligibility BEFORE the advance — it sees the pre-advance day (the
  1508              // advance bumps dailyIdx). The advance work runs regardless; an ineligible
  1509              // keeper just earns no bounty (real participants get first shot, free cranks
  1510              // are welcome).
  1511              bool eligible = _bountyEligible(msg.sender);
  1512              uint8 mult = IGameRouter(address(this)).advanceGame();
  1513              if (mult > 0 && eligible) bountyEarned = unit * ADVANCE_RATIO_NUM * mult;
  1514          }
  1515          // (2) afking-box open — FALSE during rngLock (RD-3); opens mid-day-resolved
  1516          // stamped boxes via _subOpenCursor. 1x pro-rated below the knee, flat 1x
  1517          // at/above — kills the small-batch farm-by-splitting corner.
  1518          else {
  1519              uint256 opened = _autoOpen(OPEN_BATCH);
  1520              if (opened > 0) {
  1521                  uint256 k = opened < OPEN_KNEE ? opened : OPEN_KNEE;
  1522                  bountyEarned = (unit * k) / OPEN_KNEE;
  1523              } else {
  1524                  // (3) ROUTER-06 — both categories empty: the clean no-work signal.
  1525                  revert NoWork();
  1526              }
  1527          }
  1528  
  1529          // The single unified bounty: ONE creditFlip, CEI-LAST, after the one-category
  1530          // early-return. Skipped at 0 (e.g. a mult==0 gameover advance); the category
  1531          // still ran, so we return rather than reverting NoWork().
  1532          if (bountyEarned > 0) {
  1533              coinflip.creditFlip(msg.sender, bountyEarned);
  1534          }
  1535      }
  1536  
  1537      /// @notice Drain up to `count` ready afking boxes (walks `_subOpenCursor`); returns the
  1538      ///         number opened so the caller can budget the remaining per-tx work. Unrewarded —
  1539      ///         only mintBurnie() credits. Reached via the Game's openBoxes() liveness valve
  1540      ///         (a distinct selector from the Game's human-box autoOpen(uint256), so the two
  1541      ///         do not collide; calling this module contract directly hits empty storage).
  1542      /// @param count Max afking boxes to open this call (0 = the default OPEN_BATCH).
  1543      /// @return opened The number of afking boxes opened this call.
  1544      function drainAfkingBoxes(uint256 count) external returns (uint256 opened) {
  1545          return _autoOpen(count);
  1546      }
  1547  
  1548      /// @dev In-context mint price (the bounty's ETH→BURNIE conversion divisor). Mirrors
  1549      ///      the Game's `mintPrice` (:2501) — the price for the active ticket level —
  1550      ///      read in-context so the bounty math needs no external/self call. Single use
  1551      ///      site (the bounty `unit`); never an open-time seed input (FREEZE-safe).
  1552      function _mintPriceInContext() internal view returns (uint256) {
  1553          return PriceLookupLib.priceForLevel(_activeTicketLevel());
  1554      }
  1555  
  1556      /// @dev ETH-denominated spend → BURNIE base units at the buy-context ticket price —
  1557      ///      the VALUATION BASIS for the lootbox-branch affiliate routing (DESIGN §3:
  1558      ///      affiliate + quest rewards are BURNIE flip-credit, never an ETH cut). A faithful
  1559      ///      copy of MintModule._ethToBurnieValue (:1669-1675); PRICE_COIN_UNIT (= 1000 ETH)
  1560      ///      is the inherited Storage constant already used at the bounty unit (:913). Pure —
  1561      ///      no ETH moves, no state.
  1562      function _ethToBurnie(
  1563          uint256 amountWei,
  1564          uint256 priceWei
  1565      ) private pure returns (uint256) {
  1566          if (amountWei == 0 || priceWei == 0) return 0;
  1567          return (amountWei * PRICE_COIN_UNIT) / priceWei;
  1568      }
  1569  
  1570      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
  1571                                    BURNIE claim
  1572      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
  1573      /// @notice Permissionless BURNIE claim — pays each sub its accrued `pendingBurnie` (the
  1574      ///         per-delivered-day slot-0 quest reward + the ticket buyer-bonus) in ONE
  1575      ///         `creditFlip` and zeroes it, so a re-claim finds 0. Always credits the sub, never
  1576      ///         the caller; callable anytime — the reward is already earned per delivered day,
  1577      ///         so there is no settle-timing or claim-timing edge to exploit. Off the solvency
  1578      ///         path: a BURNIE flip-credit, never an ETH cut.
  1579      /// @param subs The subscribers to pay (each credited its own accrued `pendingBurnie`).
  1580      function claimAfkingBurnie(address[] calldata subs) external {
  1581          uint256 len = subs.length;
  1582          // Presale-box eligibility for afking buyers, materialized at claim (no advance-path cost).
  1583          // The slot-0 BURNIE owed approximates the afking mint spend (100 whole BURNIE == one
  1584          // 0.01-ETH early-level buy, the price at the levels presale spans), and 25% of that spend is
  1585          // the manual buyer's presale-box credit. Granting it off the DRAINED `owed` counts each
  1586          // BURNIE exactly once (cover-buys included — they accrue slot-0 like any buy), so there is no
  1587          // double-count. Only while presale is open; the credit is unspendable once presaleOver.
  1588          bool presaleLive = !presaleOver;
  1589          for (uint256 i; i < len; ) {
  1590              address player = subs[i];
  1591              Sub storage s = _subOf[player];
  1592              uint256 owed = uint256(s.pendingBurnie); // whole BURNIE
  1593              if (owed != 0) {
  1594                  s.pendingBurnie = 0; // CEI: zero before the external credit
  1595                  if (presaleLive) {
  1596                      // A ticket sub's pendingBurnie also carries the ticket buyer-bonus on top of
  1597                      // the flat slot-0, so it overstates the mint spend — halve the ticket-sub grant
  1598                      // to net it back toward the slot-0-implied spend.
  1599                      uint256 credit = (owed * 0.0025 ether) / 100;
  1600                      if ((s.flags & FLAG_USE_TICKETS) != 0) credit /= 2;
  1601                      presaleBoxCredit[player] += credit;
  1602                  }
  1603                  coinflip.creditFlip(player, owed * 1 ether); // whole → base units
  1604              }
  1605              unchecked {
  1606                  ++i;
  1607              }
  1608          }
  1609      }
  1610  
  1611      /*------------------------------------------------------------------
  1612                              Affiliate base accessor
  1613      ------------------------------------------------------------------*/
  1614      /// @notice Affiliate-only atomic read-and-zero of a sub's accrued `affiliateBase` (the
  1615      ///         running unclaimed flat-7% affiliate balance, whole BURNIE), which the affiliate
  1616      ///         `claim` consumes.
  1617      /// @dev The read-and-zero happen together at the storage owner, so a duplicate sub in the
  1618      ///      affiliate `claim` array drains 0 the second time — the key guard against
  1619      ///      double-credit. There is no separate read accessor, so the caller can never
  1620      ///      pre-load bases into a memory array. Only `ContractAddresses.AFFILIATE` may drain,
  1621      ///      so a non-affiliate caller can never redirect a sub's base to a wrong recipient.
  1622      ///      Runs in the Game's storage context; `msg.sender` is the original caller.
  1623      /// @param sub The subscriber whose affiliate base is drained.
  1624      /// @return base The drained whole-BURNIE affiliate base (0 if already drained / never accrued).
  1625      function drainAffiliateBase(address sub) external returns (uint256 base) {
  1626          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.AFFILIATE) revert NotApproved();
  1627          Sub storage s = _subOf[sub];
  1628          base = s.affiliateBase;
  1629          s.affiliateBase = 0;
  1630      }
  1631  }

  1547      /// @notice Claim accrued ETH winnings.
  1548      /// @dev Aggregates all winnings: affiliates, ContractAddresses.JACKPOTS, endgame payouts.
  1549      ///      Uses pull pattern for security (CEI: check balance, update state, then transfer).
  1550      ///
  1551      ///      GAS OPTIMIZATION: Leaves 1 wei sentinel so subsequent credits remain
  1552      ///      non-zero → cheaper SSTORE (cold→warm vs cold→zero→warm).
  1553      ///
  1554      ///      SECURITY: Reverts if balance ≤ 1 wei (nothing to claim).
  1555      /// @param player Player address to claim for (address(0) = msg.sender).
  1556      function claimWinnings(address player) external {
  1557          player = _resolvePlayer(player);
  1558          _claimWinningsInternal(player, false);
  1559      }
  1560  
  1561      /// @notice Claim accrued ETH winnings with stETH-first payout.
  1562      /// @dev Restricted to self-claims by the vault contract.
  1563      function claimWinningsStethFirst() external {
  1564          if (msg.sender != ContractAddresses.VAULT) revert E();
  1565          _claimWinningsInternal(msg.sender, true);
  1566      }
  1567  
  1568      function _claimWinningsInternal(address player, bool stethFirst) private {
  1569          if (_goRead(GO_SWEPT_SHIFT, GO_SWEPT_MASK) != 0) revert E();
  1570          uint256 amount = claimableWinnings[player];
  1571          // Decision B (GAMEOVER-01): post-gameOver the claim ALSO pays the caller's prepaid
  1572          // afking ETH (lazy per-player merge — no unbounded loop). Pre-gameOver afkingFunding
  1573          // stays its own bucket (spent by afking auto-buys / reclaimed via withdrawAfkingFunding).
  1574          // Both this merge and withdrawAfkingFunding zero the SAME bucket → no double-spend.
  1575          uint256 afking = gameOver ? afkingFunding[player] : 0;
  1576          if (amount <= 1 && afking == 0) revert E();
  1577          uint256 payout;
  1578          unchecked {
  1579              if (amount > 1) {
  1580                  claimableWinnings[player] = 1; // Leave sentinel
  1581                  payout = amount - 1;
  1582              }
  1583              if (afking != 0) {
  1584                  afkingFunding[player] = 0;
  1585                  payout += afking;
  1586              }
  1587          }
  1588          claimablePool -= uint128(payout); // CEI: update state before external call (checked math)
  1589          emit WinningsClaimed(player, msg.sender, payout);
  1590          if (stethFirst) {
  1591              _payoutWithEthFallback(player, payout);
  1592          } else {
  1593              _payoutWithStethFallback(player, payout);
  1594          }
  1595      }
  1596  
  1597      /// @notice Fund a player's prepaid afking ETH bucket (consumed by the AfKing afking auto-buy).
  1598      /// @dev Permissionless (fund anyone) — the AfKing subscribe-forward (A2) and the OPEN-E
  1599      ///      operator-funding case both route here. The Game's bare receive() routes msg.value to
  1600      ///      the prize pool, so afking deposits MUST use this dedicated entrypoint. The reservation
  1601      ///      rides inside claimablePool (no separate aggregate) — credited in tandem.
  1602      /// @param player The beneficiary whose afkingFunding bucket is credited.
  1603      function depositAfkingFunding(address player) external payable {
  1604          if (player == address(0)) revert E();
  1605          if (msg.value == 0) return;
  1606          afkingFunding[player] += msg.value;
  1607          claimablePool += uint128(msg.value);
  1608          emit AfkingFunded(player, msg.value);
  1609      }
  1610  
  1611      /// @notice Withdraw prepaid afking ETH — the funding source reclaims its own balance.
  1612      /// @dev Un-brickable strict CEI: the GO_SWEPT guard is LINE 1 (before any debit), so a
  1613      ///      post-final-sweep withdraw reverts cleanly instead of underflowing claimablePool
  1614      ///      (which the sweep zeroes). Both debits land BEFORE the .call, so a re-entrant second
  1615      ///      call re-reads the already-debited balance and reverts. Available always pre-sweep
  1616      ///      (mid-game, after cancel, post-gameOver). The claimablePool debit stays checked math.
  1617      /// @param amount ETH amount (wei) to withdraw from the caller's afkingFunding bucket.
  1618      function withdrawAfkingFunding(uint256 amount) external {
  1619          if (_goRead(GO_SWEPT_SHIFT, GO_SWEPT_MASK) != 0) revert E();
  1620          if (amount == 0) return;
  1621          uint256 bal = afkingFunding[msg.sender];
  1622          if (amount > bal) revert E();
  1623          unchecked {
  1624              afkingFunding[msg.sender] = bal - amount;
  1625          }
  1626          claimablePool -= uint128(amount); // tandem release (checked math)
  1627          (bool ok, ) = msg.sender.call{value: amount}("");
  1628          if (!ok) revert E();
  1629          emit AfkingWithdrew(msg.sender, amount);
  1630      }
  1631  
  1632      /// @notice The canonical per-player prepaid afking ETH balance (replaces AfKing.poolOf).
  1633      /// @param player The player to query.
  1634      /// @return The player's afkingFunding balance (wei).
  1635      function afkingFundingOf(address player) external view returns (uint256) {
  1636          return afkingFunding[player];
  1637      }

  1146      /// @dev Adds ETH to a player's claimable winnings balance.
  1147      /// @param beneficiary The address to credit.
  1148      /// @param weiAmount The amount in wei to credit.
  1149      function _addClaimableEth(address beneficiary, uint256 weiAmount) private {
  1150          if (weiAmount == 0) return;
  1151          claimablePool += uint128(weiAmount);
  1152          _creditClaimable(beneficiary, weiAmount);
  1153      }

  1155      /// @dev Award sDGNRS from Reward pool on the top-3 score tiers (S>=7) Degenerette ETH bets.
  1156      ///      Reward scales by bet size (capped at 1 ETH) and score tier.
  1157      function _awardDegeneretteDgnrs(
  1158          address player,
  1159          uint256 betWei,
  1160          uint8 s
  1161      ) private {
  1162          uint256 bps;
  1163          if (s == 7) bps = DEGEN_DGNRS_7_BPS;
  1164          else if (s == 8) bps = DEGEN_DGNRS_8_BPS;
  1165          else bps = DEGEN_DGNRS_9_BPS;
  1166  
  1167          uint256 poolBalance = sdgnrs.poolBalance(
  1168              IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Reward
  1169          );
  1170          if (poolBalance == 0) return;
  1171  
  1172          uint256 cappedBet = betWei > 1 ether ? 1 ether : betWei;
  1173          uint256 reward = (poolBalance * bps * cappedBet) / (10_000 * 1 ether);
  1174          if (reward == 0) return;
  1175  
  1176          sdgnrs.transferFromPool(
  1177              IStakedDegenerusStonk.Pool.Reward,
  1178              player,
  1179              reward
  1180          );
